South Africa abɛka aman ahodoɔ a Nigeria man no de taaboɔ ato wɔn so sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ ahɔhoɔ anaa akwankufoɔ bɛfiri ɔman no mu abɛwura Nigeria man no mu ɛsiane sɛ COVID-19 Delta yareɛ no bi akɔpue wɔ South Africa man no mu.
wɔmma wɔn a wɔtuu kwan kɔɔ South Africa nnatwe mmienu akyire no kwan ma wɔmma Nigeria man no mu.
Temaamufoɔ a wɔwɔ South Africa a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔba Nigeria man no mu no, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔde wɔn ho kɔsie nna nson ansa.
Saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi nso bra Brazil ne Turkey aman no nso.
Kaaka Mohammed wuo a ɔwuiiɛ no yɛ awerɛho na ɛsan nso yɛ asefem.
Onyankopɔn mfa ne kra nsie na mema n’abuasuafoɔ no nso hyɛden.
Ntɛm pa ara no, nnipa no bi rekeka sɛ aban no hyɛ ne wuo no akyi, ɛnna afoforɔ nso rekyerɛ sɛ wɔrebɔ mpaeɛ sɛ aban no nnim ne wuo no ho hwee.
Wei nso nyɛ ara ne sa ɛsiane sɛ ɛmma nhwehwɛmu mapa a ɛtwa sɛ ɛkɔ so no nkɔ so.
Sɛ yɛhwɛ aban no awoyie fa “fix the ɔountry” nsɛnsɛm no ho a, mennyɛ nni sɛ aban no nim saa wuo yi ho bi, mpo sɛ m’ani tua pa ara sɛdeɛ amanyɛsɛm ayɛ abofono asi afa no, biribiara tumi si. Mpo sɛ ɔbarima bɛtumi asesa ne ho adane ɔbaa.
Aban no hyiaa wɔn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no sɛ nka ɔbɛma wɔn akoma aba fam.
Akyire no, ɔyɛkyerɛ no hyɛɛ dawubɔkuo mmienu no so maa wɔbɛkaa deɛ aban no reyɛ de asiesie ɔman no ho asɛm.
Na mmom yɛwɔ nkorɔfoɔ wɔ aban no mu a wɔne wɔn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no nyɛ adwene a wɔakyerɛ wɔn nso adwene sɛ wɔn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no nso nna suban pa adi.
Afei nso, yɛnyaa apolisifoɔ a wɔbɔɔ wɔn ho mmɔden biara sɛ wɔmma wɔn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no nte nsi abɔntene na wɔde COVID-19 no na ɛyɛɛ nnyinasoɔ nanso saa apolisifoɔ yi ara antumi asi nnipadɔm a wɔkɔɔ Sir John ayie ase no kwan.
Yeinom nyinaa bɛtumi ama ho kwan ma wɔde aban no fɔrefɔre owuo yi ho, mpo sɛ nnipa no bi bɛdwene sɛ ɔyɛ nokorɛ ɛsiane adanseɛ mapa biara nni hɔ.
ɛtwa sɛ yɛhunu no biom sɛ, ɛnni kwan sɛ yɛbu yɛn ani gu so sɛ amanyɔsɛm tantan a ɛrekɔ so no nso bɛtumi ama ankorɛankorɛ a wɔnni aban mu no nso bɛtumi ahyɛ nkorɔfoɔ kutupa ama wɔadi nsɛmmɔne anaa wɔde agu aban no anim ase.
Bio, adansidie biara nni hɔ a yɛbɛtumi de akyerɛ sɛ onipa bi na na ɔhyɛ Kaaka wuo no akyi.
ɛwɔ sɛ yɛyɛ nhwehwɛmu mapa a ɛyɛ korɔgyeen ma yɛhunu deɛ ɛtua asɛm yi mu.
Memfa sobɔɔ no nyinaa mmɔ asraafoɔ a wɔnnim hwee a wɔkɔkuu nnipa baanu yi.
Yɛwɔ soboɔ bi a, yɛmfa mmɔ kwan a wɔfaa so de faa wɔn adwuma ne nteteeɛ a wɔde maa wɔn no.
Aban no anim bɛkɔ so agu ase ɛnam sɛ ɛkwan a wɔfa so de fa asraafoɔ no adwuma no nyinaa akɔyɛ amanyɔsɛm na mmom ɛnnyina mmɔdemmɔ so. Wei nyinaa ka ho bi na Mobrowa Struggle kɔɔ so 2000 a na medi akotene pa ara wɔ kuo no mu sɛ twenekafoɔ.
Yɛhunuu kwan a apolisifoɔ ne asraafoɔ de yɛn faa so, sɛ mpo sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa ka yɛn.
Hwan na ɔkoto to tuo aberɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ rekɔ so?
Hwan na na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔto ne tuo? Nnipa anaa “beela”?
Saa na ɛwɔ sɛ wɔto tuo ma wɔgyae ɔyɛkyerɛ no?
Kwan bɛn so na wɔfaa so faa ɔsraani yi adwuma?
Hwan na ɔfaa no adwuma? Hwan na ɔde no faa nteteeɛ mu?
Saa onipa yi yɛ nipabɔnefoɔ a ɔhyɛ asraafoɔ atadeɛ de dadaa nnipa.
Merebɔ yɛ kabimamenkabi amanyɔsɛm no ho dawuro akyerɛ abenfoɔ ne Abibiman kandifoɔ ahodoɔ.
Deɛ nnipa dodoɔ no ara nnim ne sɛ, wɔkyerɛ sɛ deɛ ɛrekɔ so yie kyerɛ sɛdeɛ Ghana nnyiniiɛ wɔ kabimamenkabi amanyɔsɛm mu na wei ne me nsɛnkae no bɔ abira.
Deɛ merekyerɛ ne sɛ, deɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ aban no mu bi ne sɛdeɛ asraafoɔ de wɔn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no refa so no ne kabimamenkabi amanyɔsɛm bɔ abira koraa.
Sɛ woto teaa gaas wɔ wɔn a Ghanafoɔ a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no so a, ɛnya nsunsuansoɔ wɔ wɔn so?
Na nsuohyeɛ ne rɔba bulɛts nsoeɛ?
Aban bɛpɛ sɛ ɔbɛyi mpaninfoɔ a wɔda bammɔ nnwumakuo ano adi na wei bɛboa ama sɛ nnipakuo bi reyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ a, bammɔ nnwumakuo no bɛhunu sɛdeɛ wɔbɛsi adi wɔn dwuma asi afa. Aban no nso bɛpɛ sɛ wɔde bammɔfoɔ yi bɛsan akɔ sukuu mu bio akɔma wɔn nteteeɛ fa sɛdeɛ yɛne nnipa di nkitaho sɛ mentemehoase bi asi a, anaa sɛdeɛ yɛne yɛn a wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ bɛkasa ama wɔagyae ɔyɛkyerɛ no, kyɛn sɛ wɔde wɔbɛdwane dabiara akɔ kɔɔto sɛ wɔrekɔpɛ akwansie tumi.
Wei ma nnipa bo fo ma wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ.
ɛwɔ ɔmampanin no ankasa de ne nan si asɛm yi so, na ɔma nnipa nya awerɛhyɛmu na asomdwoeɛ ba ma asɛm yi to twaa.
ɔyɛkyerɛfoɔ no ani so deɛ, bammɔ adwumakuo no nnim adwuma.
ɛsiane sɛ Asomdweɛ Kansere no nso ahokeka wɔ fam nti, akɔyɛ sɛ wɔnni tumi sɛ wɔbɛsiesie deɛ ɛrekɔ so yi. ɔhaw wei nyinaa nti na ɛwɔ sɛ ɔmampanin no ankasa de ne nan si asɛm so a, ɛbɛboa. ɛyɛ sɛ ɔyɛ wei mmerɛ papa mu.
Thomas Amoani a wadi mfeɛ du-nkron a ɔwiee sukuu wɔ Adeiso Presbyterian Senior High School a ɔnyaa sokɔlahyip afiri Ghana Sɔholarships Secretariat hɔ no ada aban a ɔmampanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo Addo ase.
Krakyepanin a ɔwɔ asoeɛ hɔ, Owura Kingsley Agyemang de ato dwa sɛ, wɔama Thomas Amoani a ɔnyaa A nko ara nwɔtwe wɔ West Africa Seɔondary School Certificate Examination afe a ɛtwaa mu no sokɔlahyip sɛ ɔrekɔsua adeɛ wɔ suapɔn kɛseɛ Brunel University a ɛwɔ London mu.
Aberanteɛ a wadi mfeɛ du-nkron a ɔfiri Asuaba a ɛbɛn Adeiso na sika nni fie yi bɛsua Economics ne Business Finanɔe wɔ suapɔn no mu.
N’awerɛhosɛm yi hyetaa ɔman no mu nyinaa berɛ osuani yi ne nsɛntwerɛfoɔ twetwee nkɔmmɔ. ɔreka n’akosɛm, Thomas Amoani de too dwa sɛ na ɛtɔ mmerɛ bi a ɔtwa kwansini kilomita du-mmienu ansa ne waduru ne sukuu mu.
ɔmampanin Akufo-Addo tee saa asɛm yi na ɔhyɛɛ sɛ wɔmma no sokɔlahyip.
ɔrefiri asoeɛ hɔ no, krakyepanin a ɔwɔ asoeɛ hɔ de too nsɛntwerɛfoɔ anim sɛ, adeɛ ɔmampanin ayɛ ama Thomas no bɛhyɛ wɔn a wɔaka no nkuran ama wɔasua adeɛ yie ɛmfa ho ne fie a wɔfiri mu.
Owura Agyemang de too dwa sɛ, “mehunu sɛ nnipa bebree a wɔte Thomas wɔ hɔ na merehyɛ wɔn bɔ sɛ sokɔlahyip asoeɛ wɔ hɔ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ wɔn mmoa. ɛwɔ Thomas asɛm yi hyɛ wɔn a wɔte no no nkuran. Mɛbɔ ɔmampanin Akufo-Addo aba so wɔ deɛ wayɛ yi ho.”
ɔduruu suapɔn mu hɔ no, Thomas Amoani a n’ani agye de too dwa sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ ne man Ghana animuonyam na ɔmma Ghana nsa nsi fam da.
ɔde too dwa sɛ, “Manna anwene da sɛ ɔmampanin bɛfa krakyepanin no so ama ma akwannya a ɛte sei da. Meda wɔn ase wɔ gyidie a wɔanya wɔ me mu. Memma me man Ghana anim ngu ase.”
Brunel University London yɛ suapɔn bi a ɛwɔ Uxbridge mpɔtam mu a ɛwɔ London, England. Wɔtee saa suapɔn yi wɔ 2966 mu na wɔde saa suapɔn yi too Isambard Kingdom Brunel. Wiase mu nyinaa no sɛ ɛba engyiniɛ ne tɛknɔlɔgyi mu a, saa suapɔn yi tɔ so aduonkron mmiɛnsa, ɛnna ɛtɔ so aduasa mmienu wɔ Europe. THES nhwehwɛmu a wɔde baeɛ kyerɛ sɛ, saa suapɔn yi tɔ so du-baako sɛ ɛba suapɔn a ɛwɔ Britain man mu.
Mfomsoɔ biara nni ho sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa, ɔtemmuafoɔ Kwasi Anin Yeboah de kwaadu bɛbɔ Dr. Dominic Akuritinga Ayine a ɔyɛ lɔya na ɔsan nso yɛ Bolgatanga East mmarahyɛbɛdwani wɔ General Legal Council (GLC)
Zebilla mmarahyɛbɛdwani dadaa, lɔya John Ndebugre kyerɛ sɛ nsɛm a National Democratic Congress (NDCɔ ne wɔn a wɔkeka ho reka ɛfa saa kwaadu bɔ yi ho no, ɛwɔ sɛ Dr Ayine ba Genral Legal Council (GLɔɔ no asotwee kɔmitee no anim na wɔka ho asɛm.
“Megye di sɛ na ɔtemmuafo panin paa ne nnipa a ɛwɔ sɛ ɔhyɛ kwaadu yi ase ɛfiri sɛ asɛm a Dr Ayine de too dwa maa kwaadubɔ yi baeɛ no mmuabɔ nyinaa ne sɛ, ɛnam sɛdeɛ ɔmampanin abatoɔ no kɔɔ so nti, ɔnni awerɛhyɛmu wɔ aban mmara adwuma mu.”
ɛnam nsɛm a Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine kaeɛ berɛ a na wɔretwetwe nkɔmmɔ fa Presidential election Petition ne ɛso nsunsuansoɔ a anya wɔ Abibiman kabimamenkabi amammuo so, ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa de Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine akɔ GLɔ Asotee Kɔmitee anim.
Wɔde kwaadu abɔ Dr. Ayine ɛnam kwan a ɔfaa so twee aban mmara adwumakuo no anim, ne sɛn nti ne sɛ kɔɔto peemu a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu si dii 2020 ɔmampanin abatoɔ pɛtihyin no si faeɛ.
Pɛtihyin no kyerɛ sɛ, Dr. Ayine nnyinasoɔ a ɔde kaa n’asɛm no berɛ nkɔmmɔdie no rekɔ no ne sɛ kɔɔto peemu amfa mmara ɛda asennie nhyehyɛeɛ anni dwuma na afei nso na wɔbɔ pɛtihyina no relɛɛfs to gu.
“Dr Ayine kaa nsɛm bi sei faa kɔɔto peemu no ho mmerɛ bi atwa mu ɛfa abatoɔ pɛtihyin no ho maa kɔɔto peemu de kɔntɛmɛt kwaadu bɔɔ no. Dr. Ayine paa kɔɔto peemu no akyɛw berɛ a wɔde no kɔgyinaa kɔɔto peemu no anim ɛnam kɔntɛmɛt kwaadu a wɔde bɔɔ no no. Na ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ, sɛ ɔyɛ lɔyani na ɔsan nso yɛ aban lɔya panin abadiakyiri dadaa deɛ, wankasa yie.”
Dr. Ayine anoyie a ɔde maa atemmuafoɔ mpaninfoɔ a wɔdii abatoɔ pɛtihyin asɛm no ne sɛ, n’asɛm a ɔde too dwa no ammu wɔn animtia.
ɔsii so dua sɛ, wanka asɛm no wɔ kwan bɔne so.
“Sɛdeɛ mede too dwa wɔ me mmuaeɛ mu no, ɛyɛ m’asɛdeɛ sɛ mɛbɔ aban mmara adwumakuo dwumadie no akyi. ɛnam nteteeɛ a mafa mu ne suahunu a mewɔ nti, mɛtumi akyerɛ m’adwene afa nnoɔma a ɛnkɔ yie wɔ aban mmara adwumakuo no dwumadie ho asene Ghanafoɔ no fa bi.”
ɔsan nso de kaa ho sɛ, ne nsɛm a ɔkaeɛ no kwan so ara no no.
Dwoada a amanyɔkuo kɛseɛ a wɔnni aban mu, National Democratic Congress (NDCɔ ne nsɛntwerɛkyerɛ hyiaa wɔ Accra no, wɔde too ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa n’anim sɛ ɔtwe kwaadu a ɔde abɔ Dr. Ayine no nsan.
Mr Ndebugre kyerɛ sɛ ɔne wɔn a wɔse ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa ntwe ne kwaadu a ɔde abɔ Dr Ayine nsan no nyɛ adwene. ɔkyerɛ sɛ, Dr Ayine asɛm no ɔkaeɛ no ankɔ amma ɔtemmuafoɔ no mu baako anaa atemmuafoɔ mpaninfoɔ nson a wɔdii asɛm no. Na ɔrekasa afa aban mmara adwumakuo no nyinaa ho ɛnna ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa nso na ɔda aban mmara adwuma no ano, nti ɔno ne nipa ɛwɔ sɛ ɔde kwaadu bɔ Dr Ayine.
ɔne Citi FM a wɔwɔ Accra ntwetwe nkɔmmɔ no Benada anwummerɛ (Kotonomma da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmienu wɔ 2021 muɔ, Mr Ndebugre kaa sɛ, “megye di sɛ mfomsoɔ biara nni ho sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa de kwaadu bɛbɔ no.”
ɔde deɛ ɛsii 1996 reyɛ mfatoho no – ɔman no de kwaadu bɔɔ Mensah Bonsu, Stephen Quarɔoo ne Tommy Thompson a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Mensah Bonsu akasa atia Justice Aban nti wɔbɔɔ no kwaadu, ɛnna aban lɔya panin gyinaa aban mmara adwuma no anan mu wɔ kɔɔto.
ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa no mfom mmara sɛ ɔde kwaadu bɛbɔ no.
“Nti medwene sɛ mfomsoɔ biara nni ho sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa de kwaadu bɛbɔ no.”
Deɛ ɛdi hɔ ne sɛ, na Dominic Ayine yɛ aban lɔya abadiakyire na saa mmerɛ no na ɔne ne panin de nkorɔfoɔ kɔ kɔɔto ... nti sɛ aban lɔya panin ka sɛ wɔmfa onipa korɔ no nnyina mmara anim a, obi bɛtumi aka sɛ, na saa nipa korɔ no rekyerɛ n’adwene nti mma wɔmfa no nkɔ kɔɔto?
Daabi. ɛwɔ sɛ wokɔ kɔɔto kɔka w’asɛm sɛ wonni fo wɔ kwaadu a wɔde abɔ wo no ho.
Saa ara nso na ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa nso kyerɛ sɛ n’asɛm no agu aban mmara adwuma no anim ase.
Mr Ndebugre de kaa ho sɛ, “Nti wo deɛ kɔ. ɛwɔ sɛ wɔtena asɛm a NDC ne Dr Ayine no ankasa reka yi so wɔ Asotwee Kɔmitee no so.”
ɔkyerɛ sɛ nnoɔma mmienu na ɛwɔ ha, ɛte sɛ kɔntɛmɛt, sɛ woreka asɛm no wɔ kɔɔto na wode nsɛm bi a ɛgu aban mmara adwuma no ho fi to dwa, anaasɛ wɔde atemmuo no ato dwa na woaka asɛm fi bi afa ho no, wɔbɛtumi de wɔn agyina mmara anim ɛnam saa deɛ wei ho.
Sɛ wode fɔ wɔ kɔɔto a, wobɛtumi aka sɛ wonnye atemmuo no ntom, “na sɛ wokɔ ka sɛ amanyɔkuo no hunu sɛ Dr Ayine wɔ tumi sɛ ɔkyerɛ n’adwene nti wɔntumi mfa no nnyina mmara anim deɛ a, me ne wo nnye adwene.”
“Asɛm no nyinaa ne sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ wokɔ Asotwee Kɔmitee no anim na wokɔ ka sɛ na worekyerɛ w’adwene, na mmom sɛ woka sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa a ɛda aban mmara adwuma no ano nni ho kwan sɛ ɔde kwaadu bɛbɔ wo, na wonnye sɛdeɛ aban mmara adwuma no dii asɛm no faeɛ no ntom. Nti ɛwɔ sɛ ɔkɔ hɔ (GLɔɔ na ɔkɔkyerɛ deɛ nti a ɔkaa sɛ aban mmara adwuma a wɔwɔ Ghana mu no nne wɔn ho.”
Wɔbisaa sɛ ɛsiane sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa na ɔyɛ ɔtitenani me GLɔ a Asotwee Kɔmitee no yɛ kɔɔto no nkorabata no nti ɔde Dr Ayine rekɔgyina n’ankasa kɔɔto, na Mr Ndebugre buaa sɛ, “Worepɛ akyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ Asotwee Kɔmitee no so yɛ robɔts na deɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa bɛkyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ na wɔbɛyɛ? Sɛ woyɛ biribi sei a, wommoa ma kabimamenka bi ntu mpɔn wɔ ɔman no mu. Sɛ wowɔ kwan sɛ wokyerɛ w’adwene a, na ɛnkyerɛ sɛ wobɛtumi aka deɛ wopɛ biara.”
ɔde nnipa wɔde wɔn kɔ mmarahyɛbadwafie asotwee kɔmitee no yɛɛ mfatoho kyerɛɛ sɛ, “Saa nnipa no a wɔde wɔn kɔ hɔ no, ɛnyɛ wɔn adwenkyerɛ na wɔkyerɛeɛ? Sɛ woka sɛ mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ aporɔ berɛ a wɔnni nnyinasoɔ biara a, wɔtwe wo de wokɔ wɔn kɔmitee anim ... adɛn nti na woreka sɛn wɔntumi mfa wonnyina mmara anim?
“Menkaa sɛ deɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa no yɛɛ no yɛ anaa nyɛ.”
Deɛ mereka nyinaa ne sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa de kwaadu abɔ no na deɛ menim ne sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa no ne nipa a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔbɔ saa kwaadu no, ɛfiri sɛ n’asɛnkae tia aban mmara dwuma no ho ne wɔn fahodie ho. ɔno na ɔda aban mmara adwuma no ano ɛnna ɔde kwaadu abɔ no.
Kwaadubɔ no nkyerɛ sɛ wɔbu wo kumfo. ɛwɔ sɛ wokɔ hɔ na wokɔkyerɛkyerɛ nsɛm a wode reto nsɛntwerɛfoɔ anim no wɔ hɔ na wɔnka asɛm no.
“Sɛ wokɔ hɔ na wɔn nnyinasoɔ no nkɔ yie a, ɛhɔ na wobɛtumi aka hɔ asɛm, na seisei deɛ ka a ɔrekasa no nyinaa ho nhia. Mɛtu Ayine fo sɛ ɔmmɔ mmɔden nkɔ asotwee kɔmitee no anim na ɔnkɔka n’asɛm. ɛbɛboa wɔn ara sɛ wɔbɛkɔ na wɔama ɔtemmuafoɔ panin paa anhunu sɛ deɛ ɔreka no nyɛ nokorɛ.”.
Nsɛnsɛm a ɛbaeɛ wɔ abatoɔ a wɔtoo abatoɔ no afe a ɛtwaam no akyi no, National peace Council (NPC) de nhyehyɛeɛ agu akwan mu sɛ wɔbɛboa ama nkabom aba ɔman no mu.
Kansere no kyerɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ no adwenkyerɛ ahodoɔ no bɛtumi de basabasaeɛ aba ɔman no mu nti ɛwɔ sɛ wɔsi ano.
NPɔ kyerɛ sɛ nkɔmmɔdie bɛkɔ so amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ ne ɔmanfoɔ wɔ Ada a ɛwɔ Greater Accra mantam mu.
CommonwealthSecretariat ne United Nations Development Programme (UNDP) na na wɔsɔ saa dwumadie a wɔato ne din “Countering post 2020 election violenɔe and building ɔonsensus for greater Politicaltoleranɔe in Ghana”.
Dwumadie yi botaeɛ ne sɛ nteaseɛ bɛba ɔmanfoɔ ntɛm na aboa ama nkabom, asomdwoeɛ aba amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ ntɛm ne aboa ama ɔman no asomdwoeɛ ne nkankɔ atu mpɔn.
Wɔn wɔbaa dwumadie yi ase ne Commonwealth ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin, Rt. Hon. Patricia Sɔotland; UNDP ananmusifoɔ, Dr Angela Lusigi; ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nkitahodie so, Mr Kojo Oppong; amannwoeɛ soafoɔ, Mr Ambrose Dery ne ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ ɔman mmammɔ so, Mr Albert Kan-Dapaah.
Wɔne a na wɔwɔ hɔ bio ne abatoɔ kɔmisa abadiakyire, Dr Eric Bossman Asare; apolisifoɔ panin paa namusifoɔ, National Democratic Congress, New PatrioticParty, ɔonvention People’s Party mpaninfoɔ, asɔfo mpaninfoɔ, ahemfo ne akuo ahodoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu.
Mr Dery kaa sɛ ɛmfa ho ne nhyehyɛeɛ bammɔ adwumakuo de guu akwan ɛfa abatoɔ no ho no, basabasaeɛ ahodoɔ kɔɔ so a nnipa binom hweree wɔn nkwa, ɛnna agyapadeɛ ahodoɔ nso sɛe.
ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ basabasaeɛ ho nsɛm aduasa mmienu na ɛsii wɔn abatoɔ mpasua nnum mu wɔ ɔman no mu a, nnipa baasia hweree wɔn nkwa.
Mr Dery de too dwa sɛ aban reyɛ nhwehwɛmu afa basabasaeɛ yi ho na wɔn a wɔhyɛ aseɛ no, wɔbɛtwe wɔn aso.
Mr Kan-Dapaah nso de too dwa sɛ, sɛ ɔman no bɛtu mpɔn a, ɛgyina sɛ amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ no rete wɔn ho ase so.
Rt Hon Sɔotland bɔɔ Ghanafoɔ aba wɔ asomdwoeɛ kwan a wɔfaa so too aba wɔ ɔman no mu. ɛkyerɛ Commonwealthabusuakuo no ani gyee ho pa ara.
ɔde too dwa sɛ, Ghana akɔ n’anim wɔ kabimamenkabi amammuo mu a ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ, “ɛyɛ adesoa a ɛda kuromma no so, nso saa kuromma no abɔ wɔn ho mmɔden yie. Yɛwɔ awerɛhyɛmu kɛseɛ wɔ Ghana mu.”
ɔsan nso de too dwa sɛ ɛyɛ mmaa ne mmabunu no de wɔn ho hyɛ ɔman no mmarahyɛ mu.
ɔtitenani a ɔda NPɔ ano, Rev. Dr. Ernest Adu-Gyamfi de too dwa sɛ, saa dwumadie yi de ayɔnkofa, gyidie ne awerɛhyɛmu mapa bɛba amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ no ntam ne ɔman nnwumakuo a ɛhwɛ abatoɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu ntam.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ saa nkɔmmɔdie yi bɛboa ama wɔasiesie ɔhaw a aba 202 abatoɔ akyi no nyinaa.
ɔpanin paa ɔda Transeco Mineral ne Mining ano, Mr. Godwin Amarh asi sukuu dan adampɔn nsia wɔ Akyem Ampapatia a ɛwɔ Atiwa West mansini a ɛwɔ Apueeɛ mantam mu.
ɔbɔɔ ka GH¢295,000 wɔ saa sukuu adan yi ho; na wei ka kɔmpɛne nhyehyɛeɛ ho sɛ wɔbɛboa ama wɔn atenaeɛ mu atu mpɔn.
Wɔrebue dan no ano no, Mr Amarh kyerɛɛ sɛdeɛ ɛhia sɛ mmɔfra a wɔwɔ mfiaseɛ sukuu mu bɛnya nwomasua mapa ɛsiane sɛ ɛboa ma wɔnya nwomasua mu fapem papa.
ɔde too dwa sɛ, wɔntumi ntoto nwomasua aseɛ wɔ kwa biara so ɛsiane sɛ ɔman no mpontuo gyina nwomasua so, nti ɛho hia sɛ kɔmpɛne no nso bɛma nwomasua ahia wɔn.
“Yɛn a yɛyɛ adwuma wɔ Transeco Mining and Minerals companyayɛ yɛn adwene sɛ, yɛbɛboa ama mfiaaseɛ sukuu nwomasua atu mpɔn wɔ baabibiara yɛn dwumakuo yi bi wɔ. Wei nti na dwumakuo ayɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛboa ama nwomasua atu mpɔn wɔ baabi biara wɔwɔ.”
ɔkaa sɛ, “ɛyɛ me dɛ sɛ maba Ampapatia na merebɛbue saa sukuu yi ano. Yɛn nyinaa yɛnim sɛdeɛ nwomasua ho hia ma nnipa ne ɔman no mpontuo. Sɛ yɛbɛnya asuafoɔ ama wɔaka sukuu aduruu akyire a, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔnya fapem mapa, na wei nti na ama yɛasi saa sukuu dan yi.”
Mr Amarh de kaa ho sɛ, sukuu dan no yɛ aseda a wɔde rema ahemfo ne nnipa a wɔwɔ Ampapatia mu a wɔne adwumakuo no anya nkitahodie mapa firi berɛ adwumakuo baa wɔn mpɔtam mu no.
Mr Amarh de too dwa sɛ ɛnyɛ nokorɛ sɛ aban no de taaboɔ ato maenen so wɔ ɔman no mu.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ aban no mmom de nhyehyɛeɛ mapa aba sɛdeɛ maenen bɛtu mpɔn, na nyɛ sɛ ɔbɛgu no.
Mr Amarh kaa sɛ, “Aban mfaa taaboɔ ntoo maenen na mmom wɔkyerɛ beaeɛ ahodoɔ a ɛbɛn nsuo ne kwaeɛ no mu baabi a ɛnni kwan sɛ obiara kɔyɛ maenen dwumadie biara wɔ hɔ. Nti obiara a ɔbɛbu aban nhyehyɛeɛ yi so no, mmara ne no bɛdi.”
ɔtuu wɔn a wɔyɛ maenen adwuma no fo sɛ, wɔkɔtu maenen no na mmom wɔnyɛ no beaeɛ a wɔahyɛ wɔn no no.
Mr Amarh a ɔsan nso yɛ ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ Panin ma Ghana National associationof Small Sɔale Miners (GNASSMɔ de too ne kuomma anim sɛ wɔmmoa mma mpɔtam a wɔyɛ wɔn adwuma wɔ mu no ntu mpɔn.
ɔde too dwa sɛ wɔn a wɔtu maenen no nsesa deɛ wɔka fa wɔn ho sɛ wɔsɛe mpɔtam ahodoɔ mu a mpɔtam no nnyaa hwee firi wɔn ho.
ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ, maenenfoɔ no bi rebɔ wɔn ho mmɔden nso wɔbɛtumi ayɛ asene saa.
ɔtoo fo sɛ, “Yɛn adwumakuo yi fa nnipa bebree wɔ mpɔtam ahodoɔ a yɛyɛ yɛn nnwuma no adwuma. ɛwɔ sɛ yɛyɛ adwumaden gya biribi papa to hɔ. Menim sɛ kuomma no dodoɔ no ara a wɔasisi sukuu adan na wɔaboa ma mpɔtam ahodoɔ anya anyinam ahoɔden. ɛwɔ sɛ yɛbɔ nsɛm yi ho dawuro ma nkorɔfoɔ sesa deɛ wɔka fa yɛn ho no.”
Rebeɔɔa Foundation ne Abdul Samad Rabiu Africa Initiative (ASR Africa) de wɔn nsa ahyɛ kɔntraagye aseɛ a, sika a Rebeɔaa Foundation bɛnya yɛ $500,000.
Saa sika yi bɛfiri ASR Africa afe mu no nyinaa dwetire watwa to hɔ ama Africa Fund for SocialDevelopment and Renewal a ɛyɛ dɔla no, ɔpepem ɔha mu na ɛbɛba de aboa Rebeɔɔa Foundation nwomasua ho nhyehyɛeɛ.
ɔde n’anodisɛm reto dwan wɔ nhyiamu no ase no, ASR Africa adwuma no kwankyerɛfoɔ, Mr Ubon Udoh bɔɔ ekuo yi aba so sɛ wɔatu wɔn ho asi hɔ ama mmaa ne mmɔfra mpontuo.
ɔsan bɔɔ ekuo no aba wɔ sɛdeɛ wɔde amammuo mapa redi wɔn dwuma a aboa ama ekuo no reyɛ nnwuma bebree aboa ama nwomasua, apɔmmɔden nsɛm ne mmaa mpontuo rekɔ so.
ɔkaa sɛ, “Yɛyɛɛ yɛn nhwehwɛmu hunuu sɛ Rebeɔɔa Foundation yɛ adɔeɛ kuo a wɔn anim wɔ nyam wɔ Ghana, na ɛhyɛɛ ASR Africa nkuran sɛ yɛmmɛboa wɔn.”
Kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔda Rebeɔɔa Foundation ano, Mrs Rebeɔɔa Akufo-Addo daa ASR Africa ase wɔ wɔn mmoa wɔde aboa ekuo no.
ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ekuo no de sika no bɛboa ama mmɔfra nwomasua atu mpɔn wɔ ɔman no mu.
UK aban no kyerɛ sɛ, wɔnnim Nnamdi Kanu a ɔdi nnipadɔm a wɔwɔ Nigeria anaafoɔ apueeɛ fam a Igbofoɔ ma wɔdɔɔso wɔ hɔ no kyere ne bɔ a wɔabɔ no aba Nigeria no ho hwee.
Aban lɔya panin kyerɛ sɛ, Interpol kyee Mr Kanu a ɔyɛ Britainni na ɔsan nso firi Nigeria Kwasiada de no baa Nigeria.
Wɔde tirisin kwaadu bɔɔ no wɔ Nigeria wɔ 2017 mu nso wɔdwanee firii ɔman no mu berɛ a wɔmaa no beele.
Wɔsusu sɛ wɔkyee no wɔn UK, beaeɛ a wɔgye di sɛ na ɔteeɛ.
British Haekɔmisa Kasamafoɔ de too BBɔ anim sɛ “Yɛbɛtumi aka sɛ wɔankye Nnamdi Kanu sɛ wɔde no rekɔ ne man mu.”
ɔkɔɔ kɔɔto Benada no; ɔwɔ Nigeria apolisifoɔ akakye.
Wɔsan de no bɛkɔ akɔgyina mmara no anim wɔn Kitawonsa da a ɛtɔ so aduonu nsia.
Nnamdi Kanu gyee ne din wɔ 2009 mu berɛ a ɔhyɛɛ Radio Biafra adwuma ase wɔ London a na ɛba Nigeria. Sɛdeɛ wɔn a wɔte Biafra bɛnya wɔn fahodie nti, ɔde saa akwannya yi de too wɔn a wɔdi n’akyi no sɛ wɔtwetwe atuo wɔn Nigeria man no mu.
Mfeɛ num akyi no, ɔtee Indigenous People of Biafra (Ipobɔ a ayɛ atuatedɔm wɔn Nigeria aban no so.
Wɔdii kan kyee no wɔ 2015 mu no, ɛde ɔyɛkyerɛ bebree na ɛbaeɛ.
ɛyɛɛ me dɛ berɛ mehunuu sɛ wɔreyɛ nsiesie adwuma wɔ Independence Square afe a ɛtwam mu no.
ɔmampanin dadaa John Jerry Rawlings ayie nti na wɔreyɛ nsiesie adwuma yi.
Institute of Directors-Ghana (IoD-Gh) abɔ Bank of Ghana (BoG) aba so wɔ nhyehyɛeɛ mapa a wɔde agu akwan mu sɛdeɛ adwumakuo a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu ho bɛdwo wɔn.
Wɔasrɛ sɛ wɔne Bank of Ghana bɛnya ayɔnkofa soronko a ɛbɛboa ama adwumakuo wɔwɔ ɔman no mu amammuo bɛtu mpɔn.
Berɛ a wɔkɔsraa BoG manɛgɛmɛnt no, ɔpanin a ɔda IoD-Gh ano, Mr. Roɔkson Kwesi Dogbegah bɔɔ Bank of Ghana panin paa, Dr Ernest Addison no aba so wɔ n’amammuo papa ɔde abu sikasɛm akuo ahodoɔ wɔ ɔman no mu.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ BoG a Dr Addison da ano no aboa ma sikakorabea a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu ntotoeɛ atu mpɔn.
Asɛm a adwumakuo mpaninfoɔ yi de too dwa fa deɛ nti a wɔkɔɔ BoG ne sɛ, wɔrekɔbɔ wɔn aba wɔ kwan a wɔafa so atoto adwumakuo ho ammmuo wɔ Ghana na wɔpɛ sɛ wɔne BoG ayɔnkofa no gyina pintinn.
ɔrekasa afa nhyehyɛeɛ a IoD-Gh de agu akwan mu no, Mr Dogbegah kyerɛ sɛ IoD-Gh de nhyehyɛeɛ regu akwan mu sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ nnwumakuo mu amammuo bɛtu mpɔn wɔ ɔman no mu.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔman mu amammuo kɔɔdo nso yɛ nhyehyɛeɛ baako a wɔde regu akwan mu.
ɔdaa no adi sɛ afe biara no, wɔbɛbɔ nnipa ahodoɔ ne nnwumakuo a wɔn adwuma sɔ ani no wɔ nnwumakuo amammuo mu na wɔaboa ama mpontuo aba ɔman no mu aba so.
ɔde kaa ho sɛ adwumakuo ne ne nnwumakuo ahodoɔ aka wɔn ho abɔm ate Ghana associationof Integrated Thinking and Reporting a ɛbɛboa ama nnwumakuo aba nyam.
Panin paa ɔda BoG ano de too dwa sɛ nnwumakuo amammuo di akotene yie wɔ sikasɛm nnwumakuo mu.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ mmara a wɔbu so wɔn nnwumakuo amammuo mu, adwumayɛfoɔ no suban ne deɛ ɛkeka ho nyinaa na ɛmmoa ma sikakorabea ahodoɔ mfa wɔn ntoma pa mfira.
ɔde kaa ho sɛ, Ghanafoɔ mmoa na nnwumakuo amammuo mapa nkɔ so, na ɔde too dwa sɛ BoG nso bɛboa ama nnwumakuo no dwumadie atu mpɔn ɛsiane sɛ sikakorabea ahodoɔ no dwumadie nya nsunsuansoɔ wɔ ɔman no sikasɛm so.
Bɔɔlobɔ afe foforɔ a yɛbɛsi mu yi deɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ Arteta bɔ ne ho mmɔden.
Sɛdeɛ madi kan aka dada no, Arsenal yɛɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛyi Arteta adi na wɔn a wɔda bɔɔlobɔ kuo no ano no taa n’akyi sɛ ɔbɛsesa nnoɔma afe a ɛda yɛn anim yi.
Obiara ntumi nkyerɛ sɛ deɛ Arsenal yɛɛ no kwan so ara no no, nso bɔɔlobɔ kuo de bɔɔlobɔfoɔ a wɔyɛ adeɛ bɛba bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu.
Nnipa bebree na wɔrebisa sɛ, so Arteta bɛtumi ayɛ adwuma no anaa na bɔɔlobɔfoɔ a ɔne wɔn di dwuma no bisa wɔn ho sɛ so ɔbɛtumi ayɛ adwuma no anaa?
Arteta ne Pep Guardiola yɛɛ adwuma gyee din sɛ kookyi a ɔbɔ ne ho mmɔden berɛ na wadi mfeɛ aduasa nkron.
Nso Arsenal mmɔden te sɛ sɛdeɛ ɛteɛ no ara mfa ho sɛ wayɛ adwuma abosome du nson. Nnipa bebree reka sɛ bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mmɔden akɔ fam sene mmerɛ a na Unai Emery yɛ wɔn kookyi no, deɛ Arteta bɛdii n’adeɛ a ɔyii Arteta firii mu wɔ Europa League no mu.
Na Arteta yɛ Arsenal sahene na wɔn a wɔtae bɔɔlobɔ kuo bɔgyee ne so sɛ ɔno na ɔrebɛgye wɔn nanso ato wɔn awerɛhoɔ ne ayamhyehyɛ sɛdeɛ ɔhelsea ne Tottenham retwe wɔn mu si fa no.
ɛbɛkyɛ ansa na nnipa werɛ afi adeɛ a Super League no bɛyɛeɛ.
Na mmom mɛtumi aka sɛ wɔn a Arsenal yɛ wɔn dea no, Kroenke abusua no nni baabi biara kɔ.
Nti sɛ Arteta asɛdeɛ sɛ ɔbɛhyehyɛ bɔɔlobɔ kuo wɔyɛ nam yɛ hye na ɔbɛma mpontuo aba ne tActes mu bɔɔlɔbɔ afe a ɛda yɛn anim no mu. Anyɛ saa nnoɔma bɛtete apansam wɔ Arsenal bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu.
De Gea nnye ntom sɛ ɔbɛyɛ abadiakyire.
Manchester United gookipa, David De Gea n’anamusifoɔ rehwɛ sɛ ɔbɛtumi akɔtoa ne dwumadie no so wɔ bɔɔlobɔ kuo foforɔ mu a, mfa ho sɛ David De Gea nsa hyɛ kɔntraagye wɔ bɔɔlobɔ kuo no ase kɔsi 2023.
Nteeɛ a merete firi Old Trafford ne sɛ, mfa ho sɛ De Gea ne mprɛnprɛn gookipa a ɔdi kan, Dean Henderson ayɔnkofa yɛ no, De Gea ntena hɔ sɛ wɔma ntena nkyɛn aberɛ ɔmmɔ bɔɔlo no bi.
Manya no nteeɛ sɛ Atletiɔo Madrid, Paris Saint Germain ne Real Madrid nya no a, wɔpɛ.
David De Gea a wanya mfeɛ aduasa aduruu baabi a ne bɔɔlobɔ wɔ soro wɔ ne bɔɔlobɔ adwuma no mu, ɛmfa ho sɛ nnipa no bi a wɔwɔ bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu hunu sɛ ne mfeɛ mmienu ni na ne mmɔden aba fam.
Manigya Solskɛaer de ato dwa sɛ, “gookipafoɔ hɔ no ayɛ hyeehyeehye.
Wɔsiesie wɔn ho, wɔn mu biara wɔ mmerɛ a wɔde kɔ gyem na wɔne bɔɔlobɔfoɔ no nyinaa nso yɛ trenin bɔm. Wɔn ntam nso yɛ kama.
Ayɔnkofa soronko da wɔn ntam nti gookipafoɔ no dwumadie deɛ, dabiara ɛwɔ soro.
Wɔboaboa wɔn ho wɔn ho ma wɔn mmɔdemmɔ tu mpɔn”
Megye di sɛ deɛ kookyi yi reka no yɛ nokorɛ nanso sɛ De Gea ammɛyɛ No 1 a, na woannya bɔɔlo no bi ammɔ a, manya no nteeɛ sɛ ɔbɛfiri Old Trafford.
Mesan de West Brom bɛsan aba bio.
West Bromwiɔh Albion asan afiri Premier League no mu afe pɛpɛɛpɛ a wɔbaa league no mu.
Sɛ wɔbɛsan afiri Championship no mu aba Premier League no mu a, ɛgyina sɛ manigya Sam Allardyɔe bɛte aseɛ atena bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu bio.
ɛnni n’abakɔsɛm mu sɛ ɔde bɔɔlobɔ kuo bi awe nti ɛyɛ no awerɛho sɛ saa animguaseɛ yi aba. Sɛ West Brom mpaninfoɔ pɛ sɛ ɔtenaa deɛ a, ɛnneɛ na wɔwɔ adwuma yɛ.
Ainsley Maitland-Niles, ɔonor Gallagher ne Okay Yokuslu bɛsan akɔ wɔn bɔɔlobɔ kuo a wɔde wɔn fem West Brom no mu bio ɛsiane sɛ wɔn mmerɛ aso sɛ wɔkɔ. Matheus Pereira, ɔallum Robinson, Hal Robson-Kanu ne Karlan Grant bɛtumi abɔ wɔn ho mmɔden wɔ Championship no mu.
Onipa a ɔnim ammirika tu pa ara wɔ Manchester ɔity.
Hwan na ɔnim ammirika tu pa ara wɔ Manchester Citybɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu?
Daabi, nyɛ Raheem Sterling.
Manigya Pep Guardiola de trenen bi aba a bɔɔlobɔfoɔ biara gye bɔɔlo no to fam de kɔ ammirika bɛyɛ yaade du.
Wɔwɔ bɔɔlobɔfoɔ a wɔntumi de bɔɔlo no tu ammirika pa ara nso Gabriel ɛesus kyerɛɛ sɛ obiara nto no.
Havertz bɛtumi ayɛ asene deɛ ɔreyɛ yi.
Thomas Tuɔhel rebɔ Kai Havertz aba so ɛwɔ ne ntena mmienu a ɔto tiaa Fulham no ho.
Tuɔhel gye tom sɛ ɛfiri sɛ Kai firii Bayern Leverkusen baa Stamford Bridge no, nnoɔma nkɔmaa no sɛdeɛ ɔsi pɛ no no.
Worekɔ ɔman foforɔ mu na lɔkdaw ho nhyehyɛeɛ bebree nso wɔ hɔ maa nnoɔma yɛɛ den maa no. Afei nso ɔsan nso yɛɛ COVID-19 a ɛmaa n’ahoɔden kɔɔ fam
Tuɔhel gye di sɛ, Champions League faenal ne bɔɔlɔbɔ afe a ɔda yɛn anim no na ɛbɛma yɛhunu ne mmɔdemmɔ.
Solskɛaer reboa ama United afa ne ntoma pa afira.
Manchester United akyitaafoɔ ne wɔn bɔɔlobɔ kuo wɔ asɛm sɛ wɔhyɛ sɛdeɛ wɔn anim asi abre si fa a, nso bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu deɛ wɔanya gyidie foforɔ, nkabom ne awerɛhyɛmu sɛ wɔbɛtumi abɔ wɔn ho mmɔden.
Onipa a ɔreyɛ wei nyinaa ne Ole Gunner Solskɛaer na me ne United adwumayɛfoɔ ne wɔn akyitaafoɔ no bi dii nkɔmmɔ no, obiara ahunu sɛ mmerɛ aso sɛ wɔbɔ manigya no aba so wɔ nnoɔma a ɔde abosome du-wɔtwe ayɛ wɔ bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu.
Solskɛaer boa maa wɔde Bruno Fernandes ne Edinson ɔavani baa bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu na wɔn mmɔdemmɔ nso asɔ ani yie.
ɔavani de ato dwa sɛ ɔbɛtena bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu afe baako aka ho na gyidie a ɔwɔ wɔ Solskɛaer mu na ama watena bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu.
Biribiara rekɔ yie ma Paul Pogba na n’ani nso gye. ɔne manigya no ayɔnkofa no nso yɛ.
Sɛ wo ne United resi akan nansa yi na sɛ wohyɛ wɔn a, wɔkeka wɔn ho na mpɛn pii no wɔbɛdi nkonim.
Adeɛ baako a yɛde bɛbɔ ɔtitenani abadiakyire a ɔrekɔ, Ed Woodward aba so ne sɛ ɔmaa Solskɛaer tenaa bɔɔlɔbɔ kuo no mu ama wasesa nnoɔma ama bɔɔlobɔfoɔ no mmɔdemmɔ atu mpɔn.
ɛnam mmɔdemmɔ a Manchester United rebɔ nti, Solskɛaer abɛyɛ onipa a ne ho hia yie wɔ bɔɔlobɔkuo no mu. Wɔn a na wɔrebɔ n’akyi, adwumayɛfoɔ ne akyitaafoɔ no nyinaa gye di sɛ wei yɛ bɔɔlɔbɔ kuo mpagya ahyɛaseɛ.
Tɛɛl-teel sae
Kane pɛ sɛ ɔkɔ.
Manhunu ne mmɔdemmɔ no so berɛ na wɔne Leeds United resi akan nnawɔtwe yi awieeɛ.
Harry Kane tu ammirika pa ara mpo sene bɔɔlɔbɔfoɔ a ɔne wɔn si akan no nyinaa; ɔkyerɛ deɛ n’afɛfoɔ no nyɛ wɔ agopramma no so sɛdeɛ wɔn dwumadie no bɛkɔ tɔɔtee.
Wɔne Leeds resi akan no, na ɔyɛ dinn a menhunuu no saa bi da.
Megye di sɛ wei yɛ adeɛ a ɛkyerɛ Harry pɛ sɛ ɔfiri Spurs bɔɔlɔbɔ kuo no mu, na ɔrehwehwɛ kwan a ɔbɛfa so.
Wolves ani abere sɛ wɔbɛnya straeka.
Nuno Espirito Santos ahunu sɛ afei deɛ ɛho bɛhia sɛ ɔbɛnya straeka wɔn bɔɔlɔbɔ kuo no mu.
Pedro Neto a ɔbɔ ntɛntɛnoa ne Reben Neves a ɔbɔ mfimfini na wɔato ntena bebree ama bɔɔlobɔ kuo no, na wei kyerɛ sɛ wɔn anim hɔ no nkɔ yie.
Fabio Silva ne Raul Jimenez na wɔde wɔn akyi nso ɛnam pira nti, firi Obubuo bosome mu no, ɛimenez ntumi nsii akan.
Wolves ntena a wɔtoo no afe a ɛtwaa mu no so ate du-mmiɛnsa.
Wolves manɛgemɛnt ahyɛ Nuno bɔ sɛ wɔbɛma no sika ama wɔde akɔto obi a ɔnim ntena toɔ.
Bosome a ɛtɔ so num no ne da a ɛtɔ so du-wɔtwe na ɛimenez bɛhunu sɛ ɔbɛtumi asi akan wɔ wɔn akansie mmienu ɛtwa toɔ no mu anaa.
Wayɛ traenen bɛyɛ bosome mmienu nso wɔde taaboɔ ato ne sɛ ɔmmfa ne ti nka bɔɔl na afei nso ɔnni kwan sɛ ɔde ne ho ka wɔn a ɔne wɔn si akan no.
Sir Alex abɔ McTominay aba so.
Sɛ nipaa kɛseɛ bi te sɛ Sir Alex Ferguson kasa fa Manchester United ho a, ɛho hia sɛ wɔtie no.
N’ani agye Sɔott McTominay ho na ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ ɔsi akan dabiara ma United.
Sir Alex de too dwa sɛ, “Scott McTominay abɛyɛ bɔɔlobɔni kɛseɛ wɔ United mu”
“Sɛ wohwɛ wɔn a United de wɔn bɔ wɔn bɔɔlobɔ akɛseɛ no a, McTominay din wɔ mu.”
ɛwɔ suban da na ɛba trene nso a, ɔbɔ ne ho mmɔden.
Mede no baa bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu berɛ na ɔwɔ mfeɛ nson anaa nwɔtwe.
Na na ɔyɛ straeka
Abasobɔdeɛ kɛseɛ bɛn na ɛkyɛn wei.
Nwanwadeɛ ahodoɔ mmiɛnsa a asi wɔ bɔɔlobɔ mu...
Afe baano ne abosome nan nie, Manchester United nnii nkukuo wɔ Premier League akansie a wɔammɔ no wɔ wɔn fie da.
Sɛ wɔanni nkonim wɔ wɔn akansie a ɛda wɔn anim no a, Sheffield United bɛyɛ bɔɔlɔbɔ kuo a wɔdi kan a firi 1904-1905 bɔɔlɔbɔ afe mu a wɔnnii nkonim wɔ akansie mmienu mu ntoa so.
Dr Madzorera de too dwa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ asoeɛ a ɛhyɛ apɔmmuden nsɛm so ma yareɛ no dawuro dɔɔso, na afei nso wɔmma kwan ma nnipa frɛ wɔn wɔ tetefone sɛ wɔne wɔn bɛdi nkɔmmɔ afa yareɛ no ho ɛmfa ho ne baabi a wɔwɔ wɔ ɔman no mu.
Wɔsan nso kyerɛ sɛ wɔnyɛ kyɛkap a ɛho teɛ sene sɛ wɔbɛtwɛn ama yareɛ no akye wɔn ansa na wɔakɔ ayaresabea.
ɔaps United titenani, Lewis Uriri de ato dwa sɛ, wɔasiesie ɔhaw a ɛwɔ bɔɔlobɔ kuo no mu na bɔɔlɔbɔfoɔ a na wɔate atwea nyinaa asane aba reyɛ ahoboa wɔ wɔn akansie a wɔbɛsi wɔ ɔastle Premier Soɔɔer League no mu.
ɔne Studio 7 retwetwe nkɔmmɔ no, ɔde too dwa sɛ wɔatua bɔɔlɔbɔfoɔ sika a na akam no ama wɔn.
Nso ɔde too dwa sɛ bosome a atwam no akatua deɛ, ɛnkyɛ biara wɔde bɛma wɔn. ɔsan nso kyerɛɛ sɛ nnipa bi a wɔnnim wɔn din redaadaa ɔaps United bɔɔlɔbɔfoɔ no sɛ mma wɔnsi akan.
Utiri de too dwa sɛ deɛn nti na na bɔɔlɔbɔfoɔ nsa nkaa wɔn akatua ne sɛ na nnoɔma mu ayɛ den ama obiara wɔ ɔman no mu, na na aban no mpo mfaa wɔn sika mmaa wɔn.
Wɔn a wɔpere sɛ nsesaeɛ ba nnamusɛm ho kyerɛ sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ nsesaeɛ wɔ abɔɔhyin mmara na ɛne nnɛ mmerɛ mu abrabɔ no kɔ, na afei nso, ɛbɔ mmaayewa ne mmaa ho ban.
Sayendisa Ndlovu a ɔka SayWhat ho kyerɛ sɛ, nnipa a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu dodoɔ no ara nnim abɔɔhyin mmara no nti ɛwɔ sɛ aban no bɔ ho dawuro kyerɛ amansan.
Ndlove de too Studio 7 sɛ ɛhia sɛ wɔyɛ nsesaeɛ wɔ abɔɔhyin mmara mu ɛsiane sɛ wɔtwerɛɛ saa mmara no akyɛ.
Ndlove kyerɛ sɛ adwenem haw, HIV/AIDS ne dɛnnie bi na na ɛma ho kwan ma obi yɛ abɔɔhyin.
Ndlovu kyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmara no sɛdeɛ ɛteɛ no nsi ayaresabea biara ho kwan wɔ abɔɔhyin nhyehyɛeɛ ho na mmara ma ho kwan sɛ nɛɛse anaa dɔkota bi bɛyɛ abɔɔhyin.
Ms. Tendaishe ɔhangamire a ɔpere nsesaeɛ wɔ ɔman mma fahodie ho nso de too dwa wɔ Right Here Right Now dwumadie so sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ nsesaeɛ ba abɔɔhyin mmara no mu sɛdeɛ ɛbɛma abɔɔhyinyɛ so ate.
Ms ɔhangamire kyerɛ nhwehwɛmu da no adi sɛ, mmaa dodoɔ no ara na ɛnam abɔɔhyin nti, wɔhwere wɔn nkwa.
ɛmfa ho sɛ mmabunu dodoɔ no ara pɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nsesaeɛ wɔ abɔɔhyin mmara mu no, mmaa mpaninfoɔ no bi nso mpene so. Wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛnni kwan sɛ abɔɔhyin mmara no ma ho kwan ma wɔgye abɔɔhyinyɛ tom ɛfiri sɛ ɛmma mmabunu no mfa anidie mma nkwa.
Mmarahyɛbadwafie hyɛɛ abɔɔhyin mmara no wɔ 1977 mu ansa ɔman no renya ne fahodie.
Apolisifoɔ akye MDC-T a Nelson ɔhamisa di wɔn anim no kuo mma no bi aberɛ a wɔyɛɛ sɛ wɔrewura amanyɛkuo no asoeɛ kɛseɛ a ɛwɔ Harere no mu wɔ Morgan Tsyangirai fie.
Wei siiɛ berɛ kuo mma no bi a Ms Thokozani Khupe di wɔn anim no kɔfaa asoeɛ hɔ nɔɔnum.
Kɔɔto peemu ahyɛ sɛ Ms Khupe na ɔnni adeɛ ɛsiane sɛ na Morgan Tsyangirai afiri mu (wei si ne wuo no akyi mfeɛ mmienuɔ.
Wɔn a apolisifoɔ akye wɔn ne ɔhamisa abadiakyire mmienu, Tendai Biti ne Lynett Karenyi Kore. David ɔhimhini, Lovemore ɔhinoputsa, Gladys Hlatywayo ne wɔn a wɔkeka ho nso ka ho bi.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na wɔn a wɔkye wɔn no nam kwan so rekɔ amanyɔkuo no asoeɛ kɛseɛ hɔ na apolisifoɔ kɔkyeree wɔn.
ɛsiane sɛ na wɔfrɛ apolisifoɔ kasamafoɔ, Paul Nyathi wɔ tetefone so a wɔnnya no nti, Studio 7 nnyaa nteeɛ biara mfiri apolisifoɔ no hɔ ɛfa nnipa dodoɔ ankasa a wɔakye wɔn no ho ne kwaadu a wɔde abɔ wɔn.
ɔhamisa MDɔ kasamafoɔ Fadzai Mahere de too dwa sɛ ɛyɛ no nwanwa sɛ wɔakyere wɔn.
Kɔɔto peemu de too dwa afe yi mu sɛ, ɔhamisa ne Khupe nyinaa amammuo nni mmara kwan so na mmom mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ no nhyia na Ms Khupe na ɛbɛtoto nnoɔma. Wei ama deɛ ɛrekɔ so wɔ MDɔ mu no ano ayɛ den.
Kɔɔto peemu de asɛm yi too dwa ara pɛ na Ms Khupe yii mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ anan adi; ne sɛn nti ho ne sɛ nyɛ amanyɔkuo no mpontuo nti na saa nnipa yi wɔ hɔ.
Wɔn a wɔyii wɔn firii mmarahyɛbadwafie ne Thabitha Khumalo, Prosper Mutseyami, Lilian Timveous ne ɔharlton Hwende.
Zimbabwefoɔ bi a wɔwɔ aman foforɔ mu de ato dwa sɛ, Robert Mugabe amammuo na ɛhyɛɛ wɔn maa wɔfirii ɔman no mu. Wɔkyerɛ sɛ na ɔde nsa den na ɛrebu ɔman no.
Amanyɔsɛm kyerɛkyerɛni a ɔkyerɛ adeɛ wɔ Bergen University wɔ Norway na ɛka Zimbabwe Yibuya/Mayibuye kuo ho, Dr Viɔtor ɔhimhutu kyerɛ sɛ, ɛwɔ mu sɛ Mr Mugabe adi akotene wɔ Abibiman nkabm ho nanso abusua baako wɔ Zimbabwe a wɔnhunu no sɛdeɛ obiara si hunu no si fa.
Dr ɔhimhutu kyerɛ sɛ Mr Mugabe ayɔnkofa a ɔne Abibiman mpaninfoɔ bi wɔ yɛ sɛn nti nti no mu baako a ɛma saa Abibiman mpaninfoɔ yi de obuo maa Mugabe.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛkae Mugabe ɛnam n’adapaatwa ne n’adwenkyerɛ a na ɔkyerɛ sɛ Mmɔroɔfo ho ne sɛdeɛ na ɔsi ka aman mpaninfoɔ a wɔwɔ aman bi te sɛ United States ne Britain anim si fa.
Sɛ obi wɔ Mugabe Zanu amanyɔkuo no mu na ɔyɛ deɛ ɛntene anaa ɔkasa tia wɔn a wɔnni aban mu a, wɔtwe n’ankasa kuo mma no anim.
Wɔde Mr Mugabe bɛto mpa mu Kwasiada ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔmfaa baabi a ɔwɔ ntoo dwa.
Adɔkotafoɔ ne nɛɛsefoɔ a wɔreyɛ adwuma wɔ aban ayaresabea de ato aban no anim sɛ, ɔpɛnimma bosome no kɔ awieeɛ na sɛ aban no antuaa wɔn ka a, wɔde wɔn mfidie bɛgu hɔ bosome a ɛdi yɛn anim yi ahyɛaseɛ.
Onipa a ɔda Zimbabwe dɔkotafoɔ kuo ano, Fortune Nyamande a ɔkyerɛ sɛ Zimbabwe anɛɛsefoɔ kuo no nso hyɛ wɔn ase no atwerɛ lɛtɛ de akɔma aban no wɔ deɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ no ho.
Dr Nyamande kaa sɛ watwerɛ lɛtɛ abɔ aban no amanneɛ ɛfa wɔn atuatie a ɛrehyɛ aseɛ ɔpɛpɔn da a ɛdi kan wɔ afe foforɔ no mu.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔne anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea na ɛredi saa dwumadie yi ɛsiane sɛ wɔnni sika wɔde bɛfa lɔɔre akɔ adwuma, ɛfiri sɛ wɔn akatua ne sika bi a aban no hyɛɛ wɔn bɔ sɛ ɔde bɛma wɔn no aka mu.
Dr Nyamande san nso twee aban no anim wɔ sɛ ɔde kwasafo dawubɔ rekata deɛ dawubɔ nkrataa de ato dwa no so.
ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ sikasɛm so, Patrick Chinamasa dii kan de bɛtoo dwa sɛ aban no ntumi ntua adwumayɛfoɔ bi ka afe yi mu ɛsiane sɛ sika nni hɔ.
Dr Nyamande se, “Owura Chinamasa faa koowa nkrataa so bɔɔ dawuro faa nsesaeɛ a aba akatua mmerɛ no mu, nti yɛbɛfa saa kwan no ara so.”
Koogyifoɔ a na ɛwɔ sɛ wɔnnya wɔn akatua Dwoada no nsa aka wɔn akatua ma wɔbɔ ho dawuro Benada yi. Nanso wɔn a wɔyɛ aban adwuma te sɛ adɔkotafoɔ ne anɛɛsefoɔ deɛ, wɔbɛtua wɔn ka afe a ɛda yɛn anim yi, ɔpɛpɔn da a ɛtɔ so num.
Nanso aban adwumayɛfoɔ pii a wɔne Studio 7 twetwee nkɔmmɔ no kyerɛ sɛ wɔnni gyidie sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn akatua mmerɛ a wɔahyɛ no.
Yɛntumi ne apɔmmuden soafoɔ, David Parirenyatwa ne apaadie soafoɔ, Prisɔah Mupfumira nnii nkɔmmɔ mfa kwan a wɔbɛfa so asi atuateɛ no ano.
MDɔ amanyɔkuo a ɛnni aban mu abɔ apolisifoɔ kwaadu sɛ wɔreteetee wɔn kuo mma.
Zimbabwe mmaranimfoɔ a wɔko ma nnipa yiedie de ato dwa sɛ, nnipa aduanan nson na wɔakye wɔn nansa yi a dodoɔ no ara yɛ MDɔ akyitaafoɔ, ɛnna nson yɛ asuafoɔ a wɔkɔ sukuu wɔ Allen Wilson a ɛwɔ Harare sɛ wɔreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ a yɛmmaa wɔn kwa.
Afoforɔ binom a wɔakye wɔn ne Makomborero Haruzivishe, kane suani kannifoɔ a ɔfiri ZINASU a ɔbaa kɔɔto nnɛ ne ne yɔnko Allan Moyo.
Yɛantumi ne apolisifoɔ kasamafoɔ Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi atwe nkɔmmɔ ɛfiri sɛ na wamfa ne tetefon ne yɛakasa.
Lɔya Innoɔent Gonese a ɔyɛ MDɔ lɔya kyerɛ sɛ, Haruzivishe ne Moyo bɛpuem wɔ kɔɔto Dwoada na wɔakɔ dwenedwene kɔɔto no agyinatuo no ho.
United Nations World Health Organization (WHOɔ ada no adi sɛ Corona virus kodiawuo a akum nnipa ahannu ne aduonu mmiɛnsa wɔ ɔhina no abɛyɛ amansan nyinaa adesoa.
Nna mmienu ni, nnipa 2000 na wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔanya Corona virus , na wiase mu nyinaa nso nnipa 9800 na wɔanya bi wɔ amn ahannu ne aduonan nan.
WHO krakye panin, Dr. Tedros Adhanom Ghebrevesus de berɛ na wɔwɔ gyidie sɛ ɔhina bɛyɛ deɛ ɔbɛtumi ayɛ biara asɔ yareɛ no ano no, na wɔsuro sɛ yareɛ no bɛtrɛ akɔ aman foforɔ mu. ɛbɛtumi akum nnipa bebree.
Apɔmmuden soafoɔ, Dr. Obadiah Moyo kyerɛ sɛ Zimbabwe de nnipa a wɔboro ahannu a wɔfiri ɔhina ne aman ahodoɔ so na afa mfidie mu ahwɛ sɛ, so wɔwɔ Corona virus anaasɛ wɔnni bi.
Nnipa a wɔreyɛ wɔn ho nhwehwɛmu wɔ Zimbabwe rehyɛ wɔn dan mu nnawɔtwe mmienu.
Apɔmmuden soafoɔ dadaa, Dr Henry Madzorera de too dwa sɛ Zimababwe hia sika pii a wɔde bɛsi yareɛ yi ano na antrɛ.
ɔmampanin dadaa Robert Mugabe amu bɛduru Harare Wukuada awia na wɔde da wɔbɛyɛ n’ayie no bɛto dwa.
Dawubɔ soafoɔ, Ms Moniɔa Mutsvangwa de asɛm yi too dwa berɛ a kabenɛt nhyiamu baa n’awieeɛ.
Mr Mutsvangwa de too dwa sɛ aban no agyinatuo reboaboa wɔn ho ama Owura Mugabe ayie no.
Wɔbisaa wɔn sɛ deɛn nti akye ansa na wɔrekasa afa Mugabe ayie no hɔ a, Mutsvangwa ne amannɔne soafoɔ Sibusiso Moyo de too dwa sɛ, “ɛnyɛ ne kwan so sɛ wɔbɛka berɛ a wɔbɛyɛ n’ayie berɛ a n’abusuafoɔ da so wɔ Singapore.”
ɔse aban no ne ɔmampanin Mugabe abusuafoɔ redi nsawɔsoɔ.
ɔhene Katizagombo kasamafoɔ, Gibson ɛenami kyerɛ sɛ ntawantawa biara nni Mugabe ayie no ho ɛsiane sɛ Emmerson Mnangagwa aban no na biribiara hyɛ wɔn nsa.
Wɔbɛsie Maɛor General Trust Mugoba a ɔfirii mu nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaa mu no Wukuada wɔ Heroes Acre burial ground a ɛwɔ Harare.
Nsɛm foforɔ mu no, aban no kyerɛ sɛ Zimababwefoɔ ɔha ne aduoson-nwɔtwe na wɔn ho aka wɔ South Africa ɛnam basabasaeɛ a ɛrekɔ so no, na Zimbabwefoɔ baanu na wɔahwere wɔn nkwa.
Moyo de too dwa sɛ aban no de nhyehyɛeɛ regu akwan mu sɛ wɔde wɔn a wɔafiri mu no amu bɛba fie.
Aban no san nso kyerɛ sɛ, wɔatua apɔmmuden adwumayɛfoɔ te sɛ adɔkotafoɔ ɔham nkyɛ mu aduosia wɔ wɔn adwuamayɛ ho. ɛnnɛ na kabenɛt no ayɛ n’adwene sɛ wɔbɛhyia apɔmmuden ne sikasɛm asoeɛ no na wɔatena ase ahwɛ sɛ wɔatua adwumayɛfoɔ ka sɛdeɛ ɛsɛ.
Apɔmmuden soafoɔ, Dr Obadiah Moyo de too dwa sɛ ɔne asoeɛ a wɔhwɛ sikasɛm so no bɛtena ase ahwɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ deɛ kabinɛt agye atom no.
Adɔkotafoɔ de wɔn mfidie guu fam nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaam no sɛ wɔn akatua nso.
Ekuo a wɔate sɛ wɔde hyɛ Itai Dzamara a na ɔko ma nnipa yiedie na ɔsan nso yɛ Oɔɔupy Africa Unity Square kannifoɔ dadaa animuonyam, Itai Dzamara Trust kaeɛ International Women’s Day nnɛ.
Dwumadie yi kɔɔ so wɔ Highfield na wɔmaa mmaa a wɔbaa dwumadie no ase no paade ne deɛ ɛkeka ho.
ɔkasamafoɔ ma Dzamara abusua no a ɔsan nso ka Itai Dzamara Trust bɔɔdo no ho, Mr Partson Dzamara de too Studio 7 anim sɛ ɔhunu no sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ ɔkyerɛ dɔ kyerɛ mmaa saa bosome no mu; mfeɛ nnum a ne nuabarima firii yeraa wɔ saa bosome no mu.
ɔse ɛwɔm sɛ ne nuabarima no de ne ho hyɛɛ amanyɔsɛm, nnipa yiedie ne dawubɔ adwuma mu, na ɔyɛɛ wie nyinaa wɔ ɔdɔ mu; na Itai Dzamara Trust bɛtoa ne nnwuma pa no so.
ɔkyerɛ n’adwumakuo no aba Highfields ɛfiri sɛ ɛhɔ na wɔwoo Itai na mmom wɔbɛkɔ mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ akɔboa mmaa ne wɔn a wɔnni bi wɔ mmara, nnwomasua ne apɔmmuden mu.
Wɔn a wɔbaa dwumadie no ase mu baako ne Remeberanɔe Zuze a ɔde too dwa sɛ, mfa ho sɛ wɔnhunuu Owura Dzamara no, n’ani agye dwumadie a ekuo no redi ho.
Abaayewa a wammɔ ne din de too Studio 7 anim sɛ, wasua nnoɔma bii wɔ nnɛ dwumadie no mu.
Partson Dzamara daa no adi sɛ, wɔbɛyɛ nkaedum de akae ne nuabarima a nkorɔfoɔ bi kyee no wɔ Glen View Benada wɔ Harare.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ, seisei deɛ wɔnnim baabi a ne nua no wɔ anaasɛ ɔte ase mpo a.
ɔde too dwa sɛ, wɔn a wɔne Itai Dzamara yɛɛ adwuma te sɛ polisifoɔ dwumakuo, nnipa a wɔpere nnipa yiedie, Zimbabwe Human Rights Commission ne afoforn na wɔbɛto wɔn nsa afrɛ wɔn.
Sɛ wiase nyinaa redi atukɔtenafoɔ da kyena no, Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔyɛ atukɔtenafoɔ wɔ South Africa deɛ, biribiara nni hɔ sɛ wɔdi ahurisie ɛnam nnoɔma bɔne a ɛrekɔ so wɔ South Africa no.
Zimbabwefoɔ no bi se South Africa mmu nhyehyɛeɛ wɔne akuo bi te sɛ United Nations sɛ wɔde obuo bɛma atukɔtenafoɔ no so.
ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Migrant Support Network, Shelton ɔhiyangwa, de too Studio 7 anim sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ atukɔtena da no ho hia no, atukɔtenafoɔ a wɔwɔ South Africa deɛ, wɔwɔ nkoasom mu.
ɔhiyangwa kaa sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔwɔ South Africa nso na wɔreteetee wɔn.
ɔde kaa ho sɛ n’adwumakuo ne Zimbabwefoɔ ne aman afoforɔ di dwuma pɛ nkrataa ma wɔn.
Zimbabwe Exemption Permits krakye panin, Gladys Mangwende de too dwa sɛ, n’adwumakuo n ani di atukɔtenafoɔ awɛɛnes nhyehyɛeɛ ho nanso n’ani nso di ankorɛankorɛ yiedie nso wɔnni soɔ no so.
ɔtitenani ma Human Rights Watɔh a ɛwɔ North Africa, Dewa Mavhinga se atukɔtenafoɔ da no ho hia wɔ South Africa ɛsiane Zimbabwefoɔ atukɔtenafoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu no nti.
Owura Mavhinga toaa so sɛ South Africa aban no ngu mmara no mu ne titire ne akwantuo mu.
Zimbabweni, George Manyika nso foaa Mavhinga asɛm no so.
Gabriel Shumba a ɔda Zimbabwe Exiles Forum ano de ato United Nations, AU ne SADɔ anim sɛ wɔmma wɔn ani nkɔ nnoɔma a ɛrekɔ so wɔ South Africa no, ne titire ne Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu.
Lions de dwanetoa kɔtoo South Africa amandwoeɛ soafoɔ, Aaron Motseledi anim sɛ ɔngu wɔn mmara sɛdeɛ atukɔtenafoɔ mmrɛ ansa wɔn nsa aka wɔn nkrataa.
ɔsrɛɛ nnipa yiedie kuo ahodoɔ sɛ wɔne ne dwumakuo no nka mmɔ na wɔnkɔ ma atukɔtenafoɔ yiedie.
Atukɔtenafoɔ no mu, Francis Mukono de too dwa sɛ, wanhunu mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ atukɔtena day no sɛ ɛnam asetena a wɔtem wɔ South Africa no.
Atukɔtenafoɔ foforɔ, Steven Chiweshe nso de too dwa sɛ wanhunu sɛ wɔde sekan rewɔ obi.
Mandela Madumise, South Africa krakye panin pa ara ɔhwɛ atukɔtenafoɔ nsɛm so kyerɛ sɛ n’asoeɛ no de ato United Nations Rights Council no anim sɛ wɔmmɛboa wɔn na wɔsi ɔhaw ahodoɔ a asoeɛ no refam no ano.
Madumise kyerɛ sɛ bosome no nkɔ awieeɛ no, n’asoeɛ no bɛhunu de ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ si ɔhaw yi ano.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ bɛyɛ mpem mmiɛnsa na wɔafiri South Africa a wɔkyerɛ sɛ aban no retiatia wɔn fahodie so.
Nanso Zimbabwe aban no se nnipa binom atu kɔ aman foforɔ so wɔrekɔpɛ adwuma papa bi ayɛ.
Wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ayaresabea a anɛɛsefoɔ ne adɔkotafoɔ ka ho ano de wɔn mfidie agu hɔ bɛyɛ nna aduasa mmiɛnsa a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn akatua no so, na wɔmfaa hwee ngu akwan mu sɛ wɔreyɛ biribi afa ho.
Deɛ ɛrekɔ so ayaresabea ahodoɔ mu no ano ayɛ den. Wɔde wɔn a wɔyare no resan akɔ fie ɛsiane sɛ wɔnnya ayarehwɛ.
Nnoɔma bɛsɛe asene sɛdeɛ nnoɔma teɛ no ɛsiane sɛ Senior Health Doctors associationnso sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi amfa adɔkotafoɔ yɛkyerɛ ne wɔn akatua no ho a, wɔn nso de wɔn mfidie bɛgu hɔ. Kasamafoɔ ma ekuo yi, Dr. Aaron Musara de too Studio 7 anim sɛ nnoɔma nkɔ yie wɔ ayaresabea hɔ.
Dr Musara kaa sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ watwerɛ krataa akɔma aban no asoeɛ ahodoɔ abɔ wɔn amanneɛ sɛ ɔbɛsi fam afiri n’akonnwa no so no, ɔnnyaa mmuaeɛ biara.
Anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea nso nkɔ adwuma, na wɔse aban no nyi Amerikafoɔ sika a wɔde brɛɛ no Ahinime wɔ 2018 no mu bi ntua wɔn ka. Afei nso sɛ wɔkɔ adwuma a, ɔmma wɔn akadeɛ mfa mmɔ wɔn ho ban mfiri yadeɛ no ho.
Enoɔk Dongo a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors associationkannifoɔ se wɔne aban ne nkɔmmɔ nkɔsii hwee.
Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors association(ZHDA) kasamafoɔ, Dr Tapiwa Mungofa nso kyerɛ sɛ ɛsiane sɛ aban no mma adɔkotafoɔ no nkɔ ayaresabea nti, wɔn a wɔyare no nnya ayarehwɛ.
Owura Mungofa de too dwa sɛ mmerɛ a anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmɔfra de wɔn mfidie guu hɔ no, wɔn adwumayɛfoɔ no dodoɔ no ara tenaa fie sɛ wɔrebɔ wɔn ho ban na wɔanya COVID-19.
Studio 7 antumi ne aban no antwetwe nkɔmmɔ anhunu kwan a wɔbɛfa so asiesie saa ɔhaw yi ɛsiane sɛ ɔsoafoɔ a na ɔhwɛ apɔmmuden so, ɔbenfoɔ Amon Murwira ntumi wɔn akasa wɔn tetefon so.
Nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaa mu no, Owura Murwira de too dwa sɛ ɔne nɛɛse baako ahyɛ aseɛ retwetwe nkɔmmɔ. N’abadiakyire John Mangwiro nso de too Studio 7 anim sɛ adwuma gu wɔn so pa ara nti wɔnti ne wɔn nkasa.
ɔtitenani ma Health Services Board, Dr Paulinus Sikosana nso kyerɛ sɛ wɔreyɛ nhyiamu fa COVID-19 kodiawuo no ho nti wɔntumi ne yɛn ntwetwe nkɔmmɔ.
Apɔmmuden animdefoɔ nso kyerɛ sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ aban no yɛ biribi ma anɛɛsefoɔ ba adwuma na wɔnasi anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmɔfra sɛ wɔredi wɔn ho dɛm ano berɛ a ɔman wɔ ahohiahia mu ɛsiane COVID-19 kodiawuo a ama nnipa aduonu num ahwere wɔn nkwa no.
ɔhinhoyi CityCouncil kyerɛ sɛ wɔayɛ ahoboa sɛ wɔbɛdi deɛ kɔɔto de too dwa Dwoada sɛ kansere no nsisi adan a wɔabubu agu wɔn kurom hɔ no.
Kansere no twerɛtwerɛfoɔ, Abel Gotora ne adwadifoɔ a ɔhinhoyi kansere abubu wɔn adan retwetwe nkɔmmɔ no, ɔde too dwa wɔbɛdi deɛ kɔɔto ahyɛ kansere no sɛ wɔnsi adan a adwadifoɔ no bi abubu no no.
Nanso Owura Gotora kaa sɛ kansere no nsi adan a wɔbubu no no nyinaa, na mmom wɔbɛsi deɛ haekɔɔto hyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnsi ma nnipa baasia a wɔde wɔn kɔɔ kɔɔto no.
Tafadwa Marimo, Emmanuel Ngwaru, Richard Svosve, Pepukayi Marega ne Devis Shopo ka wɔn a wɔde kansere no kɔɔ kɔɔto no ho bi.
Saa nnipa baasia yi mu baako, Emmanuel Gwaru de too dwa sɛ n’ani gyee atemmuo a kɔɔto no de baeɛ no ho ɛsiane sɛ aban ka kyerɛɛ kansere no wɔ wɔnsiesie mpɔtam hɔ, na wanka nkyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmmubu adan.
Owura Gwaru sɛ deɛ baako a ɔdi ho haw kɛseɛ pa ara ne sɛ ɔtua sika ma kansere no sɛ wɔmfa nsisi adan. Gadzema kansela Patricia ɔhibaya se n’ani gyee kɔɔto no atemmuo no hɔ ɛsiane sɛ na ɛyɛ no den sɛ ɔbɛdi deɛ mpɔtam hɔ soafoɔ hyɛɛ no sɛ ɔmmubu adan wɔ kurom hɔ. Mmerɛ korɔ no ara no nso, wɔmaa wɔn a adwadifoɔ a wɔabubu wɔn adan wɔ dwam hɔ hyɛden.
Owura Gotora de too dwa sɛ kansere no bɛsi dwam foforɔ ama adwadifoɔ aduonum wɔ Gadzema dwom hɔ.
Kasamafoɔ ma Zimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights, Kumbirai Mafunda se nnansa yi terafikɛs reba wɔn ɔfese wɔmmɛka wɔn nsɛm ma wɔn.
Kansere pii a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu rebubu adan a wɔamfa mmara kwan so asi no gu.
Na mmom adwadifoɔ a wɔwɔ wiase afanaa nyinaa rekɔ kɔɔto sɛ deɛ kanserefoɔ no reyɛ no nyɛ.
Kɔɔto peemu de n’atemmuo bɛtoo dwa Benada fa deɛ ɔnni MDɔ amanyɔkuo no anim ɛsiane sɛ Morgan Tsvangirai ahwere ne nkwa no, nnipa dodoɔ no ara rebisa sɛ hwan ankasa na Richard Morgan Tsvangirai anaa Harvest House yɛ no dea.
Kɔɔto no de too dwa sɛ Awuraa Thokozani Khupe nni MDC-T anim kɔpem sɛ wɔbɛto aba bosome mmiɛnsa ntam.
Na mmom nnipa a wɔbɛkɔ amanyɔkuo no asoeɛ kɛseɛ mu no ayɛ den kakra ɛsiane nnipa baanu a wɔredi dwuma wɔ hɔ a wɔn din ne Ian Makone ne Reverend Tim Neil (na ɔda Church of the Province of Central Africa anaa ɔPɔA anoɔ.
MDɔ Alliance twerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin, Charlton Hwende gye di sɛ saa nnipa baanu yi na asoeɛ hɔ hyɛ wɔn nsa na wɔn nko ara na wɔbɛtumi akɔ hɔ.
Douglas Mwonzora a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no twerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin a ɛbaa amanyɔkuo no mu wɔ 2014 nso kyerɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo no hyɛ Makone ne Neil nsa.
Na mmom wɔse wɔgye di sɛ wɔmma wɔn kwa ma wɔkɔyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ. Yɛntumi ne Owura Makone ne Owura Neil ntwetwe nkɔmmɔ ntie wɔn nso ano asɛm.
MDɔ ɔtitenani abadiakyire, ɛob Sikhala kyerɛ sɛ asebɔ aba St Marys a ɛwɔ ɔhitungwiza mpɔtam a ama amanyɔkuo no akyitaafoɔ redwane afiri wɔn afie mu.
Sikhala a na ɔyɛ Zengeza West mmarahyɛbɛdwani kyerɛ sɛ polisi ɔfesa a wɔfrɛ no ɛabangwe repɛ amanyɔkuo no akyitaafoɔ akye wɔn.
Yɛbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ yɛne Owura ɛabangwe bɛtwetwe nkɔmmɔ nso na ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔyi sɛ nsɛmmisa no ano.
Studio 7 antumi ne apolisifoɔ kasamafoɔ, Assistant Commissioner Paul Nyathi ntwetwe nkɔmmɔ anhunu deɛ nti a polisini yi pɛ sɛ wɔkye akyitaafoɔ yi.
Na mmom ayɛ atesɛm sɛ kye a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkye MDɔ akyitaafoɔ asekyerɛ ne sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔgyae ɔyɛkyerɛ a wɔayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛyɛ no wɔ aman no nyinaa mu.
Sikhala a wɔkyee no bosome a ɛtwaa mu a soboɔ a wɔde bɔɔ no ne sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔtu Emmerson Mnangagwa aban gu no de ato Studio 7 anim sɛ, nnipa dodoɔ no ara na wɔredwane afiri wɔn afie mu ɛsiane sɛ wɔsuro sɛ wɔbɛkye wɔn.
Nnipa boro aduokron na wɔkyee wɔn wɔ Harare Fiada ɛsiane ɔyɛkyerɛ a MDɔ yɛeɛ saa da no.
MDɔ pɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ wɔ kuropɔn a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nanso apolisifoɔ de Public Order ne Seɔurity Actno mpɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo no bɛtoa ɔyɛkyerɛ no so.
Apolisifoɔ no de taaboɔ ato MDɔ so sɛ mma wɔnyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ wɔ Harare, Bulawayo, Gweru ne Masvingo.
Amanyɔsɛm mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmufoɔ kyerɛ sɛ wei nso bɛtumi asi wɔ Mutare a MDɔ ayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ wɔ hɔ da Yawoada no.
Haekɔɔto agyina mmarahyɛbadwafie mmara fa aban afe sikasɛm ntotoeɛ ho atu ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ atetenee so Ziyambi Ziyambi ne ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ sikasɛm so, Mthuli Nɔube asɛm ɛsiane sɛ wɔn na wɔbɔɔ MDC-T a Thokozani Khupe da ano no dwetire.
Haekɔɔto temmuafoɔ, Priscilla Munangati Manongwa de too dwa Yawoada no sɛ wɔtu Ziyambi ne Nɔube asɛn na wɔntumi nnyina MDC-T anan mu, ɛsiane wɔkyerɛ sɛ Amanyɔkuo Sikasɛm Mmara ma wɔn ho kwan ma wɔbɔ amanyɔkuo dwetire.
Na MDɔ nsa bɛka R7,500M wɔ RTGS mu.
Animdefoɔ se Nelson ɔhamisa MDɔ kɔɔ kɔɔto berɛ Awuraa Khupe afa no twerɛ nkrataa kɔɔ sikakorabea sɛ wɔreyi ɔhamisa akyitaafoɔ afiri wɔn a wɔtumi sae ma wɔyi sika firi amanyɔkuo no sika wɔ Steward Bank no mu.
Luke Tamborinyoka a ɔyɛ ɔhamisa MDC-T kasamafoɔ abadiakyire de too dwa sɛ n’ani agye atemmuo no ho.
Nso Morgen Komiɔhi a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kannifoɔ de too dwa sɛ, ɔde nhyehyɛeɛ bɛgu akwan mu akɔgye sika ɛsiane sɛ ɔn na ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kannifoɔ (ne sɛ nti ne sɛ kɔɔto peemu de bɛtoo dwa sɛ ɔhamisa amfa amanyɔkuo anni mmara a ɛwɔ amanyɔkuo no mmara kunini so nti ɔnni ho kwan sɛ ɔdi amanyɔkuo no animɔ.
Nso Owura Tamborinyoka se ɔhamisa bɛtumi agye sika no bi ɛfiri sɛ MDɔ mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ faa nam ne din so na wɔkɔɔ mmarahyɛbadwafie.
Nanso Komiɔhi kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ ɔhamisa ne afoforɔ no di mmara no so.
Nanso so, Harare mmaranimni, Kudazi Kadzere kaa sɛ wɔbɛtumi adwane atoa agyinaeɛ a wɔsii no wɔ asɛnnibea no nnafua du ntam.
Ziyambi ka kyerɛɛ studio 7 wɔ ahomatorɔfoɔ so sɛ wɔbɛtumi ato nkyea wɔ nsɛm a asɛnnifoɔ no hyɛeɛ wɔ nnafua du ntam.
Yɛntumi ne ɛaɔob Mudenda a ɔyɛ mmarahyɛbadwafie tetini ne ɔsaofoɔ a ɔhwɛ sikasɛm nkae ntie wɔn nso asɛm ɛsiane sɛ wɔn din wɔ asɛnnie krataa mu no.
mmaranimfoɔ bi nso de kyerɛ sɛ wɔamfa wɔn nsɛnkae ama a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔnnye asɛm no ntom mu a, kɔɔto no de sika no bɛma ɔhamisa MDɔ.
6.Wei nyɛ da a edi kan MDɔfoɔ reko sika yi ho.
Ɛwɔ afe 2006 mu no, akyire yi a MDɔfoɔ twerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin Welshman Nɔube ko tia Tsuangirai wɔ Ahinime bosome a ɛwɔ 2005 mu na ɔtee n'ankasa MDɔ. }kɔɔ so gyee sika a na ɛfiri MDɔ kuo no hɔ,maa Mr. Ysvangirai a ɔda dɔm dodoɔ ano wɔ mmarahyɛbadwafie annya sika biara.
Zimbabweni, Dr Rita Nyampinya a ɔka Female Prisoners Suport Trust a wɔko ma mmaa wɔ fiase kaa sɛ n’ani agye sɛ ɔnyaa 2020 International Women of ɔourage Award no.
Abasobɔdeɛ yi kae nnwuma pa a mmaa wɔwɔ wiase afanaa yɛeɛ na United State Dpartment of International Relation na wɔde abasobɔdeɛ yi ma.
Dr Nyampinga kaa sɛ wanna annwene ho da sɛ ɔbɛnya saa abasobɔdeɛ yi, na ɔkaa sɛ ɛyɛ no anigye pa ara sɛ yɛbɛkan ano aka mmaa dubaako a wɔfiri ewiase afanaa nyinaa ho.
Dr Nyampiga kaa sɛ wɔbɛtu kwan akɔ afiase ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ United State akɔsua sɛdeɛ afiase hɔ tebea sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛtumi amia wɔn ho ayɛ wɔn adwuma wɔ man mu..
Dr Nyampinga kaa sɛ wɔn adwuma no hia akokoɔduro na afei nso wɔn ani agye sɛ afoforɔ ahu wɔn nnwuma a wɔreyɛ.
Berɛ a ɔkasa wɔ dwabɔ no ase no, ɔtwerɛfoɔ ma State of International Relations, Miɔhael Pompeo kaa sɛ adwuma a mmaa dummienu yi ayɛ yɛ anisɔ na ɛhia akokoɔduru.
Wɔpaa dwumadie yi ho ntoma wɔ mfirihyia dunan a abɛsene kɔ mu.
Mmaa wɔn nsa aka saa abasobɔdeɛ yi bi firi Afghanistan, Armenia, Azerbaiɛan, Bolivia, Burkina Faso, Kazakhstan, Malaysia, Niɔaragua, Pakistan, Syria, Yemen ne Zimbabwe.
Mr Pompey kaa sɛ saa dwumadie yi ho hia ɛfiri sɛ ɛma mmaa akwannya sɛ wɔmfa nyɛ adwuma mfa nko mma mmaa yiedie wɔ ewiase afanaa nyinaa.

Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ amu no bɛba fie anɔpa tutuutu.

Nanso wei ne deɛ Leo Mugabe kaeɛ sɛ Mugabe amu no bɛwɔ n’abusuafoɔ kɔpem sɛ wɔbɛwie amena a ɛsom bo a wɔbɛsie no wɔ mu no bɔ abira.

Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ Mugabe amu no bɛwɔ Zyimba da koro na akyire no, wɔde bɛba Harare, baabi a wɔbɛsie no no.
Leo Mugabe de too dwa sɛ nnipa abɛhia wɔ faako wɔ ɔmampanin Mugabe fie a ɛwɔ Harare.
Ekuo ba baako a ɔka MDC-T amanyɔkuo a ɛnni aban a Nelson ɔhamisa da ano na ɔrehwɛ anim sɛ ɔbɛwu wɔ Zyimba nnɛ, Lloyd Tarubwa a ɔfiri Banket a wɔkyeree no de siiɛ bosome nkron wɔ berɛ a wɔamfa no ankɔ kɔɔto kaa sɛ, wɔbaeɛ sɛ ɔrebɛhwɛ sɛ ɔmampanin Mugabe awu ampa ara.
Sɛdeɛ wɔsi yɛɛ Owura Mugabe ayie no ayɛ nnipa pii nwanwa wɔ ɔman no mu. Wɔsusu sɛ amanneɛ a Owura Mugabe faa mu berɛ ɔte akonnwa soɔ na ɛde ne wuo no baeɛ.
Owura Mugabe wui wɔ Singapore wɔ bosome a ɛtɔ so nkron no mu, ne da a ɛtɔ so nsia mu berɛ a na yare abɔ no ato hɔ mmerɛ tenten bi.
Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ nkabom kuo a wɔfrɛ wɔn Amalgamted Rural Teachers Union anaa ARTUZ wɔ Zimbabwe se wɔn panin baako a wɔfrɛ no Godfrey ɔhanda no, nnipa a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu kyee no maa no dii apolisifoɔ akakye dɔnhwere mmienu a onipa biara ante ho hwee.
Nanso wɔagyae ɔhanda a ɔka ARTUZ kɔmitee no ho wɔ Mfimfini mantam no mu aberɛ a wɔhyɛɛ no ketee sɛ mma ɔne koogyifoɔ a wɔwɔ Gweru nhyia.
ARTUZ panin paa Obert Masaraure kaa sɛ yi a wɔayi ɔhanda adi no firi atua a koogyifoɔ no teeɛ no danee nnafua mmiɛna a na nka ɛwɔ sɛ ɛyɛ nnafua mmienu.
Masaraure se, koogyifoɔ no kuo no bi nso rete atua sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ wɔde bɛboa ekuo no.
ɔyɛkyerɛ no baa awieeɛ Wukuada.
Nanso Masaraure kaa sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiamu wɔ atuateɛ no akyi na wɔde adwwene anammɔn a wɔbɛtuo ho.
Yɛntumi nhyiaa ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ apaadie so, Awuraa Sekai Nzenza na yɛabisa no aban no gyinaberɛ wɔ asɛm no ho nanso ɔmfa ne tetefon no.
Firi a Fɔ Platinum afiri ɔAF Champions League no mu no ama amanfoɔ rebisa nsɛm pii fa Zimbabwe bɔɔlobɔ ho.
ɛwɔ mu sɛ aka agokansie mmienu wɔ akansie no mu deɛ, nyɛ Fɔ Platinum bɛtumi ne Esperanɔe a ɔwɔ mma nwoɔtwe anaa wɔbɛtumi adi Horoya Athletiɔ ɔlub a ɔwɔ mma nson so nkonim. Wɔdii nkoguo wɔ wɔn ankasa fie ne ɔman foforɔ so wɔ Horoya nso ano. ɛyɛ agokansie a ɛdi kan a wɔbɛhwɛ sɛ bɔɔlobɔ kuo yi nyinaa nya mma no pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Mprɛprɛn yi deɛ, Fɔ Platinum anya aba no baako pɛ afiri agokansie nnan mu nti wɔresi akan a aka no de apɛ animuonyam afiri bɛhwɛadeni Spenɔer Mushambadope hɔ.
Mushambadope se wɔnnya aba biara mfiri agokansie a aka no mu.
Afe a atwam no, bɔɔlobɔ kuo yi ara na wɔfirii mu wɔ akansie no fa a ɛdi kan. Angola Primeiro de Agosto na wɔyii wɔn firii mu berɛ a na Lunda ahyɛ wɔn bio wɔ wɔn fie.
Afe mpem mmienu ne du nson mu no, ɔaps United duru akansie no nketewa mu anso ɛkaa akuo nnɔtwe no, na wɔnka ho ɛfiri sɛ Al Ahli Tripoli a wɔfiri Lybia bɛhyɛɛ wɔn ɛka nnan maa wɔtee mu mmienu wɔ wɔn ankasa fie.
Saa afe no ara mu no, Ngezi Platinum Stars a na wɔresi Zimbabwe anan mu wɔ ɔaf ɔonfederation mu no firii akansie wɔ ɔfa a ɛdi kan no mu wɔ berɛ a Angola Libolo dii wɔn so nkonim.
Afe mpem mmienu ne dunsia mu no, Harare Citya na wɔwɔ akansie korɔ no ara mu no firii mu wɔ ɔfa a ɛdi kan no ara mu. Zanaɔo a wɔwɔ Zambia na ɔhyɛɛ wɔɔn ɛka mmienu maa wɔtee mu baako wɔ Rufaro Stadium na ɛkɔwie 3-1 wɔ Zambia.
Wei kyerɛ sɛ bɔɔlobɔ kuo a wɔwɔ kurom ha no ntumi nnyina Abibiman bɔɔlobɔ kuo a aka no anim sɛdeɛ na mfeɛ a atwam no Dynamos tumi sii akan yie tumi kɔduruu ɔaf Champions League agokansie a ɛtwa toɔ wɔ afe apem ɔha nkron aduokron nwɔtwe mu, ɛnna afe mpem mmienu ne nwɔtwe mu nso wɔduruu semi-finals.
Deɛ ɛyɛ ya kɛseɛ mpo ne sɛ, Fɔ Platinum anya aba baako pɛ wɔ agokansie nnan mu, wɔnnyaa aba baako mpo. Bio, wɔahere mma nsia wɔ agokansie nnan mu.
Asɛmmia no ne sɛ, sɛ bɔɔlobɔ kuo bi redi bɔɔlobɔ kuo nkaeɛ a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe no nyinaa so nkonim na wɔreda saa mmɔdemmɔ wei adi wɔ Abibirem a, na deɛn na ɛreka afa ɔman no bɔɔlobɔ ho?
ɔaps United kyitaani pa ara, Tinashe Musebi se, sɛdeɛ bɔɔlobɔ aba fam no, ɛhia nkanyan bebree ansa na Zimbabwe bɔɔlobɔ kuo ahodoɔ no ayɛ mmɔfra ama Lesotho, Botswana ne Swaziland.
Bɔɔlobɔ mu nkratoni Farai Kambamura se, Zimababwe bɔɔlobɔ kuo ahodoɔ no ntumi nsi akan wɔ Abibirem ɛfiri sɛ bɔɔlobɔfoɔ a wɔboaa wɔn maa wɔgyee nkurowa no nyinaa rekɔ amannɔne, titire South Africa berɛ a wɔresi akan wɔ Abibirem.
Afe a ɛtwam no, Fɔ Platinum hweree Gerald Takwara, Elvis ɔhipezeze ne Talent ɔhawapiwa. Afe wei nkoguo a wɔdii no wɔ Rodwell ɔhinyafanere a ɔgyee abasobɔdeɛ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Baroka.
Nanso John ɔhikoɔhi a ɔdii Lengthens bɔɔlobɔ kuo no anim ma wɔgyee Premier Soɔɔer League no kaa sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ Zimbabwe pagya ne bɔɔlobɔ akansie no mu wɔ ɔman no mu sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a bɔɔlobɔ kuo ahodoɔ no bɛtumi atua wn bɔɔlobɔ akatua a ɛbɛsi wɔn kwan sɛ wɔbɛtu kwan akɔ South Africa ne Zambia.
Seisei ara deɛ, Zimbabwe wɔ bɔɔlobɔ agokansie ahodoɔ mmienu pɛ, ɔastle Lager Premier Soɔɔer League ne ɔhibuku Super ɔup. Afe a ɛtwa toɔ a wɔbɔɔ Zifa ɔup no yɛ afe mpem mmienu ne num mu.
Bɔɔlobɔ kyitaani Musa Masepe se Zimbabwe nni bɔɔlobɔ akyɛdeɛ na ɛbinom pɛ sɛ wɔto nwom anaa ade foforɔ bi ɛfiri sɛ wɔn akatua no nso wɔn.
Se wei toa so a, ɛbɛkyɛ ansa na ɔman no mu bɔɔlobɔ kuo ahodoɔ no atumi ne Abibiman nkaeɛ no asi akan.
Abatoɔ a ɛresi Democratic Party anan mu wɔ US abatoɔ a wɔde reyi ɔmampanin wɔ Obubuo bosome mu no ayɛ abɛfuo ɛfiri to a wɔtoo aba no maa New York Mayor Miɔhael Bloomberg.
Bloomberg a wabɛyɛ ɔdefoɔ pa ara no ankɔgyina wɔ by-election wɔ n’amanyɔkuo no din mu wɔ abatoɔ a eɔde reyi ɔmampanin a RePublican amanyɔkuo kasamafoɔ Donald Trump nso bɛpre bi no.
Owura Bloomberg de too dwa Obubuo bosome no mu afe a atwam no sɛ, wɔreba amanyɔkuo no mu. ɔde sika a ɛboro $400M bɔɔ ho dawuro. Saa sika no yɛ wɔn dea.
ɔsikani no annyina wɔ by-election wɔ Iowa ne New Hampshire. Saa ara nso na wannyina wɔ by-election wɔ Navada ne South ɔarolina, berɛ a ɔbɛnem abatoɔ no reba wɔ aberɛ a mantam dunan na wɔbɛto aba ayi deɛ ɔbɛgyina Democratic Party amanyɔkuo no anan mu wɔ ɔmampanin abatoɔ no mu.
Berɛ a Bloomberg yɛɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛkɔ akɔpre dibea no, amanyɔkuo no mma dadaa te sɛ Berniɔe Sanders a ɔgyina Vermont anan mu wɔ senɛte ne Elizabeth Warren a ɔgyina Massaɔhusetts anan mu wɔ senɛt, hyɛɛ aseɛ kaa n’abakɔsɛm ho nsɛmmɔne.
ɔrekasa wɔ berɛ a Nevada amanyɔkuo nhyiamu kɛseɛ no reba no, Owura Sanders kaa sɛ, sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a n’amanyɔkuo no bɛtumi adi Owura Trump so nkonim no, wɔhia obi a ɔbɛtumi aboaboa ɛdɔm pii ano kyɛn deɛ asi biara wɔ AmErica abakɔsɛm mu.
Owura Sanders kaa sɛ Owura Bloomberg yɛ obi a wɔnim no yie wɔ New York mɛyɔ adwene a ɔfaeɛ sɛ ɔbɛtwe no sensɛn na wahwehwɛ Abibifoɔ ne Latinos a na ɔnyɛ no yie. ɔkaa sɛ saa anammɔntuo yi mmoa ma amanfoɔ pii nto aba sɛ wɔntu Trump adeɛ so wɔ Obubuo bosome no mu.
Nanso Bloomberg bɔɔ Owura Sanders nsɛm no guiiɛ kaa sɛ Owura Sanders a ɔredi abatoɔ no anim no, wɔayi no sɛ Democratic Party amanyɔkuo no kannifoɔ wɔ ɔmampanin abatoɔ no mu a ɛbɛwɔ Owura Trump hɔ mfeɛ nnan a ɛdi yɛn anim no.
Amanyɔsɛm mpɛnsɛmpɛsɛnmuni a ɔyɛ Zanu PF kuo ba, Frank Guni kaa sɛ, ɛda adi pefee sɛ akansie no ankasa gyina Sanders ne Bloomberg ntam. ɛwɔ mu sɛ na ɛda adi pefee sɛ seisei deɛ Sanders wɔ akyitafoɔ pii.
Guni se n’adwene mu no, ɛwɔ sɛ Bloomberg ne Sanders gyina wɔ ɔmampanin abatoɔ no mu bɔm sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛtumi adi Trump so nkonim.
Nnipa binom a wɔagyina wɔ Democratic Party amanyɔkuo no mu se: Baraɔk Obama nsiananmu dadaa, ɛoe Biden; Minnesota senɛta Amy Klobuɔhar ne mɛyɔ dada a na ɔwɔ South Bend wɔ Indiana ne gɛɛni Pete Buttigieg.
Democratic Party amanyɔkuo no wɔ 3,979 dɛligetes, na ansa na wɔbɛtumi ayi obi sɛ ɔnni amanyɔkuo no anim wɔ ɔmampanin abatoɔ no mu no, ɛwɔ sɛ ɔnya 1,990 dɛlegates.
Deɛ ɛka dɛligetes no ho bio ne sɛ, yɛwɔ dɛligates soronko ɛbɛyɛ a sɛ Democratic nhyiamu ba so wɔ Kitawonsa bosome mu wɔ Wisɔonsin a, ɛwɔ sɛ dɛligete 4,750 ne nhwɛsofoɔ, na nipa a wɔbɛto aa ayi no wɔ nhyiamu no ase no, ɛwɔ sɛ ɔnya 2,200.
Nnipa pii na wɔkɔ sikakorabea ntɛm anɔpa a wɔn gyidie ne sɛ ɛbɛma wɔn ho kwan wɔ wiase sikakoreabea kɛseɛ nanso wɔn nsusuiiɛ amma mu.
Nhwehwɛmu a Studio 7 ayɛ wɔ sikakorabea ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ Harare, Bulawayo, ɔhinhoyi, Masvingo, Mutare, Gweru ne nkuropɔn nkaeɛ kyerɛ sɛ, sikakorabea biara nni hɔ a wɔannya sika foforɔ no na sikakorabea dodoɔ no ara ntumi mmaa nkurɔfoɔ no dada no nso.
ɛossam Marwira a ɔyɛ sikakorabea adwumayɛfoɔ no mu baako kaa sɛ, watwɛn sika no ara da koro firi mmerɛ ɔtee no wɔ kaseɛbɔ so sɛ wɔde sika foforɔ reba.
Owura Marwira de too dwa sɛ na ɛho hia no yie sɛ ɔbɛtɔ sika wɔ mmɔtene so na ɔkaa sɛ ɛbɛyɛ sɛ amanfoɔ te sɛ ɔno bɛtumi anya sika afiri sikakorabea kwa.
Owura bi a ɔtɔ na watɔn sika wɔ mmɔtene so a ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔde ne din bɛto dwa nso kaa kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ na ɔrehwɛ sika foforɔ no anim nanso wanhu hwee.
RBZ, sikakorabea baatan de too dwa nansa yi ara sɛ, ɛbɛda sikakora ho nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ adi a wɔgye di sɛ ɛbɛte ɔman no hia so.
Amrado a ɔda RBZ ano, John Mangudya de ato dwa sɛ, ɔde $2M bɔndo bɛba ɛnne $2.5 bɔndo a nka ɛwɔ sɛ ɛba nnɛ.
Bankers associationof Zimbabwe krakye panin, Webster Rusere de too dwa sɛ, wɔnhwɛ sɛ sikakorabea no mu bi nsa aka sika no anaa, na ɔse RBZ nko ara na wɔde asɛm no too dwa.
Sika ho adwuma a wɔmfa kwan pa so nyɛ no de akyinigyeɛ aba ɔman no mu. ɛbinom sɛ ɛbɛboa nnipa a sika nti wɔredi awerɛhoɔ nanso ɛbinom se ɛyɛ asotwe ho nhwɛsoɔ.
Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔka kaa wɔ South Africa ho adwiri wɔn yie ɛsiane kaa a wɔrehyehye no a wɔsusu sɛ ɛyɛ South Africa ɔman mma no bi a wɔmpɛ sɛ ahɔhoɔ bɛnya adwuma ayɛ.
South Africa soafoɔ a ɔhwɛ apolisifoɔ so, Bheki Jele; ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ akwantuo soɔ, Fikile Mbalula; ne ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ apaadie so, Thulas Nxesi ne ahyɛnkafoɔ a wɔka lɔɔre akɛseɛ yɛ nhyiamu. Wɔn a wɔrepɛ adwuma ne adwumawuranom bɔɔ wɔn kɔkɔ sɛ wɔntwe wɔn a wɔrehye lɔɔre akɛseɛ no aso.
Jele bɔɔ ahyɛnkafoɔ a wɔka ahyɛn akɛseɛ kɔkɔ sɛ, ɛgya a wɔasɔ no bɛma wɔakye wɔn ɛfiri sɛ wɔresɛe ɔman no sikasɛm.
Nanso dɔnhwere mmienu akyi no a wɔkasa wiee no, wɔhyee kaa kɛseɛ wɔ N2 wɔ Durban.
ɔkasamafoɔ ma polisi, Superinendent Parboo Sewpersad de too dwa sɛ wɔahye ɛhyɛn foforɔ.
Nnawɔtwe awieeɛ yi, ahyɛn du nwɔtwe, deɛ Zimbabwefoɔ no mpɛ koraa no, wɔde gya too mu wɔ KwaZulu-Natal ne Gauteng.
Titenani ma Zimbabwe Exiles Forum, Gabriel Shumba kaa sɛ, wɔahye ahyɛn wɔ akwantepɔn a ɛwɔ SA na wɔatoto akwan no mu.
ɔregyina South Africa Zimbabwe Exemption Permits anan mu, Edward Muɔhatuta de too dwa sɛ saa asɛm no siiɛ, ɔne ahyɛnkafoɔ ahodoɔ bi nso yɛɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔrefrɛ aban no se ɔmmra asɛm no mu.
Ahyɛnkafoɔ no mu baako, George Nanyika afrɛ sɛ wɔantwetwe nkɔmmɔ.
Davie Munadawafa, ɔhyɛnkafoɔ no mu baako nso de too dwa sɛ ɔsuro sɛ ɔbɛhwere ne nkwa.
Munadawafa toaa so kaa sɛ ahyɛnkafoɔ dodoɔ no ara nnim wɔn daakye.
South Africa polisi panin, Bheki Jele bɔɔ kɔkɔ sɛ apolisifoɔ de nhyehyɛeɛ ano yɛ den bɛgu akwan mu atia wɔn a wɔrehyehye ahyɛn no. Wei na ɛboa maa wɔn aka no gyaeɛ deɛ wɔreyɛ.
Lions ka kyerɛ Studio 7 sɛ, asɛm no yɛ deɛ asi pɛ a ɛne sɛ South Africa kuro mma no aka dada sɛ aman foforɔ so nnipa ntu mfiri ɔman no mu.
Shumba nso abɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ soboɔ sɛ wɔatumi anyi ɔman no asotire wɔ asɛm no ho.
Lions toaa so kaa sɛ, wɔn adwumakuo no atwerɛ krataa akɔma ahɔhoɔ asoeɛ a ɛwɔ South Africa ne Zimbabwe a wɔreka akyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ adwuma mmɔ mu na wɔntu saa ɔhaw yi ase.
Dewa Mavhinga a ɔyɛ Human Rights Watɔh mantam kwankyerɛfoɔ wɔ Abibirem Atifi kasaa tiaa saa asɛm yi na ɔtuu obiara a ɔde ɛhyɛn di dwuma fo sɛ mma wɔntu kwan anadwo.
ɔman no sikasɛm a atɔ ape na ɛrema Zimbabwefoɔ atu kwan sɛ wɔrekɔpɛ adwuma ayɛ wɔ South Africa. Wei de basabasaeɛ aba ɛfiri sɛ South Africa kuro mma rekasa sɛ ahɔhoɔ mma wɔnnya adwuma nyɛ.
Kɔɔto ahyɛ polisi sɛ, mma wɔmfa ɛson nto Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors’ associationkrakye panin Dr. Peter Magombeyi so sɛ ɔnkɔ South Africa nkɔgye ayaresa ɛsiane sɛ nkorɔfoɔ bi kyee no siiɛ boroo no wɔ ɛbɔ bosome da a ɛtɔ so du nan no mu.

Nnipa a wɔte nkuraase wɔ Gwanda a ɛwɔ Matabeleland anaafoɔ fam ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ, mpontuo titire biara nni ha a ɛrekɔ so wɔ aban no berɛ so na ankorɛankorɛ nnwumakuo na wɔrebɔ wɔn ho mmɔden kakra.

Zimbabwe ne wiase amansan nyinaa kɔbɔɔ mu dii International Women’s day a mmaa bebree reka sɛ wɔtaa ka wɔn hyɛ ɛfiri sɛ mpaninfoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nnwene wɔn ho na wamma wɔn nyinaa akwannya korɔ.
ɛwɔ mu sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ wɔn mmara kunini a ɛma mmaa ne mmarima nyinaa akwannya pɛpɛɛpɛ deɛ, nanso mmaa no bebree a yɛne wɔn kasaeɛ no kyerɛ sɛ wɔn ho nhia aban mu nnipa, amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ, ansɔre ahodoɔ anaa nnwumakuo a wɔbɛhwɛ sɛ saa adeɛ yi bɛsi.
mmarahyɛbɛdwani dadaa a ɔsan nso yɛ mmaranimfoɔ, Awuraa ɛessy Maɛome ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ, mmaa wɔ ahokyerɛ kɛseɛ mu wɔ ɔman no mu ɛsiane yi a mmarima ayi wɔn totwene wɔ mpaninnie mu.
Wɔse akwannya kɛseɛ wɔ hɔ sɛ ɔman no bɛtumi ama ɛkwan a ɛda mmaa ne mmarima ntam no abɛn sɛ wɔdi mmara no so a.
ɔpanin a ɔda Zimbabwe Women Lawyers associationano, Abigail Matsvai ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛnnɛ yɛ da a ɛho hia yie nawɔde rehyɛ aban mpaninfoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔnni mmara a ɛma mmarima ne mmaa akwannya a ɛyɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ no so.
Mmaa ne Mmarima badwakuo no mu kuo mma no mu baako, Awuraa Tsungirai Hungwe-ɔhimbunde de too Studio 7 anim sɛ, nkyerɛkyerɛ a ɛmu da ho bɛhia sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛkyerɛ amanfoɔ mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ akwannya pɛ a ɛda mmaa ne mmarima ntam.
ɔse n’asoeɛ no rebɔ mmɔden yie sɛ wɔne amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ bɛtwetwe nkɔmmɔ na wɔama mmaa akwannya pɛ wɔ abatoɔ no mu sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a mmaa dodoɔ no ara bɛtumi apere akonnwa.
Afe yi fa a wɔrehyɛ no asɛntitire ne Think Equal, Build Smart, Innovate for ɔhange.
Awura Maɛome kyerɛ sɛ sɛdeɛ asɛntitire no siiɛ no, ɛwɔ sɛ abatoɔ kɔmisa no de ne tumi boa ma mmaa ne mmarima nya nkonnwa dodoɔ pɛ wɔ 2023 abatoɔ no mu.
Awuraa Matsvai nso afoa saa nsesaeɛ kuo yi so wɔ akannifoɔ dibea mu.
Awura Maɛome kaa bio sɛ, ɛwɔ sɛ mmaa ka wɔn ho bɔ mu na wɔako wɔn ko bɔm na wɔama mmarima aka wɔn ahyɛ.
ɔkaa sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ mmarima dodoɔ no ara wɔwɔ amanyɔkuo no mu mpɛ sɛ wɔpɛ firi hɔ, na ɛno nti na wɔne mmaa wɔwɔ hɔ no rede ham so. Wei nti na mmaa no ntumi nkɔpere diberɛ bi.
Wɔdi International Women’s Day ɔbenem da a ɛtɔ so nwɔtwe afe biara. Wɔdi saa da yi kyerɛ mmaa mpontuo wɔ dwadie, amanyɔsɛm ne dwumadie afoforɔ mu, na wɔde kyerɛ sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ mmaa nya akwannya mmarima nya no bi.
Wɔdi dwumadie yi a aban nsa hyɛ aseɛ wɔ Gokwe a ɛwɔ Midlands mpɔtam no na nnwumakuo ahodoɔ no diiɛ no mmeaeɛ mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ. MDɔ kannifoɔ Nelson ɔhamisa nso diiɛ wɔ ɔhitungwiza.
Dawubɔ nnwuma a Zimbabwe Human Right Commission ka ho nso de too dwa sɛ, ɛyɛ den sɛ mmaa bɛkɔ wɔn anim ɛsiane sɛ sikasɛm ho nsɛm mma wɔn kwan.
Zimbabwe peace Prroject nso de wɔn anodisɛm ɛfa dwumadie no baeɛ sɛ wɔreko atia wɔn a wɔtiatia nnipa yiedie so nkanka deɛ ɛkɔɔ so ɔpɛpɔn mu berɛ a na ɔyɛkyerɛ rekɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa.
Apaadie kɔɔto ama mmɔfra a wɔnkɔ adwuma no dɔnhwere aduanan nwɔtwe sɛ wɔmfa nkɔ adwuma ɛsiane sɛ wɔn atuateɛ no mfa mmara kwan so.
Apaadie atemmuafoɔ Rodgers Manyangadze ne Lawrenɔe Murasi ama adɔkotafoɔ nna mmienu sɛ wɔnkɔ adwuma.
Kɔɔto no nso buaa sɛ ntawantawa a ɛda mmɔfra adɔkotafoɔ ne aban no ntam no, wɔama wɔn nnawɔtwe mmienu sɛ wɔmpɛ obi mma no siesie asɛm no.
Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors’ associationkrakye panin abadakyire dadaa, Doctor Masimba Ndoro se ɛmfa ho ne deɛ kɔɔto no de ato dwa no, adɔkotafoɔ no nni ho kwan sɛ wɔnkɔ adwuma.
Studio 7 bisaa no sɛ, sɛ wɔanni deɛ kɔɔto aka no sɛ a, wɔnsuro sɛ wɔbɛhwere wɔn adwuma, Dr. Ndoro de too dwa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ wɔn a wɔafa wɔn adwuma no yɛ deɛ ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ biara ma wɔnkɔ adwuma.
Lɔya ma Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors’ Assoɔiation, Doug ɔoltart kyerɛ sɛ ɔnni kɔɔto no nyɛ adwene nso ɔbɛhwɛ deɛ nti a wɔreka saa.
ɔolhart san nso kaa sɛ, sɛ adɔkotafoɔ no pɛ a, ɔwɔ akwannya sɛ ɔkɔ dwanetoa wɔ kɔɔto peemu wɔ atemmuo no ho.

Adɔkotafoɔ no de wɔn mfidie guu hɔ ɛbɔ da a ɛtɔ so mmiɛna a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔnni adwuma biara yɛ.
Adɔkotafoɔ mpaninfoɔ a wɔkɔ adwuma no nso hyɛ dan mu Yawoada a ɛtwaam no a wɔmpue a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn akatua ne ayaresabea tebea a ɛwɔ mu no nyɛ.
US aban no de ato dwa sɛ ɔyɔlone idai asɛe Maniɔaland mpɔtam no na atowerɛkyɛm yi bɛkɔ so ateetee nnipa a wɔwɔ hɔ no.
ɔne Studio 7 retwetwe nkɔmmɔ US ɔman ananmusini asoeɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no, ɛason Taylor a ɔyɛ USAID kwankyerɛ panin a ɔhwɛ atowerɛkyɛm mmoa so kaa sɛ, mmerɛ wɔne ne akuo ahodoɔ redi ntikaho sɛ wɔbɛyɛ akwan na wɔasisi adan a asɛe no, wɔde wɔn ani rekɔ nnuane nnipa bɛdi so sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ nnipa nhwere wɔn nkwa.
Taylor de too dwa sɛ atowerɛkyɛn a asi wɔ Maniɔaland mpɔtam no ano yɛ den pa ara a Zimbabwe aban no nko ara ntumi nsɔ ano.
Taylor a ɔkɔɔ Maniɔaland mpɔtam de nnuane kɔmaa wɔn no kyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛɛ no nwanwa mmerɛ a ɔhunuu sɛdeɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ mantam no redi abooboo.
ɔkaa se mmɔfra a ɔhunuu wɔn no wɔ awerɛhoɔ mu. ɔde too dwa sɛ ɛho hia sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ Maniɔaland no bɛnya nnoɔma bi te sɛ nnuane ne baabi a wɔbɛda. Afei nso ɛwɔ sɛ wɔboa wɔn ma wɔn akoma tɔ wɔn yam.
Taylor de too dwa sɛ, wɔduruu ɔhimanimani ne ɔhipinge no, wɔanhunu wɔn a wɔse ɛsiane wɔn amanyɔkuo a wɔdɔm nti wɔnnya mmoa mfiri aban no hɔ no.
USAID sɛ Zimbabwe aban no bisa nko ara deɛ a, wɔn nso de animdefoɔ bɛkɔ Zimbabwe sɛ wɔnkɔkyerɛ Zimbabwefoɔ sɛdeɛ wɔbɛhunu berɛ ne beaeɛ a ahum no bɛba ne kwan a wɔbɛfa so abɔ nnipa ne agyapadeɛ ho ban.
Firi mmerɛ a ɔyɔlone Idai no siiɛ no, United States ama Zimbabwe $2.6M.
Zimbabwe aban, United Nations ne NGOs ahodoɔ ahyɛ dwumadie bi asɛ sɛ wɔrepɛ $60M de ahwɛ wɔn a ɔyɔlone Idai ama wɔn ho aka no.
Wɔsusu sɛ nnipa 300,000 na wɔhia mmoa wɔ Maniɔaland mpɔtam mu na wɔn mu 129,00 yɛ nkwadaa.
Mansini nkron aa ɔyɔlone Idai sɛeɛ no, sukuu ɔha ne du-mmiɛnsa na ɛsɛe a ama asukuufoɔ 90,000 nnya baabi nna.
Aban no se nnipa 300 na wɔakan wɔn aka ho, ɛnna nnipa 399 na wɔhweree wɔn nkwa.
Wɔrehwɛ anim sɛ nnipa dodoɔ no bɛkɔ anim.
Ayarefoɔ binom se wɔregye ayaresa wɔ amannɔne ɛfiri sɛ anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmɔfra ate atua na wɔsoro sɛ wɔbɛtumi awu wɔ ayaresabea a wɔnnya ayarehwɛ.
Nhwehwɛmu a Studio 7 yɛɛeɛ akyerɛ sɛ, ayarefoɔ binom retu kwan akɔ aman foforɔ te sɛ South Africa, Botswana ne Zambia akɔgye ayaresa ɛnam atuateɛ a anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmɔfra ateɛ no.
Ayarefoɔ no mu baako a yɛne no kasaeɛ wɔ Parirenyatwa, Awuraa Molline ɔhindove kaa sɛ, ɔtaa ba ayaresabea hɔ bɛpɛ ayarehwɛ nanso biribiara nkɔ so.
Awuraa ɔhindove kaa sɛ, ɔrekɔ South Africa akɔgye ayarehwɛ ɛfiri sɛ ɔsuro sɛ nsukum bɛku no wɔ berɛ a ne nan sisi nsuo mu.
N’abusuafoɔ no mu baako, Fiona Muɔhabaiwa kaa sɛ, ɔnni hwee yɛ sɛ ɔde no bɛkɔ Zambia ɔkyena akɔgye ayarehwɛ. Na ɔkyerɛ sɛ ne boɔ yɛ den.
Nhwehwɛmu a Studio 7 yɛɛeɛ akyerɛ sɛ, ɔman no ayaresabea a wɔatoto mu no reha adwene, na nnipa pii repere sɛ wɔbɛfiri ɔman ayaresabea no mu akɔ ankorɛankorɛ ayaresabea mu akɔgye ayarehwɛ.
Wilbert Kasanze kaa sɛ wayi ne yere afiri ɔhegutu General Hospital sɛ ɔrekɔhwɛ no wɔ ankorɛankorɛ ayaresabea a ɛwɔ ɔhitungwiza.
Kasanze se dabiara lɔɔre akɔbadie firi ɔhegutu kɔ ɔhitungwiza no ama ne bɔtɔm sika nyinaa asa.
Health Services Board de ato dwa sɛ mmɔfra anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔaku ahomegyeɛ mu no bɛsan aba adwuma ntɛm pa ara.
Bɔɔdo no nso aka akyerɛ atuatefoɔ no nyinaa sɛ wɔmfa wɔn nnwuma nto hɔ na sɛ wɔrepɛ adwuma deɛ a, wɔnsan mfa adwumapɛ ho krataa mmra.
Wei firi nsɛm a ɔmampanin abadiakyire ɔonstantino ɔhiwenga de ato dwa a ɔreka akyerɛ nɛɛse atuatefoɔ no nyinaa sɛ wɔmmfa wɔn nnwuma nto hɔ.
Nanso Zimbabwe Doctors for Human Rights se yi a aban no ayi anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmɔfra so no adi nni mmara so ɛsiane sɛ anɛɛsefoɔ no nni ayidie abodin nkrataa.
Bɔɔlobɔni Lionel Messi a ɔbɔ bɔɔlo ma Argentina ne bɔɔlobɔkuo a ɛwɔ Spain a wɔfrɛ Barcelona sɛ ɔmmɔ bɔɔlo mma Argentina man no bio berɛ a wantumi annye kuruwa baako mpo.
Messi de saa asɛm yi too dwa berɛ ɔopa AmErica agokansie a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ United States a Argentina dii nkukuo wɔ bɔɔlobɔ a ɛtwa toɔ wɔ akansie no mu aberɛ ɔhile hyɛɛ wɔn no gyee kuruwa no. Wei ne deɛ ɛtɔ so mmienu a ɔhile ahyɛ Argentina agye kuruwa no.
ɔhile hyɛɛ Argentina Kwasiada aberɛ a Francisɔo Silva bɔɔ bɔɔlo no too baabi Argentina gookipa Sergio Romero antumi anyɛ ho hwee.
Aman mmienu yi ko teeɛ aberɛ a obiara anto antena wɔ nnipadɔm 82,000 a na wɔwɔ East Rutherford a ɛwɔ New York ɛersey anim.
Aman a wɔbɔ ɔopa AmErica no nyinaa wɔ North ne South AmErica.
Mfeɛ mmiɛnsa a ɛtwaa mu no, Argentina dii nkukuo wɔ ɔhile nsa nano berɛ a wɔko tee a obiara nhyɛ bi. Messi antumi anhyɛ ne panaati no. Argentina dii nkukuo 4-2 wɔ panaatis no mu.
Afei Messi de too Tyɔ Sports nsɛntwerɛni anim sɛ ɔmmɔ bɔɔlo mma Argentina bio ɛsiane sɛ wantumi annye kuruwa no ɛmfa ho sɛ na ɛyɛ n’anisoadehunu.
Messi adi mfeɛ aduonu nkron.
ɔde Barcelona agye Champions League kuruwa no nnan. Nso, ɔntumi mfaa Argentina nnyee ɔopa AmErica anaa World ɔup.

Bere a Studio 7 duruu Mpilo ayaresabea hɔ no, na ayarefoɔ bi a wɔn yareɛ no ano yɛ akɛseɛ te sɛ apemfoɔ a wɔn mmɔtɔfowa ho atɔ kyɛm no, na wɔagya wɔn kwan ma wɔkɔ fie.

Owura Mapfumo kaa sɛ, ɛho hia sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ bɛda no adi sɛ wɔn ani nnye deɛ ɛrekɔ so wɔ wɔn man no, na sɛ nnoɔma nkɔ yie a, ɛyɛ ɔmam mma no asɛdeɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ.
Owura Mapfumo se ɔremmɔ ahomansia berɛ a ɔyɛkyerɛ no rekɔ so na ɔne Zimbabwefoɔ no bɛka abom ayɛ akyerɛ wiase nyinaa aban nkanka ɔmampanin Mugabe sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ nnoɔma sesa wɔ ɔman no mu.
Mapfumo ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ, “Meyɛ dwontoni nanso ɛwɔ New York mɛka afoforɔ ho ayɛ ama yɛyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ atia kɛtɛasehyɛ ne nhyɛsoɔ a Mugabe aban no de Zimbabwefoɔ refam no.
