Obert Masaure a ɔyɛ ARTUZ kannifoɔ kyerɛɛ mu kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ, ɛnyɛ adwumakuo no dɛ sɛ wɔbɛhunu asukuufoɔ a wɔnnya sika ntoa wɔn nnwomasua so, nkanka ne akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔdi hia no.
Masaraure kaa sɛ, esiane sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ no akatua ɛnso wɔn ne wɔn abusuafoɔ no nti, wɔretwerɛ nkrataa agyae adwuma no akɔhwehwɛ adwuma foforɔ.
Yɛntumi ne ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nwomasua so, ɔbenfoɔ Paul Mavhima nnii nkɔmmɔ ntie n’ano asɛm.
Sɛdeɛ wiase nyinaa ayi Ahinime bosome asi hɔ sɛ wɔde bɛbɔ dawuru afa kokoram yadeɛ a ɛtɔ mmaa nofo mu no, ɔanɔer associationof Zimbabwe kyerɛ sɛ wɔdwene ho wɔn sɛ nnipa bi nnim hwee fa yareɛ no ho wɔ ɔman no mu.
Kuo yi amannebɔ kyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔka wɔanya kokoram yadeɛ no di nkan kɔhunu wɔn a wɔhwɛ adwene mu yadeɛ no ansa na wɔakɔ wɔn a wɔatu wɔn ho asi hɔ sɛ wɔbɛboa ahwɛ wɔn a wɔanya kokoram yadeɛ no hɔ. Sɛ ɛkɔba no saa nso a, ɛma yadeɛ no ko yɛ den pa ara.
Priscilla Mangwiro a ɔyɛ ɔanɔer associationof Zimbabwe kɔnsɔɔltant de ato dwa sɛ ɛtwa sɛ wɔn a wɔanya saa yadeɛ kɔ adɔkotafoɔ a wɔaben wɔ kokoram yadeɛ ho kɔgye ayarehwɛ.
Awuraa Mangwiro kyerɛ sɛ ɛho hia sɛ berɛ-ano-berɛ-ano nnipa bɛkɔ ayaresabea sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ wɔn nnipadua mu nhwɛ sɛ wɔanya kokoram yadeɛ no bi ahinta a, nkanka ne nofoɔ mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwiro kyerɛ sɛ nofoɔ mu kokoram yɛ yareɛ a ɛtɔ so mmienu a ɛreku mmaa wɔ Zimbabwe.
Awuraaa Mangwiro kaa sɛ, ɛfiri Ahinime da a ɛdi kan no a wɔhyɛɛ aseɛ bɔɔ nofoɔ kokoram mu dawuro no, n’adwumakuo ne de mmaa a wɔboro aduonum na afa afidie ahwɛ sɛ wɔwɔ yadeɛ no bi anaasɛ wɔnni yadeɛ no bi. Na nɔmma no bɛkɔ soro kɔsi bosome no awieeɛ.
Berɛ ɔtee ɔanɔer associationof Zimbabwe dwumadie no ho asɛm no, ɔbaa a wɔfrɛ no Gertrude Magwaniza de too dwa sɛ ɔde ne babaa kɔɔ hɔ na wɔhunuu kokoram wɔ ne nofo mu.
Awuraa Mangwira kyerɛ sɛ nnoɔma bebree na ɛtumi ma mmaa nya nofoɔ mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwira de too dwa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ wɔma wɔn ani kɔ nsesaeɛ a ɛba mmaa nofo mu. Wɔyɛ saa a wɔbɛhunu sɛ wɔwɔ nofom kokoram anaa wɔnni bi.
Awuraa Mangwiro kaa sɛ mmaa dodoɔ no ara dwene sɛ sɛ wɔnya kokoram a na ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔrebɛwu, nanso nnoɔma bebree na wɔbɛtu ayɛ ama mmaa atena wiase akye.
Awuraa Mangwiro kyerɛ sɛ adeɛ baako a ɛma kokoram ne nnuane a anwa ne asikyire wɔ mu bebree.
Awuraa Mangwiro atu mmaa fo sɛ wɔmfa saa akwannya yi so nkɔhwɛ wɔ wɔwɔ kokoram anaa wɔnni bi, na wɔmma wɔn nimdeɛ mfa yadeɛ no ho.
Nnipa boro mpem num na afe biara wɔnya yadeɛ yi bi na yareɛ a ɛyɛ hu de nnipa dodoɔ no ara bɛkɔ adɔkorafoɔ hɔ.
Aban pɛtro dwumakuo, Petrotrade se sɛ aban no kɔso kyerɛ sɛdeɛ wɔntɔ anaa wɔtɔ fango a, ɛnneɛ fango a ɛho akɔ atwee no nkɔ da.
ɔde n’anodisɛm fa mmarahyɛbadwafie fango boɔ nhyehyɛeɛ reto dwa no, Petrotrade krakye panin dadaa Godfrey Nɔube de too dwa sɛ sɛ wɔma adwumakuo akwannya ma wɔtɔ anaa wɔtɔn fango sɛdeɛ wɔn ara pɛ a, wei bɛyɛ yie.
Owura Nɔube gye too mu sɛ, wei bɛma boɔ akɔ soro nanso ɛno ara ne kwan a ɔman no bɛtumi asi ɔhaw no ano.
Mr Nɔube de too dwa wɔretwɛn aban no fango ma fango boɔ no kɔ fam wɔ ɔman no mu, na daakye no wɔbɛnya fango bebree.
Mr Nɔube kyerɛ sɛ fango a aban no tɔ a ɛhɔ akɔ atwee no ho nhwɛsoɔ a ɔde too dwa ne sɛ, bosome nsia a na ɛdi afe a ɛtwaam no anim no, wɔtɔnn fango lita ɔpepem aduonum, nanso saa mmerɛ koraa no mu afe yi mu, wɔatɔn lita ɔpepem aduasa nsia pɛ.
Berɛ wɔbisaa no kwan a ɔbɛfa so asiesie fango a ɛho akɔ atwee no, ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ ma wɔn a wɔdum gya, Gloria Magombo kaa sɛ ɔhaw no nkɔ aberɛ wɔn a wɔde wɔn dwetire abɛhyɛ ɔman no mu so.
ɔsan nso kyerɛ sɛ wɔresɔ ɔhaw no ano a, ɛhia ɔman no nyinaa na nyɛ n’asoeɛ no nko ara.
Awuraa Magombo rekyerɛ n’adwene fa sɛ wɔde semaate kaade bɛtɔ fango sɛdeɛ amrado a ɔda CentralBank, John Mangudya de too dwa sɛ kaade no bɛkyerɛ fango dodoɔ a wo lɔɔre no anom no, ɔde too dwa sɛ nhyehyɛeɛ amma mu ɛsiane COVID-19 yareɛ no.
Awuraa Magombo de too dwa sɛ ɔntumi nkyerɛ berɛ nhyehyɛeɛ no bɛyɛ yie mfa ho sɛ Owura Mangudya ka kyerɛɛ kɔmitee bosome a ɛtwaa mu no sɛ ɔwɔ anidasoɔ sɛ Kɔtɔnima bosome no nkɔ awieeɛ wɔbɛtumi de kaade no adi dwuma sɛdeɛ wɔaka no.
Wei maa mmarahyɛbadwa kɔmitee bo afu na wɔde ato dwa sɛ wɔn a wɔdum gya no nyɛ wɔn adwuma yie. Sɛdeɛ Awuraa Magombo nso kaa sɛ wɔate afiri kɔmitee no kuo mma hɔ nnɛ sɛ, beaeɛ a wɔtɔ pɛtrol wɔn ɔman no mu bebree no, wɔde AmErica dɔla no na ɛtɔ.
Kɔmitee no de too dwa sɛ wɔredwene ho sɛ fango a akɔ atwee no renya nnoɔma so nsunsuansoɔ wɔ ɔman no mu.
Memeneda yi, Zimbabuefoɔ dii wɔn nnaduasa afahyɛ a wɔde dee wɔn ho firii aborɔfo nsɛm ni nkoasom a abibifoɔ kɔɔ mu no
Saa Abibifoɔ fahoɔdii yi de anidasoɔ baa sɛ da bi wɔbɛnya Aborɔfo fahodii no bi
Nanso no mfeɛ aduanan akyiri a ɔman no nyaa fahodie no, nneɛma asɛe sene sɛ deɛ ɔsusui no mpo, wɔnni nnwuma mpo a wɔde reboa wɔn abusua
Wɔse adwadie nsɛm mpo nnyɛ a, wɔn hu deɛ wɔreyɛ mpo anaa deɛ daakye no wɔ ma wɔn
Apɔmuden nsɛm koraa nyɛ sene sɛdeɛ anka ɔman no rehwehwɛ afiri wɔn hɔ no
Kakra wɔn a wɔreyɛ adwuma no nso daa no wɔrekɔ atwe wɔn akwantenpɔn mu aperɛ deɛ eyɛ
ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnanagagwa a wɔde no aba 2017, yi ɛnam ɔmanpanin Robert Mugabe a asraafoɔ no tuu no no ama ɔmanfoɔ anidaasoɔ
Nanso wɔn mu binom nhyɛ da nne wɔn ho a deɛ wɔgu reka ara ne sɛ nneɛma gye a na ɛregye nsam
Nti biribiara nni hɔ a ZanuPF amanyɔkuo no ayɛ ama ɔman no mfeɛ aduanan yi
Zanu amamnyɔkuo no North Amɛrɛka titenani no sɛ Regis ɔharumbira sɛ wɔn amanyɔkuo no ayɛ pii a wɔama Abibifoɔ nsaase sɛ woyɛ wɔn amanyɔkuo ba anaasɛ wɔnnyɛ amamnyɔkuo ba
Mr. Churumbira kaa sɛ, n’amanyɔkuo no awie nhwehwɛmu a afa wɔn a wɔanya nsaase a yɛde yɛ afuo ɛnna wɔn wɔn nso a wɔnnyaa bi no ɛsɛ sɛ wɔnya bi a wɔte amanɔne no
Nanso Timothy Muringai, ɔtwerɛfoɔ abadiakyire a ɔwɔ MDC-T north Amɛrika amanyɔkuo no mu no antumi anni ne bɔhyɛ so.
Wɔnse nneɛma asɛe mfeɛ pii wɔ adwadie mu, apomuden mu, adwumaguo mu ama nnipa pii no ara tete fie
Attorney Ntabazinduna Nhlanhlayamangwe Ndiweni anaa Lord Felix Ndiweni ne de ato High kɔɔto anim sɛ wɔn sesa n’atennie no mfa no nto mu mfeɛ 18
Ishe ne nnipa 23 bi, wɔkyee wɔn wɔrebu afasuo a ɛwɔ Feti Mbele a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔfiri Ntabazinduna mansin no mu
Eyi na ɛde monaatoɔ nsusui no ba Mbele yere a wɔato ne monaa n. Nonkangelo Mpengesi
Lord Ndiweni mmaranimni, Dumisani Dube, ka kyerɛɛ studio 7 sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ no mmu ahemfo a wɔwɔ n’abatoɔ mpɛsoasoɔ
ɔnnwomtoni a wagye din Thomas Mukanya Mapfumo se, ɔrehwɛ kwan de dwom bi aba saa bosome yi mu berɛ wɔn mfidie no asɛe yi
Saa adwuma yi wɔ Eugene, Oregon a ɛwɔ Amerika man no mu a wɔfrɛ no Traɔkdown Studios. Dr. Mapfumo ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 no sɛ nnwom 15 a wayɛ no 7 pɛ na aka
Haekɔɔto ahyɛ sɛ Heal Zimbabue manpanyin, Rashid Mahiya, anya baeli a yɛbɛdi n’asɛm wɔ fie
Mahiya, a ɔda afiase no wɔrehwɛ anim sɛ wɔbɛyi no fiada wei, nanso apolisifoɔ sɛ wɔntumi anwie wɔn nkrataa ho adwuma no
Mahiya mmaranimni a ɔka Zimbabwe Lawyers for Human Rights, Tonderayi Bhatasara ho ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ kɔɔto no gyee Mahiya akwantuo nkrataa kaa sika $ 1,000 no a wɔgyee no ho
"Yɛagye kɔɔto no asɛnnie no ato mu, ɛfiri sɛ deɛ na yɛrehwɛ anim ne sɛ kɔɔto no bɛgyae no. Bhatasara ka kyerɛɛ VOA’s Studio 7
Mahiya ka wɔn a wɔkyee wɔn no ho sɛ wɔretu anammɔn de atu aban no aguo no
Berɛ a na ɔne ɔtwerɛfoɔ ma Zimbabwe MedicalAssoɔiation, Saɔrifiɔe ɔhirisa, rekasa no ɔkaa sɛ wanya krataa afiri dɔkota paninho a ɛrehyɛ no sɛ ɔmfa n’adwuma nto hɔ
ɔhirisa, a ɔyɛ ɔyaresafoɔ so paninno, kaa sɛ nnwuma adɔɔso ama adokotafoɔ mpaninɛnam sɛ, adɔkotafoɔ nketewa no kɔ straike no nti
ɔhrirsa kaa sɛ, sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ na adwuma no akɔ yie nti no, wɔhia dokotafoɔ mmabunu no sɛ wɔbɛba abɛyɛ adwuma
Mr ɔhirisa rekasa no ɔkaa sɛ nnipa a wɔrebɛgye ayarehwɛ abu so wɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ no mu ɛnam dokotafoɔ bɛyɛ 533 a wɔmma adwuma no nti
ɔtwerɛfo ma Zimbabwe Hospital Doctors Assoɔiation, Mthabisi Anele Bhebhe nso kaa sɛ, n’ani nnye asɛm a ɔmanpanin dada ɔonstantino ɔhiwenga kaa sɛ adɔkota nkumaa no gu so wɔ sukuu mu no
ɔhewenga a ɔkaa saa asɛm no no wɔfaa no sɛ ɔne nkɔmmɔtwetwe a ɔne aban no redie no anim mfa adɔkotafoɔ a wɔte fie no ho ne anɛɛsefoɔ a wɔn so te fie no ho
Wɔn anammɔntuo no pii no ara na wɔakasa atia, berɛ a wɔde asraafoɔ na ɛredi asɛm no
Adɔkotafoɔ nketewa no se, ɛsɛ sɛ aban no ma wɔn akadeɛ ne ntaadeɛ a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma berɛ a wɔreyɛ adwuma no na wɔsan nto wɔn akatua mu
Nanso aban no nso see wɔnni sika nti ɔntumi nyɛ deɛ wɔreka no
Wɔatumi ante deɛ ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ apomuden so, Mr Obadia Moyo reka no a ɔkɔɔ pɛdiatiriki wɔ nhyimu no bi no
Labor kɔɔto no abu aban no agyinatuo no agu ɛnam sɛ aban no amfa nkrataa biara ankɔ
Doug ɔoltart, mmaranimni a ɔgyina Zimbabwe Hospital Doctor's associationananmu wɔ Labor kɔɔto kyerɛ sɛ nkrataa papa biara mfii Health Services Board, HSB no hɔ mmae nti wɔntumi ntena asɛm no so
Kɔɔto no hyɛɛ HSB’s mmaranimfoɔ sɛ wɔnyɛ nkrataa no a ayera no ho adwuma wukuada
Nanso adɔkotafoɔ no se wɔrekɔ asɛnnibea no nyɛ adeɛ a ɛbɛma wɔasan aba adwuma
Ekuo yi manpaninabediakyire dada, Masiba Ndoro kaa sɛ n’adwuma no ɔhia sɛ wɔbɛtu ka da biara
Adɔkotafoɔ nketewa no kɔɔ straeke ɛbɔ 3 a wɔreka sɛ wɔnni akodeɛ a wɔde yɛ adwuma
Adɔkotafoɔ mpaninfoɔ a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Senior Hospital Doctors' association nso kɔɔ straeke Yawoada yi a wɔn nso sɛ wɔn akatua nyɛ na wɔnni apomuden akyiri asibaa biara
Adɔkotafoɔ mpanyinfoɔ a wɔkyerɛɛ krataa faa de wɔrekɔ mu no sɛ, ɛyɛ nkwasɛm sɛ dɔkotafoɔ bɛkɔ adwuma berɛ a wɔnni akadeɛ a wɔde reyɛ adwuma
Adɔkotafoɔ no nso bɔɔ aban no akyi sɛ, wɔato akatua mu 60%, na wɔnte aseɛ
Berɛ koro no ara mu no, wɔayi, adɔkotafoɔ mmienu afiri hɔ a University of Zimbabwe se wɔaka straeki no hɔ, na wɔasan ama ntumi binom agyae adwuma.
Wɔatwe Dr. Bothwell Mbuvayesango asɛn ɔno nso na wɔabene wɔ pɛdiatiric nhwehwɛmu emu
Dr. Mbuvayesanguo nyaa din maa ne ho efiri aberɛ a wɔyɛɛ sɛɛgeri maa ntaafoɔ a na wɔn ti bɔ mu nowɔ 2014 mu no a Dr. Wake nso abɛn wɔ akoma nhwehwmu mu.
Zimbabwe associationof Doctors for Human Rights akasa atia Dr. Mbuvayesangano ntwesan no pa ara
Yɛntumi ntee mfiri University of Zimbabwe anaa aban no nka ɛfa ayarehwɛ ho
Nanso nsɛnkae a ɛfiri apomuden soafoɔ, Health Minister Obadiah Moyo kyerɛ sɛ dɔkotafoɔ nsan nkɔ adwuma
Moyo kaa sɛ, aban no retwe deɛ ɛbɛfiri asɛnnie no mu aba no, ɛno na ɛbɛkyerɛ deɛ aban no nyɛ
Adɔkotafoɔ tee atua ɛbɔ 3 no ɛnam sɛ wɔse wɔnni sika a wɔde kɔ adwuma
Aban no ne ahɔhoɔ adwuma asan nteasɛ krataa sɛ wɔde koal bɛkɔ India ne ɛapan
Berɛ a wɔrekasa fa nteasɛ apam a wɔne Viɔtoria ɔonsulting ayɛ no ɔsoafoɔ, Winston ɔhitando,  aban no anisoɔdehunu ne sɛ ɔman no bɛdi koah dwa
ɔhitando kaa sɛ Zimbabwe rehwe sɛ ɔde koal tɔnso ɔpepempem 25 na ɛbɛkɔ nanso no wɔrehwɛ sɛ ɔpepem 3 bɛkɔ aberɛ biara
ɔsan kaa sɛ India na wɔde koal kɔ hɔ pa ara afe biara
Saa nhyimu no ara ase no, ɔmanpanin Emerson Mnanagwa kaa sɛ Zimbabwefoɔ ntumi nnya ayɔnkofa a ɛda ɔman no mmienu ntam no ho mfasoɔ mapa
Studio 7 ntumi nhuu saa adwuma kuo a ɔne Viɔtoria ɔonsulting , na hefo koraa na wɔhwɛ adwuma no so

ɛkɔnɔmist, Nyasha Muɔhiɔhwa nso kaa asɛm koro no ara
Mr. Muɔhiɔhwa nso kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde yɔnkofa a ɛda ɔne aman foforo ntam di dwuama
Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ minerase so no ntentanfiri no so no, kyerɛ sɛ koah papa, ne mmeaeɛ 29 a wɔwɔ
Adwuma kuo abien a ɛyɛ Hwange ɔolliery ne Mountain Resourɔes, na wɔtu koah pa ara
Nnipa baasa a wɔka MDC-T amanyɔkuo a Nelson ɔhamisa di anim no, wɔkye wɔn wɔ Harare Fiada, na wɔgyae wɔn wɔ $ 1,000 baeli ho
ɔtemmuafoɔ ɔhanɔellor Bianɔa Makwande rekasa no wɔkyerɛ sɛ saa ɔhamisa abadiakyirefoɔ mmienu yi Tendai Biti ne Ms. Lynett Karenyi Kore, wɔn twerɛfoɔ Ms. Gladys Hlatywayo, twerɛfoɔ abediakyire Mr Lovemore ɔhinoputsa, ne wɔn kɔmiteeni ne amanyɔkuo no twerɛfoɔ abadiakyire no David ɔhimhini ne Ms Vongai Tome.
Wɔhyɛ saa mmarima yi sɛ obiara ntua $1,000 ɛfa MDɔ’s Morgan Tsvangirai fie no ho
Ms Makwande kaa sɛ, wɔn a wɔkyee wɔn no bɛkɔ kɔɔto bio kitawonsa 24, ɛnam adrɛɛse a wɔnyaa wɔ apolisifoɔ hɔ no akɔsi sɛ wɔbɛtie wɔn asɛm.
Berɛ a wɔn Studio 7 rekasa no fa atemmuo no ho no, alɔyafoɔ no baako, Aleɔ Muɔhdehama, kaa sɛ kɔɔto no ahyɛ nnipa no sɛ wɔnni hɔ sɛ ɔbɛ nsɛe wɔn dwuma die ne wɔn nhwehwɛmu.
Mr. MuChadehama nso kaa sɛ, ɛwom sɛ nnipa baasa na wɔkyee wɔnfaa sɛ wɔakɔ atia kriminaa lɔɔ no, wɔn a wɔkyee wɔn no kɔɔ kɔɔto anɔpa yi, wɔsan de wɔn kɔɔ apolisifoɔ hɔ sɛ wɔabu ɔovid 19 mmara so

Amnyɔkuo no panyin, Nelson ɔhamisa, aka sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so ako ama nsesa aba ɔman no mu ɛmfa ho ne nnipa binom a wɔkye wɔn

Saa ɔfisa yi, Shungudzemoyo Kaɔhe, wɔbɛdi n’asɛm wɔ fie
Deɛ ɔda Prophetiɔ Healing and Deliveranɔe (PHDɔ Ministries, Walter Magaya nso akasa afa ne kyeɛ wɔ Zimbabwe no ho, na ɔreka sɛ ɔde Aguma aduru a ɛboa tu HIV/AIDS, kansa ne ade aba

Mmom no, nsɛm a wɔreka atia Magaya wɔ Zimbabwe no, Aretha Midiɔal companyno, wɔahu sɛ, sɛɛ wɔntwerɛɛ wɔn din wɔ Mediɔines ɔontrol Authority of Zimbabwe, na ɛnam saa nti no Health Professions Authority mmaa wɔn kwan sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ Aguma aduru no mu sɛ ɛyɛ adwuma anaa ɛnyɛ adwuma
Dɔkota a ɔwɔ ayarebea bi wɔ Francistown, Sengaphi Khuzwayo, buu Magaya animtia ɛnam sɛ na wɔrepɛ sika
Mr. Magaya adi kan de wantwitwe aba ɔman no mu ɛfiri berɛ a ɛbɛtɔɔ dwa sɛ wato ɔbaa bi mmonnaa no, nanso kɔɔto no bɔɔ asɛm no gui
Pɛdiatiris a wɔnni ayaresabe hɔ no, ama ampemfoɔ rekɔ ahohiahia mu wɔ ayaresabea hɔ te sɛ deɛ ɛwɔ ɔhinhiyi General Hospital no.
Ms. Lisa Sibanda yɛ ɔbaa a wabrɛ afiri postpartum depression ho
Ms. Sibanda kaa sɛ ne baa a na ɔnyini nwie no, wuu wɔ ne yafunu mu berɛ a na wɔrewo Benada no nanso na dɔkota biara nni hɔ a wɔbɛboa no a ɛnam so maa nɛɛseni a ɔbɛboaa no kum ne ba no

Ms. Sibanda kaa sɛ wɔgu so rekɔ nsu twa mu haw mu, ɛnam saa nti wɔntumi nkɔ agyanan a ɛwɔ ayaresabea no so
Erasmus Zindoga a ɔde ne yere baa Kariba no kaa sɛ ɔnnyaa mmoa biara mfirii dɔkota biara hɔ nanso deɛ wahu no no nyɛɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ne yere no

Mashonaland West yaresafoɔ panyin, Tapiwa Dhliwayo kaa sɛ adɔkotafoɔ nkɔ adwuma wɔ mpɔtamu hɔ baabiara
Mmom no ɔsan kaa sɛ, ɛnyɛ nɛɛsefoɔ nko ara na ɛsɛ sɛ, wɔhwɛ mmaa a wɔn nyinsɛn asɛe te sɛ deɛ ɛsii wɔ ɔhinhoyi ayaresabea no.
ɔhinhoyi CityCouncil kasamafoɔ, Tiɔhao Mlauzi de nsɛnkae bi too dwa nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaa mu no, deɛ ɔkae ne sɛ, ɔhinhoyi nnipa a wɔwɔ hɔ no dodow yɛ 120,000 no rekɔ nsuo ahohiahia mu ɛnam pumps mmiɛnsa a asɛe no
Kansa associationof Zimbabwe hyɛ ɔmanfoɔ sɛ ɔmma wɔn ho kwan na wɔnyɛ wɔn nnofoɔ ho nhwehwɛmu ntam ɛnam sɛ yareɛ no ho yɛhu
Nnipa boro 5,000 na afe biara wɔhu kansa yareɛ nkorabata no bi wɔ wɔn ho wɔ Zimbabwe na wɔn mu dodow no ara hu pɛdiatriste fa saa yareɛ yi ho
Kuo no manpaninno, ɛunior Mavhu, se wɔwɔ adwene bi sɛ wɔpɛ wɔhwehwɛ mmaa ne mmarima nnofo mu hwɛ sɛdeɛ wɔbɛtumi aboa wɔn
Wɔaka sɛ kansa reku nnipa pii no ara wɔ ɔman yi mu, ne titiriw ne mmaa ɛwom sɛ mmarima na wɔwɔ no pa ara
Kansa asoeɛ no baako rehyɛ mmaa ne mmarima nyinaa sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ kansa dwumadie no mu aberɛ a wɔrehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛsi birɛst kansa bosome no mu wɔ Ahinime mu, na wɔadi wiase nyinaa birɛst kansa bosome no
Wiase nyinaa rehwɛ kwan sɛ, wɔbɛsi bosome yi mu na wɔahwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛkae mnnipa wɔ birɛst kansa ho ne ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so abɔ wɔn ho ban afiri ho
Ms. Mavhu susu sɛ yɛnhwɛ obiara daa nyinaa sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛtumi asi yareɛ yi ano na ante atɛse.
Zimbabwefoɔ di wɔn afe mmienu afahyɛ Memeneda yi fa atutotɔɔ a ekuu nnipa baasa wɔ Harare berɛ nnipa binom baa mmɔtene so bɛkyerɛɛ gye a wɔnnye 2018 abatoɔ no nto mu
Saa akum yi kɔɔ wiase afaanan nyinaa ɛnam nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a na wɔfiri aman hodoɔ so no nyinaa na wɔrehwɛ ɛtoɔ a na edi ka a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Zanu Pfni, Emmerson Mnangagwe ntam ɛnam deɛ Robert Mugabe a wanya ne baabi no yɛe nti.
Na Mnangagwe ne Nelson ɔhamisa a ɔyɛ MDɔ kannini na ɛrepere akonnwa no.
Berɛ a atutotoɔ no wie no, aban no tee abadwakuo ma wɔhwehwɛɛ mu. Na kuo yi nnaanoni ne South Africafoɔ manpanindada Kgalema Motlanthe.
Abadwakuo yi de nsɛnkae yi bi baa a na ɛkyerɛ sɛ asraafoɔ no ne apolifoɔ no kumm nnipa nsi na saa nnipa yi no ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtwe wɔn aso. ɛhyɛɛ sɛ aban no ntua wɔn a wɔkuu wɔn no abusua ka
Mr. Motlanthe abadwakuo yi nso san kaa sɛ, aban no mfa wɔn a wɔkuu wɔn no mma nkɔ sukuu, na ɛmma apolisifoɔ ne asraafoɔ mfa mmara no nhyɛ wɔn nsa
Human rightfoɔ kyerɛ sɛ aban no mfaa ose nyɛɛ ɔyɔ ɛfa de Motlanthe abadwakuo no kae no ho
Nanso amaneɛ soafoɔ, Moniɔa Mutsvangwa se aban no nim deɛ abadwakuo no aka nyinaa na wɔregu reyɛ nhyehyɛe de afa ho

Madhuku kaa sɛ wɔde kɔkɔbɔ akɔ ama aban no sɛ ɔnhwɛ na ɔmpɛ biribi mma wɔn ɛfiri sɛ ɔman no asraafoɔ na ɛkum wɔn

ɛkyerɛ sɛ simasin aduanan akyiri no wɔhuu ayeforo kunu no sɛ ɔrefi efie hɔ na ɔrepa awarefoɔ no akyɛw.
ɛhɔ no ara wɔhuu sɛ maame bi pue hɔ frɛɛ 911 a ɔrepɔɔto no
Maame no ka kyerɛɛ apolisifoɔ no sɛ ne kunu no wɔ fie hɔ a ɔrewura efie no mu.
Deɛ efie no yɛ ne dea no rekyerɛ no sɛ, wɔamfa hwee wɔ fie hɔ
Ebinom ayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ ɔde nsɛnkae yi regu ntentan fidie so
Atɔni ɛim Biɔkerton, kaa sɛ, kɔɔto no ahyɛ sɛ wɔmfa sini no mmra a wɔnyɛ hwee mfa ho
ɔhyɛɛ apolisifoɔ nso sɛ wɔmfa frɛ a wɔfrɛɛ 911 no nyinaa saa da no mmɛto dwa.
Berɛ a Biɔkerton ne Mr. William Denselow twetwee nkɔmmɔ no eNɔA de too dwa sɛ berɛ a ayeforo kunu no refiri fie no na ne bo mfui.
Biɔkerton kaa sɛ, ne nsɛm a ɛtwa toɔ a ɔkae a ne sɛ ɔpaakyɛw
Mfonini a ɛdii kan baa abɔntene no mu no, ayefokunu no bisaa apolisifoɔ no nnipa korɔ a wɔyɛ na wɔbɔɔ no tuo tuu no wɔ ayaresabea hɔ.
ɔde too dwa sɛ, na wɔnnim sɛ Myeni annu ne ho na apolisifoɔ no hɔ na bideo no wɔ, nanso wɔhyia nsɛntwerɛfoɔ no, wɔde too wɔn anim sɛ ɔtoo hyɛɛ wɔn so.
Biɔkerson kaa sɛ wɔbɛhwehwɛ nokorɛ no sɛdeɛ wɔbɛhunu deɛ ɛresi.
Wɔrekyerɛ sɛ ntawantawa bi asi wɔ IFP mu wɔ Melmoth.
Wɔabu IFP kanselɛsfoɔ kwaadu sɛ wɔrebo abammɔfoɔ a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɔɔ nnipa mmiɛnsa tuo wɔ amanyɔkuo no nhyiamu a ɛkɔɔ so Thubalethu, Mthonɛaneni (Melmothɔ Kwasiada awia no.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ abammufoɔ no sii nnipadɔm no ano sɛ wɔmma wɔnkɔ beaeɛ a wɔreyɛ nhyiamu no.
Amanyɔkuo no fa bi de soboɔ bɔɔ amanyɔkuo no mpaninfoɔ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔhyɛ wɔn so berɛ a wɔresrɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmma IFP kansela baako a wɔayi no adi bɛsan aba.
IFP mpaninfoɔ frɛɛ saa nhyiamu wɔ King ɔetshwayo borɔno so sɛdeɛ wɔbɛsiesie asɛm a ama mpɔtam no akyɛ no. Nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaam mu no, wante aseɛ sɛ wɔde kanselɛs a wɔayi wɔn adi no resan aba a mɛyɔ dadaa Bonginkosi Biyela ka ho.
Public kuo ba baako a ɔmpɛ sɛ ne din bɛto dwa a na ɔka ɔyɛkyerɛ no ho berɛ na wɔretoto wɔn atuo no, abɔ IFP mpaninfoɔ ne kanselɛs a na wɔwɔ hɔ soboɔ sɛ wɔn a wɔka kyerɛ abammufoɔ no sɛ wɔnto wɔn tuo sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ wɔntumi nyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no.
“Na yɛreyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ no wɔn abɔntene ɛfiri sɛ wɔamfa yɛn kwan amma yɛankɔ nhyiamu no ase ɛfiri sɛ nnipa a wɔwɔ hɔ no firi borɔno ahodoɔ.
Kuo ba de too dwa sɛ, ntawantawa no nyinaa hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ yɛkyee Public kuo ba a na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkɔ nhyiamu no ase. Wei maa abammɔfoɔ ne kanselɛs a wɔwɔ hɔ no akwannya maa wɔtoo tuo.”
IFP kannifoɔ a ɔwɔ Mthonɛaneni a na ɔmpɛ sɛ ne din bɛba abɔntene kaa sɛ, na Public kuo mma a wɔwɔ mpɔtam no mu akyɛ.
“Nnawɔtwe a ɛtwaam no, wɔyɛɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔmmɛkyerɛ deɛ nti a wɔayi wɔn kansela no afiri wɔɔdo.
Wɔahyehyɛ nhyiamudie ama kanselɛs ne IFP mantam mpaninfoɔ no nyinaa sɛ wɔmmɛma wɔ mmuayɛ.
Ntawantawa no hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a amanfoɔ no mu bi sii hɔɔlo no kwan no berɛ nhyiamudie no hyɛɛ, na wɔhyɛɛ aseɛ paa abammɔfoɔ no aboɔ. Wei na ɛmaa abammɔfoɔ no nso hyɛɛ aseɛ totoo tuo.
ɔde too dwa sɛ na etuo nso hyɛ amanfoɔ no bi ho.
Mɛyɔ a wɔayi no foforɔ Mbangiseni Biyela, n’abadiakyire Phumlani Ntombela ne kanselɛs a wɔwɔ Mthonɛaneni kuroakɛseɛ mu nyinaa na wɔbaa saa nhyiamu yi.
Wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛte mantam kannifoɔ no anodisɛm, nso wɔannya wɔn.
Kuroakɛseɛ no nyinaa kasamafoɔ, Thami Shangase de too dwa sɛ, ɛnyɛ munisipal no na ɔhyehyɛɛ nhyiamu no. ɔde kaa ho sɛ biribiara wɔ apolisifoɔ nsam.
IFP ɔman mu nyinaa kasamafoɔ, Mkhuleko Hlengwa kaa sɛ amanyɔkuo no de n’anodisɛm fa asɛm no ho bɛto dwa nnɛ.
Basabasaeɛ hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ wɔyii Bisela ne kanselɛs anan adi. Wei maa amanfoɔ no mu kyɛeɛ nkanka ne IFP kuo mma a wɔda munisipal no ano.

Mbete kyerɛ sɛ wɔmmu n’ani angu kɛtɛasehyɛ so.

Awuraa Mbete reyi nsɛm ano ɛfa kwaadu a wɔde abɔ no sɛ mmarahyɛbadwafoɔ no mu bi ho bɔn wɔ kɛtɛasehyɛm no, ɔde too dwa sɛ nnipa biara ne n’adwenkyerɛ, ɛnna nsɛm no bi nso yɛ atesɛm ɛfiri sɛ animdefoɔ nni adansidie biara.

Benada no Mr. ɔhiwenga hyɛɛ sɛ adɔkotafoɔ no nyinaa nkɔ adwuma

Wɔde ɔosafa ɔup no reyɛ ahoboa ama Afɔon no ɛwɔ sɛ Zimbabwe gye kuruwa a wɔgyee no deɛ ɛtɔ nsia afe a ɛtwaa mu no

Zimbabwe bɔɔlobɔfoɔ bi te sɛ Tendai Darikwa, Admiral Muskwe, ne Aleɔ Mudimu na pɛ wɔn nso ba ɔosafa ɔup akansie no mu
Afe yi Zimbabwe bɔɔlɔkuo no na kura team pa ara a wɔde rekɔ Afɔon no mu esiane bɔɔlobɔfoɔ bi te sɛ Knowledge Musona ne Marvelous Nakamba nti

Mapondera nso kyerɛ sɛ buronya yi ɔne n’abusuafoɔ ne ne nnamfonom bɛhyia wɔ ne fie a ɛwɔ Harare adi agorɔ. Mr. Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ ɛwɔ Ghanafoɔ ho hoahoa wɔn sɛ Global peace Index Report  de ato dwa sɛ sɛ ɛba asomdwoeɛ mu nsɛm a Ghana ne ɔman a wɔtɔ so mmienu wɔ Abibirem ha. ɔsane bɔɔ NPP ne NDC aba so sɛ wɔaboa ama ɔman asomdwoeɛ aba ɔman no mu
ɔtoaa so sɛ wei yɛ abasodeɛ a ahemfo, amanyɔkuo, abanbɔfoɔ, ɔmanpanin, mmarahyɛbadwan, kɔɔto ne media no aboa ama ɔman Ghana anya
ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ Regional ɔoordinating Council (Rɔɔɔ bɛboa ama saa asomdwoeɛ yi akɔ so atena hɔ afebɔɔ
ɔrekasa wɔ Electoral Justice dwumadie ase, Alhaɛi Suallah Abdallah Quandah a ɔyɛ twerɛtwerɛfoɔ panin ma Bono mantam peace Council de too dwa sɛ ɛnam Electoral Justice so nti na amanyɔsɛm atumi agyina wɔ ɔman no mu
ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ mu sɛ ɛwɔm sɛ Electoral Justice dwumadie nyɛ adefoforɔ bi na mmom sɛ ɔman sɛ ɔman bɛtu mpon wɔ abatoɔ ne amanyɔsɛm mu ɛnni kwan sɛ wɔtoto wɔn dwumadie ase
Alhaji Quandah kyerɛɛ hia a ɛho hia sɛ ɔman biara nya Electoral Justice a ɛbɛboa ama wɔn abatoɔ mu nsɛm akɔ tɔɔtee
Abuakwa South mmarahyɛbɛdwani Samuel Atta Akyea ahyɛ Ghanafoɔ bɔ sɛ sɛ Nana Addo aban mu ɔpɛpɔn da a ɛtɔ so nson wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne du nson mu a Ghanafoɔ haw nyinaa to bɛtwa
ɔkyerɛ sɛ Nana Addo aban no bɛma ɔman no sikasɛm ho atɔ wɔn ɛfiri sɛ wɔayɛ sikasɛm ho nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔde bɛgu akwan mu
Atta Akyea rekyɛ Asiakwa SOS adeɛ wɔ East Akim mansini wɔ Atɔeɛ mantam no mu no, ɔde too dwa sɛ ɔpɛpɔn bɛhyɛ berɛ foforɔ ase wɔ Ghana a ɔmanfoɔ no ho bɛtɔ wɔn wɔ sikasɛm ne biribiara mu
ɔde too sɛ sɛ ɔmanpanin Nana Addo a wɔayi no ma no asoeɛ dwumadie biara a wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛsɔ mu na wabɔ adwuma pa
Nnoɔma a ɔde maeɛ no bi ne ɛmo bɔtɔ nson, anwa, nkyene, asikyire, milk, nsa ne sika a wamfa ne dodoɔ anto dwa
Wɔahunu anuanom mmiɛnsa a wɔdaa wɔ beaeɛ a wɔn maame tɔn nsa wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem mansini no mu wɔ Apueɛ Mantam no mu sɛ wɔawu
Wɔn baasa wuiɛ esiane generator nwusie a wɔtwe kɔɔ wɔn mu no
Inspɛkta panin George Sakyi a ɔwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta station de too dwa sɛ obi frɛɛ wɔn ɔpɛnimaa no sɛ mmɔfra mmiɛnsa bi awu wɔ beaeɛ bi a wɔnom nsa
ɔkyerɛ mu a berɛ a ɔne ne ɔfisɛrs no duruu hɔ na wɔde awufoɔ no Abena Amos, , Arabi Dadzi, 13 and Akaba Dadzi, 7  adi kan kɔ Tarkwa aban ayaresabea a wɔretwɛn amannebɔ a ɛfa wɔn wuo no ho
ɔne Starr kaseɛ nsɛntwerɛni Emmanuel Ohene Gyan rekasa no, Mr. Sekyi kyerɛɛ mu sɛ na awufoɔ no ne wɔn maame na ɛte a na maame no na na ɔhwɛ Golden CityKitɔhen so wɔ Tarkwa Nsuem mansini no mu
ɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛɛ wɔn adwene wɔbɛda wɔn maame nkyɛn berɛ a wɔboaa wɔn maame ne no yɛɛ adwuma wieeɛ no
ɔfisa no kyerɛ mu a, ɔpɛnimaa da no wɔdumm kaseɛ esiane nsubrane a ɛtɔeɛ da no mu nti. Wei maa Madam Dadzi sɔɔ generator no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ ne mma no bɛda kanea. Adeɛ kyeeɛ a ɔkɔɔ so shop no mu no na ɔkɔhunuu sɛ ne mma no awu
Baako a ɔka ho a na watwa ahwe no regye ayarehwɛ. Apolisifoɔ no rehwɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ asɛm a asi no ho
Frankaatufoɔ ma National Democratic Congress (NDCɔ, John Mahama de ato dwa sɛ sɛ ɔyɛ nkonimfoɔ wɔ ɔpɛnimaa abatoɔ no mu a ɔbɛtaataa Menzgold panin Nana Appiah Mensah a dodoɔ no ara nim no sɛ NAM ama watua ɔmanfoɔ no sika ama wɔn
ɔrekasa wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem wɔ Apueɛ mantam no, Mr. Mahama de too sɛ ɛyɛ no nwanwa sɛ Akufo Addo no ɛmfa ho sɛ NAM agye ɔmanfoɔ no agyapadeɛ na mmom ɔde n’aniberɛ asi ɔmanfoɔ no so
ɔtoaa so sɛ, ɛdeɛn na ɛwɔ NAM ho a ɛma no yɛ soronko a Akufo Addo rebɔ ne ho ban no? Adɛn nti na wɔte apolisifoɔ gu kɔstɔmɛrs no so aberɛ a NAM-1 nam hɔ kwa
ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ n’aban bɛyɛ NAM ne ne mpaninfoɔ ho nhwehwɛmu yie na wɔagye ɔmanfoɔ no sika ama wɔn
Otemuafoɔ Ellen Asamoah a ɔtenaa Menzgold panin NAM asɛm so sɛ Nkran Circuit kɔɔto atu asɛm no ahyɛ Ahinime da a ɛdi kan wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu mu
Na ɔman no adi kan abɔ NAM soboɔ wɔ Kotonimaa wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu no mu wɔ Nkran Circuit kɔɔto
Polisi sɔpretɛnɛnt Sylvester Asare de too kɔɔto no anim sɛ akwankyerɛ a ne nsa aka ne sɛ ɔmfa soboɔ foforɔ ne NAM akyɛwpa nto hɔ ansa
Ayɛwohomɔbɔ no mu no, ASP Asare kakyerɛɛ kɔɔto no wɔretu kɔɔto no fo sɛ wɔntie akwankyerɛ a aba wɔ asɛm no ho no
Wɔsrɛɛ kɔɔto no sɛ wɔntu asɛm no nhyɛ da wɔn ne kwaadubɔfoɔ no nkɔyɛ ahoboa wɔ asɛm no ho mmra
ɔkaa sɛ sɛ afotusɛm no ba a wɔbɛma wɔn aso ate na wɔasiesie wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn kwaadu no ama wɔn aba kɔɔto abɛyɛ nea ɛfata
Nanso wɔkɔɔ kɔɔto Dwoada no kwaafubɔfoɔ no srɛɛ kɔɔto sɛ wɔntu asɛm no nhyɛ da foforɔ na kɔɔto tiee wɔn
NAM a wɔabɔ no kwaadu no daa ne ho adi wɔ kɔɔto
Ayɛwohumɔbɔ da a ɛtɔ so mu wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne du nkron mu no, Nkran Circuit kɔɔto maa NAM bail GHS billion
ɔkaa sɛ ɔnni fɔ wɔ soboɔ du mmiɛnsa a aban no de abɔ no no ho. ɛno aban no ayɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ nsesaeɛ wɔ soboɔ no mu na wɔahunu kwan a wɔbɛfa so
Afei nso ɛwɔ sɛ ɔde ne ho bɛkyerɛ apolisifoɔ Wukuada nnɔn du biara
Soboɔ a wɔdii kan de bɔɔ no bi ne korɔbɔ, adansekrumu, adwumayɛ a ɛnni nkrataa, agudeɛ tɔn a ɛnni nkrataa ne money laundering
Afei nso sika a na wɔte wagyegye afiri ne kɔstɔmɛrs hɔ dodoɔ nyinaa yɛ GHS billion
Okada a wɔde di daadaa dwuma reyɛ ayɛ ɔhaw
Apolisifoɔ nso kyerɛ sɛ korɔno bebree a ɛrekɔ so, akwanhyia ne mmara a wɔnni so wɔ akwantempɔn so nyinaa yɛ motorfoɔ
Akyinninyeɛ nni ho sɛ okada twie a ɛrekɔ so bebrebe no de ɔhaw reba na ɛwɔ sɛ wɔwɔ nhyehyɛeɛ de si ano kwan
Mmerɛ pii na yɛde aka ɔhaw a okada a wɔtwi yi de da
Saa berɛ yi ɔhaw baako a ɔman no rehyia ne sɛdeɛ wɔbɛfa so ate motor ne okada a wɔde di daadaa dwuma no
Afe mpem mmienu ne du mmienu mu no, mmarahyɛbadwam de Road Traffiɔ Regulations, 2012 (L.I. 2180 ɔ yɛɛ mmara a ɛbɛhwɛ akɔneabadie mu nsɛm
Mmara no baa sɛ ɛnni kwan sɛ wɔde okada ne motor fa ɔmanfoɔ no gye sɛ ebia wɔde di dwuma sɛ ɔourier anaa delivery Services. Afei wɔhyɛɛ DVLA sɛ ɛnni kwan sɛ wɔma motor foɔ no krataa a wɔde di dwuma sɛ wɔde reyɛ adwuma afa ɔmanfoɔ
Okada ne pragya no abunkam afa ɔman yi mu a wɔmfa ho ne mmara a mmarahyɛbadwam no hyɛeɛ no
Sɛ wokɔ nkuraaseɛ no mu a okada ne pragya no na wɔde kɔ adwa so, asopiti ne mmeammea ahodoɔ
Wɔn a wɔwɔ kuro kɛse mu no fa okada ne pragya sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔnni traffik mu
Esiane sɛ ne boɔ yɛ fo nti no dodoɔ no ara pɛ ne fa
Sɛ kaa nni a pragya ne okada yi ara na wɔdwane kɔtoa no
Nanso nnipa pii no ara na ɛmpɛ okada ne pragya esiane dede ne atuturasɛm a wɔdi no akwan so nti no
Akwanhyia ahodoɔ a ɛnam okada so ɛba no yɛ adeɛ a ɛwɔ sɛ ani kɔ ho
Nnwumakuo bebree a Ghana Medicalassociationne National Road Safety Authority ka ho na afrɛ sɛ wɔntua okada a ɛdi dwuma wɔ ɔman no mu no
Wei ato ɔman no agyaagyaa mu
Aba saa no sei ɛfiri sɛ ɛmmfa ho ne mmara a wɔahyɛ de atua saa nnoɔma yi, abɛyɛ ahotɔsoɔ ama Ghanafoɔ pii
Yɛn a yɛwɔ Daily Graphic ha deɛ yɛsusu sɛ ɔman no hwɛ mmara no bio na yɛhwɛ akwan pa a yɛbɛtumi afa ama saa dwumadie yi akɔ so
Sɛ wokɔ India a pragya na ɛdi akɔtene wɔ wɔn akɔneabadie mu nanso yɛntee nsɛmnsɛm fa ho te sɛ deɛ yɛte no Ghana no
Enti ɛdeɛn na yɛbɛtumi asua afiri India hɔ a yɛbɛtumi de aba de aba yɛn sestɛm no mu?
ɛwɔ sɛ yɛde hyɛ yɛn adwene mu sɛ esiane adwumasɛm a ayɛ den nti wɔn wɔtwi okada ne pragya hu no sɛ ɛyɛ adwuma a wɔbɛnya afiri mu de ahwɛ wɔn ho ne wɔn abusuafoɔ
Seesei ara okada ne pragya abɛyɛ ɔhaw ne ateetee na yɛn yɛwɔ Daily Graphic susu sɛ yɛma wɔn nteteeɛ ne yɛyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔbɛfa so aka afidie no a ɛbɛboa ama ɔman no akɔ so
Wɔrehwɛ mmara a ɛma kwan ma wɔyɛ adwuma no, wɔyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛhwɛ wɔn a wɔka afidie no sɛ akwanhyia biara ba mu a
Sɛ wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ no gu akwan mu a ɛbɛboa ama Ghana Polisifoɔ no ahyɛ mmara no kena na aboa ma wɔakye okada ne pragya a wɔde di krɔno no
Mprɛmprɛn yi Ghanafoɔ pii no ara na wɔn adwene ayɛ wɔn ntata wɔ saa mmara yi ho esiane ɛho mfaso papa ne bɔne
Daily Graphic gye di sɛ sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ mmara ne pɛrepɛreyɛ ba yɛn akwan so ne yɛn akɔneabadie mu nsɛm mu deɛ a ɛnneɛ ɛwɔ sɛ yɛsɔ yɛn mmɛn mu na yɛhwɛ ɔhaw yi mprɛmprɛn yi ara anaasɛ yɛnhwɛ koraa.
Menkae da biara m’ani gyee wɔ Ghana sɛ Fiada a atwa mu yi a na ɛyɛ Green Ghana da.
Yei ne da a yɛn nyinaa ara bɔɔ mu kɔɔ abɔten sɛ yɛrekɔ dua dua. 
Mebaa Ghana mfeɛ aduonu atwa mu yi mahunu sɛ nea ɛrekɔ so wɔ yɛn man yi mu nea ɛwɔ asaase ho adesua nwoma mu no bɔ abira. Yei abɛyɛ nkunimdie dwumadie a yayɛ sɛ yɛ de bɔ yɛn nsaase a ɛresɛe ho ban.
Nnuaba ɔpepem nnum na Nsaase ne Agudeɛ Asoeɛ no de maa yɛn sɛ yɛndua no de anigyeɛ a ebi so mmaaeɛ wɔ mmerɛ tenten mu na aba.
Ghanafoɔ bɛhwɛ ahu a na adeɛ baako a ɛhia sɛ yɛte y'ani hwɛ sene bibiara aka paa ara ne yɛn nsaasetam teabea a yɛfrɛ no Ghana no. 
Adeɛ a ɛho hia sene akwan mu mmena, sukuu dan a atete, ayaresabea a nni mpa anaa sukuu nkwadaa nni abɛɛfo badwemma mfidie mpo no, merepae mu aka sɛ mpo yareɛ a ɛretrɛ no adeɛ baako a ɛwɔ sɛ yɛn nyinaa bo fu ho paa ne yɛn nsaase tebea, nsaase a ayera ne kwaeɛ, ne nsutene awe, sutɔberɛ Kɔtɔnima bosome a seisei ara abɛyɛ ɔhyew ne ɔpɛ. 
Menhwɛɛ asaase ho adesua nwoma a asuafoɔ resua wɔ sukuu mu nansei nanso mɛtumi aka sɛ sɛnea na Ghana nsaase teɛ berɛ a ne mekɔ sukuu no nte sɛ nnɛ Ghana. 
Yɛgu so kasa fa kwaeɛ dodoɔ ho nanso nokwasɛm no sɛ nnyɛ sei na yɛn nsaase no teɛ 
Yɛgu so kasa fa kwaeɛ mu mmoa ho nanso y'aku wɔn nyinaa ara agye watenabea abɔ so.
Kwaeɛ dodoɔ ne mu mmoa no abɛka yɛn kasa ho nanso nte saa ara koraa
Mpo nea na yɛdwene sɛ ɛyɛ kwaeɛ a yɛmfa yɛn nsa nka no nyinaa ara yatu mu agudeɛ ne sika kɔkɔɔ nyinaa ara ama no asa. 
Ebia yɛn nokwaredie 
M'adwene mu no sɛ nipa anaa nnipakuo biara wɔ hɔ a ɛwɔ sɛ yɛbɔ wɔn din huru wɔn wɔ Ghana ha a na ɛyɛ wɔn a annyɛ w'asɛnhia sɛ wɔbɛkɔ abɔnten akɔpɛ nnuaba akɔ dua nnua Fiada a atwa mu yi no.
Sɛ wohu sɛ ɛho behia a wobɛkasa afa bibiara ho a, nneɛma a nkɔ yie, akwan a yɛnguu so, Free SHS, bosea a yɛrebɔ ho, akwan a nkanea nni so mpo Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ atɛmmuo na woannua dua Fiada a atwa mu yi a, 
Mɛsusu ho sɛ sɛ wo ka nnipakuo yi ho a ɛnkaa akyire sɛ wobɛsan woho. 
Yɛredua nnuaba ama anyini abɛyɛ nnua a ɛyɛ fɛ na ɛgyina so de akata yɛn man yi so yɛ mmere tenten adwuma. 
Yadua nnua yi awie no, ɛwɔ sɛ yɛhwɛ wɔn yie ma wɔnyini na ɛno nso hia mmerɛ ne adwumaden. 
Fiada atwa mu yi nsuo tɔɔ wɔ Nkran, (mate sɛ ɛtɔɔe wɔ mantam ahodoɔ wɔ ɔman yi mu) yɛhwɛ sɛ nea ɔpɛ aba yi a na megye di sɛ na ɛtwa sɛ ɛtɔ. 
Nsuo antɔ a ɛwɔ sɛ yɛtae gu nnuaba no so nsuo. Na mmerepa biara nni hɔ nsene Kitawonsa da a ɛtɔ dubaakob a yɛtu sii hɔ sɛ yɛbɛdua nnua nanso wiem nsakyeraeɛ ne yɛn nsaase nte sɛ nea na ɛte kane no biom nti ɛwɔ sɛ ani ba nnuaba no ho yie.
Sɛ woannua dua Fiada a atwa mu yi a wobɛtumi adua baako anaa mmienu bi na woaboa abɔ nea yadua dada no ho ban 
Mmere tiawa pɛ na yɛde twa dua ato fam nanso woredua ama n'aso aduru mpɛnpɛnsoɔ a ɛsi pi no yɛ mfeɛ bebree asɛm.
Sɛ yɛbɛtumi adane yɛn nsaase yi ani akɔ 'kwaeɛ brentuo' a asaase ho adesua nwoma ne y'afahyɛ ho nnwom, sɛ nea ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo kaaeɛ no, yɛreyɛ Ghana ahaban mono bɛba abɛyɛ dwumadie titire ama yɛn.
Mesusu sɛ nea ɛdi kan no sɛ yɛbɛgyae asaase sɛeɛ na yɛma yɛn nsaase mmerɛ ma ne home na ɛsa neho yareɛ wie na yɛdua nnua no a ɛbɛnyini wɔ asomdwoeɛ mu.  
Mereda m'anikusɛm bi adi wɔ ha. Meyɛ kwaeɛ mu ba, yɛwoo me kwaeɛ mu nanso ɛwɔ mu sɛ bea koro no koraa nnyɛ kwaeɛ mu biom. 
Medɔ nnua, bibiara ntumi nhyɛ anigyeɛ awia nsutɔ berɛ wɔ kwaeɛburentuo mu ne hwam a nsuo no tɔ wie a ɛfiri annwea no mu ba no. 
Ɛwɔ sɛ abɔfra biara nya saa suahunu yi mu akwannya hwɛ wiem mu nnua a anyini sene wɔn nana prenu.
M'anikusɛm foforɔ a mereda nadi ne nnipa a medɔ wɔn yie wɔ wiase mu ha paa ne ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nsaase ne agudeɛ so, Samuel Abu Jinapor, Mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Damango. 
Mmerɛ bi a atwa mu a yɛyii wo sɛ ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ fagudeɛ so no, na ɛyɛ adwuma ɛyɛ fɛ, afei rekɔ atia asaase ne nsu sɛeɛ ne mfidi a yɛde tutu fam hyeɛ.
Mepɛ sɛ Ghana san kɔ ne nkyi kɔ yɛ ɔman a ɛwɔ kwaeɛbirentuo, nnua a ɛgyina so, nsutene a ɛyɛ fɛ na ɛyɛ korɔgyee na mepɛ sɛ yei nyinaa ara si wɔ Ɔ soafoɔ Abu Jinapor mmerɛ so.
Na mehunuu nea menyɛ meho berɛ a mehunuu sɛ ɔhyɛ Rangers ataadeɛ Fiada a atwa mu no nanso mehunuu adwumaden a ɛkɔ dwumadie yi nhyehyɛeɛ ne wieeɛ mu. Mema no tiri nkwa na mewɔ awerɛhyɛmu sɛ nnuaba a yɛduaa no Fiada no nyinaa ara bɛtena na anyini. 
Ahaban mono Ghana bɛyɛ yiedie Ghana.
Sɛ ɛba dwom pa a, woyi highlife dwontoni Akwaboah nsi nkyɛn a nnyɛ yie nanso ɛnnyɛ den koraa sɛ worebobɔ dwomtofoɔ a ɛdi mu a wobɛbɔ no afa so firisɛ nnyɛ dabiara na yɛte no nka.
Nanso dwontoni no se nha no koraa sɛ ɔnka amanfoɔ adwontofoɔ a ɛdi mu kuo ho. ƆƆ ka kyerɛɛ. Graphic Showbiz sɛ ɔne dwontoni biara nni akansie na biom nso ɔnyi n'anim nkyerɛ dabiara no ɛboa no ma no pa dwom pa ho adi. 
Akwaboa kyerɛ mu sɛ, dwom a yɛda nadi ntoatoasoɔ sɛ ɛbɛma dwontoni din aka manfoɔ tiri mu no nnyɛ bɔhyɛ wɔbɛkura wo mu daa. 
"Mempere meho mpa dwom ho firisɛ mepɛ sɛ meto me bo ase na menya no yie. Adwontofoɔ bebree a wɔn dwom gyee din nanso berɛ tiawa mu no yanhunu wɔn biom. Mempɛ sɛ mɛyɛ te sɛ saa adwontofoɔ yi. Bibiara nhyɛ me so sɛ me mpa dwom ho ntama nti berɛ biara me de dwom foforɔ bɛba biara no Ghanafoɔ dɔ no ntɛm paa ara"
"Nnyɛ sɛ dabiara wopa dwom foforɔ adi. Ghanafoɔ yɛ soronko nti sɛ wɔyɛ wadwene sɛ wɔmfii wo a bibiara nni hɔ woyɛ a ɛbɛsɔ wɔn ani. "Mfeɛ du nnum akyi mpo mɛpɛ sɛ mɛyɛ sei are sene sɛ mɛpa dwom ho ntama ntoatoasoɔ ama maanfoɔ werɛ afiri me afe baako anaa mmienu akyi" sɛ nea ɔsee Graphic Showbiz nansei ara no.
Zimbabwe apolisifoɔ ahyɛ anammɔntuo bi a ɛbɛko atia ayakayakadeɛ a mmaa ne mmayewa wɔ abatoɔ berɛ mu.
Nnipa ho faahodie kuo te sɛ mma faahodie, Canada Asoeɛ a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe ne Zimbabwe Man Kwaadubɔfoɔ Asoeɛ boaa apolisifoɔ daa saa dwumadie yi adi Wukuada.
Apolisifoɔ panin, Commissioner-General Godwin Matanga rekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no daa no adi sɛ polisifoɔ mfa nsɛm a ɛfa mmaa ayakayakadeɛ ahogono so. 
Ɔ hyɛɛ mmaa nso sɛ wɔnyi hu nto nkyɛn na wɔmbɔ ayakayakadeɛ ho amanneɛ. 
Mmaa nkabomkuo dwamtenani, Sally Ncube tɔ kɔɔ so kaa sɛ n'ani asɔ polisifoɔ no atuhoakyɛ adwuma a wɔde rebɔ bɔ mmaa ho aban afiri ayakayakadeɛ ho wɔ abatoɔ berɛ mu. 
Dawurubɔ adwumayɛfoɔ biara nni hɔ mprenpren yi 
Ayaresafoɔ a ɛwɔ man yi mu ayaresabea te sɛ West End ne Parirenyatwa ayɛ wɔn adwen sɛ wɔnnhwɛ ayarefoɔ a wɔsusu sɛ wate corona virus no bi firisɛ wɔnni ho nimdeɛ biara. 
Nɛɛsefoɔ bi nom nso tee atua wɔ Mpilo Ayaresabea Dwoada no firisɛ wɔnni ahobanbɔ nneɛma wɔde bɛko atia yareɛ no. 
Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ nyarewa a ɛsae wɔ Apɔmuden Asoeɛ Dr. Portia Manangazira ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ Zimbabweni baa bi a ɔfirii China baeɛ nso annya ayarehwɛ wɔ Parirenyatwa hɔ. 
Parirenyatwa Ayaresabea yɛ nhwehwɛmu akyire baa agyinaeɛ sɛ wɔnhwɛ mma ayarefoɔ nte corona virus yareɛ no nti ayarefoɔ nkɔ gye ayarehwɛ wɔ Wilkins Hospital ne Beatrice Infectious Ayaresabea sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ a ayarefoɔ ne ayaresafoɔ a ɛwɔ ayaresabea hɔ nte corona virus yareɛ no.
Ayaresabea no toaa so sɛ wɔbɛsi apata bi wɔ abɔnten na wɔde ahwehwɛ wɔn a nteeɛ kyerɛ sɛ wate yareɛ no bi na wɔwie a ɔde wɔn akɔ ayaresabea a agye nteteeɛ wɔ yareɛ no ho.
Harare Kurokɛseɛ panin a ɔda ayaresa ano, Dr. Prosper Chonzi nso kaa sɛ West End ayaresabea no amma ho kwan sɛ wɔbɛboa Chinani baa bi a na wɔsusu sɛ ɔwɔ yareɛ no bi ma no wuui nanso na ɛnte saa. 
Yɛfrɛɛ ayaresabea no wɔ ahomatrofoɔ so wɔka kyerɛɛ yɛn sɛ yɛmfa yɛn nsɛmbisa mmra nanso yannya mmuaeɛ biara berɛ a yɛkɔɔ mframa mu
Nnipa bɛyɛ mpem mmiɛnsa ne aha nnwɔte akyiri aduowɔtwe mmienu na yareɛ yi aku wɔn wɔ wiase afanaa nyinaaa ara
China na di kan wɔ nnipa a awu kɛse paa ansa na Italy ne Iran atoa so. Wɔ Abibirem, nnipa mmienu na awu wɔ Egypt ne Morocco. 
Nanso Abibirem aman dubaako a yareɛ yi aka wɔn ne Algeria, Burkina Faso, South Africa, Senegal, Tunisia, Togo, Egypt, Cameroon, DRC, Nigeria ne Morocco. Nnipa du mmiɛnsa na yareɛ yi aka wɔn wɔ South Africa.
Harare Kurokɛseɛ Fotufokuo abɔ manfoɔ a wɔte Budiriro ne Glen Norah mpɔtam sɛ mma wɔn nnom abura mu nsuo anaa mbura a wɔretutu firisɛ nsuo no nnyɛ. 
Ɛnam nsuo a ɛho ayɛ den nti, manfoɔɔ a ɛtete Glen Norah ne Budiriro de abura mu nsuo na ɛyɛ adeɛ. 
Nanso fotufokuo no kasamafoɔ Michael Chideme kaa sɛ nhwehwɛmu kyerɛ wɔyɛɛ no wɔ Budiriro akuraase wɔ Glen Norah huu sɛ fagutudeɛbea bebree no ara ayamtuo yareɛ te sɛ ayamtuo atiridi asɛe wɔn nsuo 
Mr Chideme kaa sɛ fagudeɛtubea bebree no ara mu nnɔ nti ɛbɛma yareɛ no akɔ soro  
Chideme kaa sɛ fotufokuo no rema manfoɔ a ɛwɔ mpɔtam yi nsuo dabiara. 
Panin a ɔda Mpɔtam Nsuo Nkabomkuo ano, Mr Hardlife Mudzingwa bɔɔ futofokuo no akyi sɛ ɛnam nsuo a mma nti na manfoɔ retu fagudeɛ no.
Mr Mudzingwa toaa so sɛ mantam bi nom nnya nsuo dabiara.
Harare manfoɔ bebree no ara nnya nsuo dabiara ɛno nti na fagutudeɛ ɛrekɔ so nkuraaseɛ berɛ wabra sɛ mma obiara nnyɛ saa. 
Manfoɔ nso se nsuo no yɛ fin paa nti ama wɔdwen wɔn apɔmuden ho. 
Nneɛma nkɔ so yie wɔ mmɔfra ayaresabea firisɛ nɛɛsefoɔ nnyɛ wadwuma yie. 
Ayarefoɔ a ɛwɔ Parirenyatwa Ayaresabea ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ wɔn ho dwirii wɔn berɛ a aban bɔɔ ka boaboaa nnipa ano wɔ man no afanaa berɛ na ayarefoɔ resesa ntatea firi w'ano wɔ ayaresabea hɔ. 
Shupikai Gachitawa wɔ abɔfra ne nan mu abu da Parirenyatwa Ayaresabea. Ms Gachitawa se wɔmma no nnuro, nnware no mpo na kampɛsɛ wasiesie ne kuro nam sɛ nɛɛsefoɔ nni hɔ nti
Ms Gachitawa kaa sɛ aban no ntie manfoɔ suu na wɔnhyehyɛ nɛɛsefoɔ mma wɔn mmɛyɛ adwuma.
Ayarefoɔ a ɛwɔ Innocent Mazise nsam abɔ aban no soboɔ sɛ wayi nɛɛsefoɔ a wate atua no adi. Mr. Mazise kaa sɛ aban no nhwehwɛ nɛɛsefoɔ no nsɛm mu na ɔntoto. 
Papa bi a na ɔmpɛ sɛ yɛbɔ ne din ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ ayaresabea adan no hɔ nte firisɛ nnipa biara nni hɔ wɔresiesie hɔ. Ɔ toaa so kaa sɛ ayarefoɔ no bi rewuwu firisɛ nnuro ne aboafoɔ biara nni hɔ. 
Maame baako a ɔse mma yɛmmɔ ne din se Ms Gumbo aka akyerɛ no sɛ ɔreyɛ ntotoeɛ sɛ ɔbɛyi ayarefoɔ ɛwɔ ne nsam afiri ayaresabea hɔ firisɛ yɛmmaa no nnuro fi Dwoada. 
Twerɛtwerɛfoɔ ma Zimbabwe Ayaresafoɔ a wɔhwɛ nnipa faahodie, Evans Masitara kaa sɛ aban agyinaeɛ sɛ ɔbɛyi nɛɛsefoɔ adi no yɛ animguasesɛm firisɛ wɔrebrɛ yareɛ no ho. 
Wɔ krataa wɔtwerɛ kɔ maa kuo mma no, Zimbabwe Nɛɛsefoɔ Nkabomkuo no kaa sɛ aban agyinaeɛ no mmɔ wɔn hu. Nteeɛ kyerɛ mu sɛ wɔbɛtoa atuateɛ no so. 
Ɔ manpanin abɛdiakyire Constantino Guvheya Chiwenga twerɛɛ krataa yii nɛɛsefoɔ nyinaa adi nnora. 
Nnaadaa kasamfonini bi a Islamic State daa nadi bosome atwa mu kyerɛɛ kuo no nsa a wɔto frɛɛ manfoɔ sɛ wɔntrɛ Jihad dwumadie wɔ wiase afanaa nyinaa berɛ a wɔbɔɔ anuanom a ɛwɔ Burkina Faso ne Mali aba so sɛ wahyɛ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛdi dwuma ama kuo no. 
Ansarul Islam a ase kyerɛ ne sɛ Islam Banbɔkuo yɛ mantam kuo bi a nsɛnpakani a wagye din yie Ibrahim Malam Dicko tee no 2016 mu. Ɔ kyerɛ mu sɛ ɔne Islamists akofoɔ a ɛwɔ Mali no bɔɔ ani tuu wɔn so sa gyee man no atifi bɔɔ so wɔ 2012 mu maa French aban no te gyinaa mu. 
Dicko wuui Oforisuo bosome wɔ afe 2017 mu no ne nuabarima Jafar na di kuo no anim seisei ara wanya akodeɛ mmoa afiri AQIM ne ISGS, sɛnea Nipa Faahodie Kuo seɛ no. 
Adwuma ne mpuntuo ho ateetee ama Burkina Faso abɛyɛ beaeɛ a Jihadfoɔ no retete manfoɔ biom nso akuo nktetewa bebree a wɔnnka akuo akɛseɛ a wɔde ahofama ama Nkramosom gyedie yi.
Sikasɛm ho benfo no kyerɛɛ mu sɛ bebree no ara reko kuayɛ nsaase anaa reko atia aban kɛtɛasehyɛ nanso "wɔgye Jihadfoɔ" din no to mu firisɛ wɔyɛ Kramofoɔ"
Nanso Ncube kaa sɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ nnya gyedie wɔ aban no mu sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ ama mpuntuo aba sikakorabea nkorabata no mu ama man fotoɔ no so aba mfasoɔ ama manfoɔ. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ wɔde akwan hodoɔ agu kwan mu sɛ ɛbɛboa ama nneɛma asi yie wɔ ɔman no mu.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Kwekwe Mfinimfi Matambanadzo nso ka kyerɛɛ Ncube sɛ te a ɔtee nhoma no mu duru firii US dollar no ho ama nneɛma mu ayɛ den wɔ man no mu. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ ɛho bɛhia sɛ aban bɛhwɛ nea wɔbɛtumi ayɛ na watoto adwumayɛfoɔ ne ankorɛankorɛ nnwuma akatua mu sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛne nneɛma boɔ bɛsi asikan. 
Nanso Mr Ncube kaa sɛ aban atoto adwumayɛfoɔ akatua mu dada ɛno nti na wɔde mfasoɔ akeka ho no. 
Wɔn san nim sɛ ankorɛankorɛ adwumayɛfoɔ regye akatua keseɛ.
Nanso Mr Matambanadzo kaa sɛ akatua ntomu no so amma mfasoɔ firisɛ nneɛma boɔ nso akɔ soro ntɛm paa ara.
Nanso Mr. Ncube kaa sɛ ɔnhwɛ Amɛrika dollar no so ntoto adwumayɛfoɔ akatua mu, ɔtoaa so kaa sɛ ɛwɔ mu sɛ nneɛma boɔ rekɔ soro nanso nneɛma no bi boɔ reba fam firisɛ nnipa kakra bi na ɛretɔ. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ ɛda hɔ pefee sɛ na nnwuma akɛseɛ retɔ aburolyire sika firi abɔnten nanso ɛwɔ sɛ wɔtɔ firi sikakorabea mmom.
Ɔ kaa sɛ sikakorabea wɔ Amɛrika dollar ɔpepem aha nnwɔtwe aburokyire sika mu na ɛno ne sika wɔbɛsɛe wɔ nnwuma akɛseɛ ho. 
Wɔ nsɛm foforɔ mu no, Chipinge Mmarahyɛbɛdwani Matthew Mlambo kaa sɛ n'ani nnye sɛ watu nnipa mpem mmienu afiri wɔn nsaase so. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ yei rekɔ so mantam bebree wɔ ɔman no mu.
Ɔ soafoɔ abɛdiakyire a ɔhwɛ Kuayɛ so, Douglas Karoro kaa sɛ nnipa a watu wɔn yɛ wɔn a na ɔte baabi na nnyɛ te sɛ nantwie adidibea so. 
Watu mmusuakuo bebree afiri nsaase a aban de maa wɔn mfeɛ atwa mu wɔ Chemagora a ɛwɔ Midlands ne Mashonaland West. Faahodie akofoɔ nso redi asɛm yi ho abooboo. 
MDC a Nelson Chamisa da ano no se wankɔ nhyiamu a manpanin Emerson Mnangagwa frɛɛeɛ no firisɛ Mwangagwa no ara na ahwɛ ama basabasayɛ aba man no mu.
MDC no kyerɛ sɛ Mr Mnangagwa nni ho kwan sɛ ɔfrɛ kasakyerɛ ma akuo mmienu no berɛ a ɔyɛ kuo no mu nipa. 
Ɔ reyi nsɛmmisa wɔ nsa a ɔto frɛɛ no wɔ manpanin dwumadibea no, MDC adwumayɛfoɔ panin, Sessel Zvizvai kaa sɛ wɔn panin no antumi amma nhyiamu no firisɛ na nsɛm bebree wɔ hɔ a ɛwɔ wɔpɛ ho asɛm ka.
Mr Zvizvai kaa sɛ na manpanin abatoɔ no ka nsɛm a ɔdii kan dii ho ho abooboo.
Ɔ san kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ manfoɔ a wɔnnyɛ amanyɔsɛm na di nkitahodie no anim sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ a pɛpɛɛpɛyɛ bɛkɔ ama obiara 
Mr Zvizvai san kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ nkabomkuo te sɛ Southern African Development Community, Africa Union ne United Nations boa nkitahodie no.
MDC no abɔ nnipa du bi din ama Mnangagwa sɛ wɔne Chamisa nnya nkitahodie.
Nea ɛka yei bi ho ne sɛ wɔbɛgyae ahunahuna, wɔbɛhwɛ sɛ wɔnnto obiara mmonaa, wɔbɛyi nnipa a ɛda afiase ɛnam amanbuo nti, aban bɛyi wɔn nsa afiri mmara dwuma mu ne obuo ma nnipa faahodie. 
Kuo no kasamafoɔ, Jacob Mafume ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ ntamsiesie nhyiamu no, Mnangagwa nyi asraafoɔ mfiri mmɔten so na ɔmma kuo a ɛsɔre tia no mu nnipa a wadwane afiri kuro no mu nsan mmra wakyi. 
Kramofoɔ Akofokuo mmiɛnsa a ɛdi mu agye Burkina Faso atifi ne atɔeɛ abɔ so: Ansarul Islam,  Group for The Support of Islam and Muslim (GSIM) ne Islamic State in the Greater Sahara (ISGS)
Ntohyɛsoɔ a ɛmu yɛ den a asi nansei ara ne Ɔ pɛpɔn bosome wɔ afe 2016 mu a ɛsii wɔ ahɔhogyebea bi a ɛwɔ Burkina Faso ahenkuro Ouagadougou mu a ɛkuuu nnipa aduasa - a al-Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb (AQIM) nsa hyɛ aseɛ - kuo yi ne Jihadfoɔ akuo mmienu na aka abɔ mu - Ansar Dine ne al-Mourabitoum ate GSIM
Manyuchi a WBO Silver Belt no yɛ no dea no ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ Ali firi a wafiri mu no de amena kɛseɛ na abɛto hɔ firisɛ ɛnam so maa manfoɔ bebree no ara ani bɛgyɛɛ kuturuku agodie no ho. Manyuchi kaa sɛ, "Barima a na ɔwɔ adom akyɛdeɛ, na me papa nso bɔ akuturuku nti na ɔpɛ n'asɛm na na mebu no firisɛ ɛnam no so na menyaa ahoɔden wɔ agodie no mu"
Ɔ kɔɔ so kaa sɛ, "Na dodoɔ no ara nim Muhammad Ali sɛ ɔkaa sɛ - sensɛn wiem te sɛ afafantɔ na bɔ te sɛ wowa," Yɛnim me sɛ me yɛ wowa a menni meho adaagye firisɛ me din de nwowa buo nti ɛyɛ m'ani gye sɛ Muhammad Ali ko maa me dɔm firisɛ ɛwɔ ne mfonini na ɔno ne nea ɔda nso, meserɛ meka sɛ mɛkɔ so de suahunu a menya firii Muhammad Ali hɔ no ako"
Wiase mpaninfoɔ a Amɛrika manpanin a watwa mu, Bill Clinton ne aburokyire mpaninfoɔ na wɔrehwɛ w'anim sɛ wɔbɛkɔ ayie no. Abɛdiakyirefoɔ bebree no ara na ne Ali bɛdi nkra Fiada yi. Akwan a ɛrekɔ ayie no ase bɛbɔ mma. 
Ali abusuafoɔ kaa sɛ ayiyɔ no ba awieɛ a obiara bɛkɔ fie akɔ sie wufoɔ no. 
Abusua kasamafoɔ, Bob Gunnell kaa sɛ ɔhyɛɛ Ali ayie da mfeɛ bebree atwa mu firisɛ na n'apɛdeɛ no no. Na ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyi obibiara asotire fa n'agyamdie ho. 
Ɔ woo Ali sɛ Cassius Marcellus Clay Jr wɔ afe 1942 mu nanso ɔsesaa ne din berɛ a ɔfirii Kristosom mu kɔɔ Kramosom mu. 
Ɔ san nyaa sika kɔkɔɔ animuonyamhyɛdeɛ wɔ akofoɔ nketewa a ɛwɔ amuɛdurufoɔ kuo no ase berɛ a ɔdii Zbigniew Pietrkowski a ɔfri Poland so nkunim. 
Amɛrika nnwuma bebree refa COVID-19 haw ho adwen sɛ ɛnam so na ama adwumayɛfoɔ dodoɔ no ara reyɛ adwuma afiri w'afie mu sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ a yareɛ no ntrɛ. 
Amanneɛ kyerɛ mu sɛ nnwuma a aka yɛyɛ no fie a nnyɛ yie no te sɛ nnuane nnwuma no ayiyi nnwumayɛfoɔ no bi adi firisɛ wɔntumi nkɔ adwuma. 
Mantam bebree a ɛwɔ Amɛrika no abra nnipa bebree nhyiamu te sɛ adidibea ne sinihwɛbea nti ɛnam so ama wayi nnwumayɛfoɔ a ɛwɔ saa beaeɛ asi nkyɛn kɔpem berɛ a nneɛma bɛyɛ yie. 
US aban no abɔ amanneɛ sɛ wayi dollar ɔpepepepem ato nkyɛn sɛ ɔde bɛsɔ ɔman no sikasɛm asene na ɔde aboa nnwuma ne nnipa yareɛ no aka wɔn no.  
Nnipa bɛbro mpem nsia na wanya yareɛ yi bi wɔ Amɛrika ama bɛbro ɔha ahwere wɔn nkwa. 
Zimbabweni bi a ɔte Amɛrika kuro Maryland mu a yɛfrɛ no Ms. Shingie Mangwiro a ɔno nso reyɛ adwuma firi fie se nsusuiɛ a ɛfa adwuma a yɛyɛ no fie no yɛ nsusuiɛ pa na ɛboa ma nnipa bebree nhyiamu so te.
Ms. Mangwiro a ɛtɔ da a ɔhaw ba a ɔyɛ adwuma firi fie no se ɔnni haw biara fa ne fie mfidie ho firisɛ dabiara ɔnya kwan di no dwumadie.
Wɔsan se anammɔn a US manpanin Donald Trump ne aban nsoeɛ atu no bɛboa asɔ ɔhaw yi ano. 
Nanso Ms. Mangwiro rehyɛ manfoɔ a wɔwɔ fie sɛ ɛwɔ mu sɛ yareɛ no nwuraa Amɛr wɔmma ahonidie nnyɛ w'asɛnhia 
Nnipa wɔnni baabi te name nsuyiri a ɛsii wɔ Tokwe Murkosi nsuban a Masvingo masnini mu afe a atwa mu no se asetena mu ayɛ den ama wɔn firisɛ mmoa biara mfiri aban ne NGOs hɔ mma biom. 
Ɔ bɔɔ amanneɛ yi berɛ ɔpaa nhwehwɛmu a ɛfa ɔhaw a nnipa nam mu ho ntama. 
Ɔ rekasa wɔ Human Rights Watch mmara a ɔpaa ho ntama wɔ Nuanetsi Ranch no nhwehwɛmu kyerɛɛ mu sɛ nnipa a wɔnni baabi te ɛnam nsuyiri no nti ani ngye sɛ aban no mmaa wɔn baabi ntenaa afe baako akyi.

Ms Muzenda se nipa no wɔ yareɛ no dada nti aduane a ɔnnya wɔ baabi watu wakɔ tena asi wɔn ho kwan sɛ wɔbɛnom wɔn nnuro nti wɔrewuwu dada.

Mprenpren no, Dewa Mavhinga ne Humans Right Watch adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔreyi nnipa afiri hɔ no hyɛɛ Humans Rights Commission no sɛ wɔnyɛ nhwehwɛmu mfa tu a ɔretu nnipa afiri Tokwe Murkosi no ne tia a ɔretitia nnipa faahodie so no.  
Yɛnntee asɛm yi ho biribiara mfirii aban hɔ firisɛ mantam soafoɔ Kudakwashe Bhasikiti mfa n'ahomatrofoɔ ɛna afisɛm soafoɔ Kembo Mohadi nso reyiyi Basikiti nsɛmmisa ano. 
Mavhinga hyɛɛ wɔn a asɛm ato wɔn no sɛ wɔmfa sɛm no nkɔ asɛnnibea.

Khumalo kaa sɛ na ɛyɛ no hwahwa sɛ na FIFA ntua n'adwumayɛfoɔ ka berɛ a na ɔnya sika mmoa firi FIFA hɔ. 
Bɔɔlbɔ kyeame Prosper Muzanharo kaa sɛ nkuguo a Yong Warriors dii wɔ South Africa no ne mmɔdenbɔ nni twaka biara na mmom na kɔm na ɛde wɔn ɛnam sika a na ZIFA mfa mma wɔn nti. 
Agonkansie kyeame Howard Musonza kaa sɛ ZIFA bɔ fam nti sɛn wɔntumi ntua adwumaɛ ka a wɔnyi wadi. 
Young Warriors ne tetenani foforɔ, Nation Dube a ɔbɛhyɛɛ Pasuwa anan mu no na bɛtu kwan akɔ Africa Games wɔ Congo Brazaville wɔ Ɛbɔ bosome mu.
Warriors nso bɛnya tetenani foforɔ berɛ wɔn ne Guinea bɛsi akan wɔ afe 2017 Africa Cup of Nations Ɛbɔ bosome mfitiaseɛ mu. 
Asɔre mpaninfoɔ rehyia mu abɔ mpaeɛ apɛ ɔhaw yi ho anoyie berɛ a Manpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa refrɛ nkabom afiri amanyɛkuo ahodoɔ hɔ. 
Watwa intanɛt mu san ahyɛ mmara ato hɔ sɛ mma obiara mpue wɔ Eswatini, Abibirem Anaafoɔ ahennie a na yɛfrɛ no Swaziland no mu.
Wayi Banbɔ akofoɔ asotire sɛ nnipa a wɔreyɛ yɛkyerɛ no asuae sɛ wɔbɛyere yɛkyerɛ no mu ara akɔpem se wobɛyɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ amanyɛ no mu.
Sɛntwerɛni bi ka kyerɛɛ BBC sɛ na atuturasɛm rekɔ so anadwo berɛ wɔ Manzini kurokɛseɛ mu ama watoto ɔman no ahyɛ nyinaa ara mu.
Ɔ yɛkyerɛ a akɔ so nna kakra yi ama bebree akɔ da ayaresabea, ama watoto nnwuma a ɛwɔ ahenkuro Mbabane mu a ne ɛyɛ ɔhene no dea mpo wasɛe no. 
Atuateɛ yi fa akatua bɔne, amanyɛ mu nhyɛsoɔ akɔ so mfeɛ bebree na apagya ne mu wɔ Eswatini. Nea ɛtwa toɔ koraa no yɛ mmaranim ho suani bi wuo ho. 
Berɛ a aban reka sɛ ne wuo no yɛ nkwanhyia no, nnipa a wɔreyɛ yɛkyerɛ no kyerɛ sɛ apolisifoɔ na kuu no. 
Ɔ yɛkyerɛ no ngyinasoɔ no nyinaa ara ne berɛ tenten a manfoɔ ani nnye  wɔ ahennie kakra a aka wɔ wiase mu ha. 
Ɔ hene Mswati a ɔtɔ so mmiɛnsa a ɔbɛdii adeɛ mfeɛ aduonu mmiɛnsa a atwa mu no ɔhyɛ na bu man no.
N'akyibɔfoɔ abɔ ɔhene a wadi mfeɛ aduonum mmiɛnsa yi ne ne nyere du nnum soboɔ sɛ wasetena yɛ sɔkyee na biom nso ɔreteetee manfoɔ wɔmpɛ n'asɛm. 
Nteeɛ kyerɛ mu sɛ asɛnnibea bi a ɛwɔ Morocco abu ɔbaa bi a ɔfri Italy nanso ne nkyi Morocco atɛn sɛ ɔnkɔ da afiase mfeɛ mmensa ne fa sɛ wadidi Kramosom atɛm wɔ Facebook so berɛ a ɔdii Quran twerɛ kronkron no ho fɛw. 
Papa a ɔwoo ɔbaa a wadi mfeɛ aduonu mmiɛnsa se wɔkyeree no wiemhyɛn agyinaeɛbea a ahenkuro Rabat mu berɛ ɔfirii France man mu a ɔresua adeɛ no.
Somkuo bi a ɛwɔ Marrakesh ahyɛ takrawogyam atia ɔbaa no abɔ no kwaadu ama mpaninfoɔ.
Ghana manpaninNana Akufo-Addo atu abɛdwa asi hɔ sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ nnipa mmienu a wɔbɔɔ wɔn tuo ɔyɛkyerɛ no mu no.
Nnipa nnan na wɔpiraa berɛ a manfoɔ ne banbɔ adwumayɛfoɔ de sii ani wɔ Ejura kuro mfinimfi mu.
Basabaeɛ no hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a ɔboo abranteɛ a ɔbɔ aban akyi a yɛfrɛ no Ibrahim Mohammed a n'ahotɛ din de "Macho Kaaka" nnawɔtwe awieɛ mu wɔ Ejura a ɔfaa mu hweree ne nkwa. 
Polisifoɔ kyerɛ sɛ atuatefoɔ no sisii akwan berɛ a wɔsiee no wieeɛ Benada no. 
Polisifoɔ kaa sɛ wɔde atuo, asekan ne aboɔ guu banbɔ adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔtuu wɔn sɛ wɔnkɔ hwɛ mma nneɛma ntɔ din 
Ɔ kuu atuatefoɔ no berɛ banbɔ adwumayɛfoɔ no buee gya 
Liberia nnubɔne polisifoɔ panin baako de kyɛwpa akɔma Mmarahyɛbɛdwani bi a ɔbɔɔ no soboɔ sɛ ɔdi nnubɔne ho dwa. 
Panin yi kaa wɔ nnubɔne ho ahwɛyie nhyiamu ase sɛ ɔne Mmarahyɛbɛdwani nyaa nkitahodie maa no hunuu sɛ ɔkura ntampe, kooken ne heroine wɔ ne kaa mu. 
Wammɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani yi din.
Ɔ bɔɔ soboɔ yi ho dawuro wɔ nkrataa ne intanɛt so maa nnipa aduoson mmiɛnsa mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no too nsa frɛɛ no sɛ ɔmmɛyi nsemmisa bi ano. 
Ɔ de panin yi baa Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no, ɔgye too mu sɛ ɔbɔɔ soboɔ no nanso wammɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no din maa ɔserɛɛ bɔnefakyɛ. 
Ɔ tuu asɛnnie no hyɛɛ da berɛ a wɔde mmrika faa panin yi kɔɔ ayaresabea. 
Nnubɔne nom abɛyɛ haw kɛseɛ ama Liberia man no ɔko nakyi, Asoeɛ a ɛreko tia nnubɔne nni sika a wɔde reko atia nnubɔne dwadie. 
Ethiopia Aban Panin Abiy Ahmed abu n'ani agu akofoɔ wɔkyeree wɔn Dwoada wɔ Tigrayan mantam ahenkuro Mekelle mu. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ, "Yɛhyɛɛ aseɛ twee yɛn ho firii Mekelle no nnipa bebree ho dwirii wɔn. Nanso mmerɛ sooe a yɛtwee yɛn ho no na biribi soronko biara nni mu." 
"Nea na ɛkura wɔn mu no ayera mprenpren" 
Nanso akofoɔ gu so kyerɛ mu sɛ aban asraafoɔ no boo wɔn san hyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnkɔ. 
Aban Panin abɛdiakyire Redwan Hussein dii kan sɛ asraafoɔ no bɛtumi asan agye Mekelle bio nnawɔtwe mmiɛnsa akyi.
Ɔ kaa sɛ aban wɔ sikasɛm ho ahiadeɛ di ho dwuma. 
Ɔ kaa sɛ aban asɛe dollar ɔpepepem mmienu akyiri pɔ mmienu bosome nnwɔtwe atwa mu wɔ Tigray wɔ mmoa mu. 
Ɔ ko no akɔ so ara fi Obobuo bosome mu ama ɛnam so ama nnipa mpempem awu ama mantam hɔ agyigya. 
UN aserɛ kwan a ɔde bɛwura Tigray akɔ boa manfoɔ a ahokyerɛ ne kɔm ɛreku wɔn no. 
Tebea bɔne yi nhini nyinaa ara firi Ethiopia amanbuo no. 
Fi afe 1994 mu, Ethiopia mmusuakuo ahodoɔ na adi ɔman no mantam du no so.
Mokae saa Tigray kuo no a ɛwɔ tumi no? Saa kuo yi, Tigray People's Liberation Front (TPLF) di mu na maa wɔhyɛɛ saa nhyehyɛɛeɛ yi. 
Na ɛyɛ kuo nnan nkabomkuo na dii Ethiopia man no fi afe 1991 berɛ a wɔtuu asraafoɔ aban adeɛ so. 
Wɔ saa nkabomkuo ase no, Ethiopia man no bɛgyinaaeɛ san dii yie nanso na nsɛmmisa wɔ nipa fahodie ne kabi-ma-menka bi ho.
Awieɛ no, nea nnipa nnye ho no bɛdanee ɔyɛkyerɛ maa aban sesaa nneɛma mu hwɛɛ maa wɔyii Mr Abiy sɛ Aban Panin.
Mr Abiy sesaa amanbuo mu tee kuo foforɔ (Prosperity Party) tuu Tigray aban mu mpaninfoɔ adeɛ so san bɔɔ wɔn kwaadu sɛ wadi dwirim ne wahyɛ nipa so.
Saa berɛ yi ara mu no, Mr Abiy hwɛ maa asaase ho ntɔkwa a na ɛda wɔn ne Eritrea ntam no baa awieɛ, yei maa no nyaa Nobel Peace Prize wɔ afe 2019 mu 
Saa ntotoeɛ yi maa Mr Abiy nyaa manfoɔ abasobɔdeɛ nanso ɛde ɔhaw baa wɔn a na wɔbɔ n'akyi wɔ Tigray mu. 
Tigray mpaninfoɔ nhuu Mr. Abiy nsakraeɛ yi sɛ kwan a ɔrefa so asɛe Ethiopia amanbuo nhyehyɛeɛ no na ɔde tumi no nyinaa ara aba ne nsam.
Ntɔkwa no mu yɛ kɛse wɔ Ɛbɔ bosome no mu berɛ a Tigray buu aban mmara so too wɔn nkoara mantam aba. 
Aban kɛseɛ no tuu abatoɔ no hyɛɛ da ɛnam corona virus yareɛ no nti kyerɛɛ sɛ wabu mmara so. 
Ɔ ko no mu yɛɛ den berɛ a aban no gyaee sika a na ɔde ma Tigray san twaa ayɔnkofa a na ɛda wɔn ntam wɔ Ahinime bosome mu.
Saa berɛ no Tigray mpaninfoɔ no kaa sɛ yei kyerɛ sɛ "wasuae ɔko"
Ɔ haw no payaa ne mu maa ɛwieeɛ no wɔbɔɔ Tigray akofoɔ no kwaadu sɛ wato ahyɛ asraafoɔ so awia wɔn akodeɛ
Mr Abiy kaa sɛ Tigray traa "ahoma kɔkɔɔ no."
Ɔ kaa sɛ afei ayɛ ɔhyɛ ama aban no sɛ wɔne asraafoɔ no si ani. 
Wayi Algeria Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Ayman Benabderrahmane sɛ ɔman no aban panin foforɔ berɛ a mmarahyɛbɛdwafie too aba a nnipa kakra bi pɛ na baa abɔnten bɛtooe bosome ahyaseɛ no  
Afei ɛwɔ sɛ Mr. Benabderrahmane a na ɔyɛ Sikakorabea Kɛseɛ panin no te aban foforɔ a ɛbɛhwɛ atoto Abibirem Atifi man no sikasɛm a ayɛ basaa no. 
Fango ne gyaframa ho sika a aba fam ne corona virus yareɛ no ama nsakraeɛ bɔhyɛ a Manpanin Abdelmajid Tebboune hyɛɛeɛ berɛ a ɔbɛdii adeɛ bosome du nnwɔtwe ayɛ den sɛ ɔbɛdi so.
Kramofoɔ kuo a wɔtɔɔ so mmiɛnsa wɔ abatoɔ no mu se wɔn nso bɛka aban foforɔ no ho. 
Ɛwɔ sɛ aban mu panin foforɔ a wayi no yi abisadeɛ a ɔyɛkyerɛ kuo bi a agye din a wɔfrɛ wɔn Hirak de ato n'anim sɛ ɔnyɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ amanbuo no mu. 
ɛde ɔmampanin daa Abdelaziz Bouteflika amammuo no baa awieeɛ wɔ 2019 mu.
Hirakfoɔ da so rekyerɛ sɛ obi nkɔtɔ aba no na wɔda so reyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ wɔn nkuro ahodoɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu.
Nnipa yiedie kuo ahodoɔ de ato dwa sɛ, wɔakye wɔn kuo mma bebree de wɔn akɔgyina kɔɔto anim, na wɔde bi nso agu afiase.
Namibia mampanin Hage Geingob kyerɛ sɛ ɔman no wɔ ahohiahia mu ɛsiane nnipa dodoɔ a Coronavirus aku wɔn wɔn ɔman no mu, na kɔɔ ara na ɛrekɔ soro.
ɔde n’anodisɛm reto ɔman no anim no, ɔkyerɛ sɛ Namibiafoɔ 513 na Coronavirus no aku wɔn nna dunum ntɛm ni, na nnipa a wɔawu firi Kɔtɔnima no abɔ ho mmiɛnsa.
Wei yɛ owuo adi ɔman no nya pa ara ɛsiane sɛ wɔn dodoɔ nyinaa yɛ 2.5M.
ɔde nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ regu kwan sɛ onipa ntumi mfiri kuro foforɔ so nkɔ kuro foforɔ so no, Mr Geingob de too dwa sɛ nnoɔma bɛtumi agye nsam kɔsi bosome a ɛtɔ so nwɔtwe no.
ɔmampanin no kasa wieeɛ no, ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ apɔmmuden nsɛm so, Kalumbi Shangula de too dwa sɛ, “ɔman no rebrɛ sɛ ɛbɛtena ase... Yɛreko agye wɔn ara kra.”
ɔde too dwa sɛ, ɔman no mmɔkyire mu nyinaa ayɛ ma.
ɔsoafoɔ no de kaa ho sɛ, wɔde mpa bebree reba na afei nso wɔde mfidie a ɛma nnipa mframa ma wɔhome nso bɛba.
ɔde n’asɛm reba awieeɛ no, ɔmampanin Geingob srɛɛ nnipa no sɛ wɔnni mmara a wɔde aba no so, afei nso ɔgye di sɛ ɔman no bɛfa ne ntoma afira.
Wɔde barima a wɔde no firii Netherlands baa Rwanda no akɔtɔ afiase mfeɛ du-num ɛnam nnipa a ɔkuu wɔn berɛ a na wadi mfeɛ du-nkron.
ɔredi ɛean-ɔlaude Iyamuremye asɛm no, ɔde too dwa sɛ ɔnnim 1994 Tutsis ne Hutus nnipa bɛyɛ 8000 a wɔwuiiɛ no ho hwee.
Haekɔɔto no kyerɛ sɛ Iyamuremye ka Hutufoɔ a wɔkuu nnipa a wɔte Tutsi wɔ Kigali no ho bi.
Barima a wadi mfeɛ aduana num kaa n’asɛm sɛ ne maame mpo yɛ Tutsini.
ɔtemmuafoɔ no de too dwa sɛ nka wɔbɛtumi de Iyamuremye akɔ afiase ne kwa nna nyinaa nanso ɔnyɛ saa ɛfiri na ɔyɛ abɔfra na ɔdii saa bɔne no, na afei nso ɔgyee Tutsifoɔ no bi nkwa.
Wɔkyee Iyamuremye wɔ Netherlands wɔ 2013 mu. Na ɔyɛ drɔbani wɔ Israel ne Finland ɛmbasi.
Dutɔh man no de no kɔɔ Rwanda 2016 mu.
Wɔakye Jihad nnipa a baanu sɛ wɔnim nnipa a wɔwuii wɔ Solhan basabasaeɛ a ɛwɔ Burkina Faso atifi-apueeɛ fam no ho bi. Saa awerɛhosɛm yi sii bosome a ɛtɔ so nsia ne da a ɛtɔ so nnan a nnipa 130 hweree wɔn nkwa.
Kwaadubɔfoɔ de too dwa sɛ wɔakye nnipa baanu a wɔdi mfeɛ aduonu nwɔtwe.
Wɔn baanu no nyinaa kyerɛ sɛ wɔka Mouhadine kuo a ɛkyerɛ sɛ “Nnipa nkabom” no ho a wɔsusu sɛ ɛyɛ al-Qaeda kuo no mu baako.
Wɔkyekyɛ mu akuo bebree a wɔwɔ Burkina Faso na wɔayɛ basabasaeɛ bebree wɔ Niger ne Benin.
Kwaadubɔfoɔ no kaa sɛ wɔn na wɔmaa basabasaeɛ kɔɔ so wɔ Solhan, Sebba, Boundore ne Koholoko wɔ Niger ahyeɛ so.
Kwaadubɔfoɔ no asrɛ sɛ wɔnyɛ nhwehwɛmu mfa asɛm yi ho.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ basabasaeɛ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Solhan akuraa hɔ no yɛ basabasaeɛ a ɛyɛ awerɛhosɛm pa ara asi wɔ Burkina Faso firi Oforisuo wɔ 2015 mu.
Ama nnipa bebree nnye ne sɛ bammɔkuo ahodoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu bɛtumi asi Jihadfoɔ basabasaeɛ ano wɔ ɔman no mu.
ɔmampanin Roɔh Marɔ ɔhristian Kabore de too dwa Kwasiada anwummerɛ wɔ kasafidie ne TV so sɛ, ɔhyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔde asraafoɔ dodoɔ bɛkɔ beaeɛ nsɛm yi rekɔ so no.
Engirisi asraafoɔ bɛyɛ 300 na wɔde wɔn aba Mali ɛsiane Islamic State kuo (IS) a wɔafiri Middle East aba Africa no nti.
Mfeɛ mmiɛnsa anisoadehunu a ɛsi wɔn ani a wɔto ne din Operation Newɔombe no, UN asraafoɔ bɛyɛ 15,000 a France da anim no reboa sɛ asomdwoeɛ bɛba Sahel.
Mali ka Sahel aman a wɔne Jihadfoɔ de abɔ anim no na basabasaeɛ a wɔrekɔ so nyɛ koraa.
Global Terrorism Index a ɔde baa Obubuo da a ɛtɔ so 25 kyerɛ sɛ, Islamic State kuo IS afiri Middle East aba Abibirem ne South Asia a nnipa a wɔkumm wɔ wɔn Saharan-Africa akɔ n’anim 67%.
Global Terrorism Index amannebɔ ne sɛ, “ISIS kuo ahodoɔ a aba Sub-Saharan Africa no na ama basabasaeɛ aba aman a wɔwɔ saa beaeɛ hɔ no mu.”
“Aman nson a basabasaeɛ aba mu pa ara wɔ Sub-Saharan Africa ne Burkina Faso, Mozambique, DRɔ, Mali, Niger, Cameroon ne Ethiopia”.
Amannebɔ no kyerɛ sɛ 2019 mu no, “sub-Saharan Africa na ISIS basabasaeɛ kɛseɛ no ara kɔɔ so maa nnipa 982 hweree wɔn nkwa”.
Jihadfoɔ dwumadie wɔ Abibiman no akyɛ.
Al-Qaeda kannifoɔ Osama Bin Laden de bɛtenaa Sudan ansa na ɔresan akɔ Afghanistan wɔ 1996 mu.
Nigeria Boko Haram kuo no nso a wɔakyee sukuu mmaa wɔ Chibok wɔ 2014 mu no nso nam Jihad so yɛɛ basabasaeɛ bebreee wɔ 2010 mu.
Na nnɛ deɛ, sɛdeɛ akuo ahodoɔ ne Jihad kuo de abɔm no, basabasaeɛ wɔ beaeɛ hɔ rekɔ soro.
US State Department for ɔounter-Terrorism kɔɔdinɛta, Ambassador Nathan Sales kyerɛ sɛ IS ne al-Qaeda dwumadie no afiri Syria ne Iraq akɔ West ne East Africa ne Afghanistan.
ɔkyerɛ sɛ, “Africa na abɛdi kan sɛ ɛba beaeɛ a wɔbɛsi basabasaeɛ ano a”.
Nanso, ɛnyɛ aban no ne saa basabasaeɛfoɔ nko ara na wɔde abɔm; al-Qaeda ne IS akyitaafoɔ nso de abɔm a ɛnyɛ ketewa koraa na ano ayɛ den pa ara a French Jihad nimdefoɔ, Oliver Guitta a ɔwɔ GlobalStrat Risk ɔonsultanɔy ahyɛ nkɔm sɛ:
“Mfeɛ aduonu a ɛda yɛn anim yi, Africa bɛtu Middle East, na ɛhɔ na Jihad basabasaeɛ no bɛkɔ so pa ara”.
Al-Qaeda ne IS nyinaa mpɛ wɔmpɛ akannifoɔ a wɔfrɛ wɔ “apostates” no asɛm.
Nanso sɛdeɛ wɔyɛ wɔn nnoɔma no bɔ abira.
IS basabasaeɛ a wɔyɛ no ano yɛ den pa ara.
Wei ma atuterafoɔ ne nnipabɔnefoɔ na wɔdi kuo no anim, na afei nso wɔpɛ sɛ wɔka Nkramofoɔ dodoɔ no ara nso hyɛ.
Al-Qaeda ne akuo ahodoɔ a wɔhyɛ wɔn ase botaeɛ ne kuro mma a wɔnni awerɛhyɛm biara wɔ aban no amammuo ne apolisifoɔ no mu bɛtae wɔn akyi a, na wɔgyina so deɛ wei ayɛ deɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ.
Wiase aman ahodoɔ a wɔnni sika dodoɔ no ara bɛn Sahara desert.
Wɔfrɛ saa beaeɛ yi “the Sahel”, na Arabic kasa no mu ɛkyerɛ “the ɔoast”.
Aman a wɔwɔ Sahel borɔno so ne Mali, Chad, Niger, Burkina Faso ne Mauritania, na basabasaeɛ bebree na akɔ so wɔ saa aman yi mu.
Nsukɔm, hia, kɛtɛasehyɛ ne adwuama a ɛho ayɛ den na ɛreku wɔn a wɔte borɔno hɔ.
Ambasada Sales kyerɛ sɛ, “West Africa yɛ beaeɛ a aman no nni wɔn nsaase so tumi, asraafoɔ tiatia nnipa fahodie so na wɔn ahyeɛ so nso ho bammɔ wɔ fam.”
Jihad kuo a wɔdi dwuma pa ara wɔ borɔno yi so ne ɛama’at Nusrat Al-Islam wa’l-Muslimin (ɛNIMɔ a ɛhyɛ al-Qaeda ase.
Saa kuo yi Islamic State in the Great Sahara (ISGSɔ a ɛhyɛ IS ase na wɔrepere so wɔ borɔno yi so. Afe yi deɛ, ntɔkwa pii nkɔɔ so wɔ wɔn ntam.
Nigeria abere wɔ Jihad basabasaeɛ nsa no, na aban no ntumi ma biara ntɔ n’akwan mu wɔ ɔman no atifi-apueeɛ fam. ɛhɔ na Boko Haram kuo hyɛɛ aseɛ.
Global Terrorism Index kyerɛ sɛ Boko Haram ama nnipa 37,500 na ahwere wɔn nkwan a nnipa wɔboro 19,000 na awuo wɔ Nigeria ɛfiri 2011 reba no. Na nyɛ Nigeria nko, na mmom aman a wɔne no bɔ ahyeɛ nso ka ho.
Afe 2015 mu no, Boko Haram fa bi kɔhyɛɛ IS ase a wɔbɛfrɛ wɔn ho “Islamic State West Africa Provinɔe (Iswapɔ a wɔtwa ahyeɛ a wɔmmrɛ ho kɔfa aman sɔɔso wɔ Lake Chad wɔ 2018 mu.
ɛfiri hɔ na IS rebɔ n’akuo no fa a ɛwɔ Abibiman mu kyidɔm.
Basabasaeɛ rekɔ so wɔ Boko Haram din mu. Ekuo bi de mfonini bi baa abɔntene ɔpɛnimaa da a ɛdi kan a a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn na wɔkumm akuafoɔ bebree wɔ Borno State. Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔne aban asraafoɔ na ɛdii saa dwuma no.
Asraafoɔ ne infomɛhyin kakra bi na aman wɔwɔ Europe de aboa Nigeria. Wɔkyerɛ sɛ kɛtɛasehyɛ ne nnipa yiedie a Nigeria asraafoɔ no tiatia so nti na wɔntumi mmoa Nigeria sɛdeɛ ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ.
Wei nyinaa ka ho bi na wɔnnye aban no nnie na nnipa dodoɔ no ara de wɔn ho kɔdɔm Boko Haram ne Jihad akuo ahodoɔ wɔ borɔno no so.
Oliver Guitta se, “Kɛtɛasehyɛ a ɛwɔ Nigeria na resɛe biribiara.”
Al-Qaeda basabasaeɛ no hyɛɛ aseɛ wɔ Algeria.
Nti ɛnyɛ nwanwa sɛ kannifoɔ foforɔ a Al-Qaeda wɔ Islamic Magreb (AQIMɔ firi Algeria.
Abu Obaida Al-Annabi abɛhyɛ Adbelmalik Droukdel a France asraafoɔ kumm no wɔ Mali wɔ bosome a ɛtɔ so nsia mu no anan.
Al-Qaeda akyitaafoɔ ani agye sɛ wɔayi no sɛ kannifoɔ, ɛnna IS akyitaafoɔ nso sɛ wɔnnye ne Jihad ho abɔdin ntom.
Tunisia a ɛyɛ ɔman a ɛso wɔ borɔno no so de nnipa dodoɔ pa ara (15 kɔsi 20,000ɔ a wɔn ankasa kɔɔ Syria de wɔn ho kɔdɔm IS kuo firi 2013 kɔsi 2018.
Basabasaeɛ pii na ɛrekɔ wɔ Tunisia.
Basabasaeɛ pii na ɛrekɔ so wɔ Libya firi berɛ a Arab Spring Revolt tuu Muammar Gaddafi adeɛ so.
N’amammuo no baeɛ awieeɛ ma ho kwan mma atuo ne topaeɛ bebree firi aban no akakye kɔɔ Sahel aman so. Wei maa IS Jihadfoɔ no ho yɛɛ den wɔ Libya apueeɛ fam.
Somalia kuo al-Shabab kuo a ɛkyerɛ “mmabunu” wɔ Arab kasa no mu no yɛ Jihad kuo baako a wɔwɔ ho yɛ hu wɔ Abibirem.
Nathan Sales kyerɛ sɛ, “Al-Shabab kuo no hunu ne ho sɛ ɛyɛ al-Qaeda kuo a wɔn mmɔdemmɔ wɔ soro pa ara.”
Aman ahodoɔ bebree na wɔapɛ sɛ wɔbɛtu wɔn ase nanso nyɛ Al-Shababfoɔ atumi aduru Kenya ne Uganda, na wɔsan ato topaeɛ wɔ Somali ahenkuro Mogadishu mu.
US Speɔial Operations topaeɛ a wɔto firii Dɛibouti kumm al-Shabab akannifoɔ nyinaa nso ekuo no atumi asɔre bio.
Wɔatumi nso adi kuo a ɛhyɛ IS aseɛ a siesie wɔkɔhyɛ Horn of Africa atifi-apueeɛ fam.
IS nyaa wɔnyaa atifi mansini mu wɔ ɔapo Delgado yɛ basabasaeɛ ho nhwɛsoɔ baako a wɔhyehyɛɛ biribiara wɔ intɛnɛt so.
Aban no mu nnipa kyerɛ sɛ Jihadfoɔ a wɔredi dwuma wɔ Mozambique no faa intɛnɛt no so na wɔfaa nnipa firii Tanzania a IS foɔ wɔwɔ Syria ne Irag ankasa amma hɔ.
Amannebɔ pii na ɛbɔ abira wɔ basabasaeɛ a ɛsiiɛ wɔ ɔabo Delgado wɔ IS din mu a nnipa aduonum firii wɔn nkwa wɔ agopramma so.
Nanso IS kuo no nsa da aban no so.
Oliver Guitta se, “IS nam Mozambique mu a asraafoɔ ntumi nyɛ wɔn hwee”.
Wei bɛma basabasaeɛ aba.
G7 nhyiamu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Loɔh Erne bosome a ɛtɔ so nsia no mu wɔ 2013 mu no, G7 sae kɔntraagyi sɛ wɔntua sika a basabasaeɛ kuo ahodoɔ no repɛ no.
Mfeɛ nson baeɛ no, wɔtua sika a wɔnnim ano kɔgye Europe adehyeɛ. Britain ne AmErica mmaa na wɔtae ku wɔn.
Jihadfoɔ yi agyae French adehyɛ bebree a wɔwɔ Sahel. Wɔgyae wɔn sɛdeɛ wɔn nso yi Jihad atuterafoɔ a wɔwɔ afiase wɔ Mali no.
Mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmufoɔ kyerɛ sɛ sika a wɔatua ma Jihadfoɔ a wɔwɔ North ne West Africa a wɔkyekye nkorɔfoɔ bɛboro €100 m ($120m; £90mɔ.
Jihadfoɔ yi de saa sika yi tɔ atuo bebree, atopaeɛ, kaa papa, nhwɛniwa, tetefon na afei nso wɔde fa afoforɔ ma wɔbɛka kuo no ho. Wɔde saa sika yi ara nso mu bi ma aban mu nnipa.
Atowerɛkyɛm a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ nsɔre mu wɔ Burkina Faso no nso bɛyɛ Jihadfoɔ nsa ano adwuma. ɛmfa ho sɛ asraafoɔ pɛ sɛ wɔtu wɔn ase no, Jihadfoɔ yi dwumadie kɔɔ ara na ɛrekɔ soro wɔ borɔno no mu.
ɔman no amannɔe soafoɔ kyerɛ sɛ wɔbɛtu basabasaeɛ yi ase abɛyɛ ɔko a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔko gye Sahel borɔno no nkwa a Burkina Faso, Chad, Mali, Mauritania ne Niger ka ho.
Bosome kakra yi, Jihad asraafoɔ yi ama nnipa 100,000 na adwane afiri wɔn afie mu wɔ Burkina Faso.
Bosome a ɛtwaam no, basabasaeɛ bɛyɛ nnum na akɔ Akristofoɔ so, na wei dodoɔ no ara kɔ so berɛ a wɔreyɛ asɔre. Ekuo biara nkaa sɛ wɔn na wɔdii saa dwuma no nso wɔsusu wɔn a wɔyɛɛ saa no yɛ Jihadfoɔ.
Dɛallil Lounnas a ɛyɛ ɔbenfoɔ wɔ asraafoɔ nsɛm wɔ Al Akhawayn University a ɛwɔ Moroɔɔo kaa sɛ, “wei kyerɛ sɛ wɔasesa sɛdeɛ wɔyɛ wɔn nnoɔma mu”.
ɔse, “Firi mmerɛ a Jihadfoɔ hyɛɛ wɔn basabasaeɛ ase wɔ mpɔtam ha no, mpɛn pii no wɔmfa wɔn asɛm nkɔ ɔsom kumaa no so, nkanka ne Akristofoɔ.”
Wei ama Burkina Faso abakɔsɛm sɛ wɔfoaa ɔsom biara so no resɛe na wei yɛ Jihadfoɔ no kwan a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔfa so ma ntawantawa bɛtɔ asom ahodoɔ ntam ne borɔno borɔno ntam.
Louis Audet-Gosselin a ɛwɔ ɔanadian Network for Researɔh Terrorism se, “ɛyɛ kwan a atwam a basabasaeɛfoɔ no pɛ sɛ wɔkenyan basabasaeɛ kɛseɛ wɔ ɔman no mu.”
Basabasaeɛ ne ntɔkwa nso yɛ akwan a ɛma Jihadfoɔ yi kwa ma wɔnya nkorabata wɔ beaeɛ bi na wɔdi beaeɛ no so.
Owura Audet-Gosselin de too dwa sɛ, “Mmammɔsɛm rekɔ fam dabiara wɔ ɔman no mu. Jihad akuo yi regyina brane nkakrankakra a ɛrema aban no ne ɔman no tumi rekɔ fam wɔ nkuraseɛ ne kuropɔn mu.”
Wɔn a wɔde wɔn ani asi wɔn so no ne ɔman no wɔ twaka ti sɛ afotufoɔ a wɔwɔ nkuraaseɛ, mɛyɔs, apolisifoɔ, aban nnwumayɛfoɔ ne kuro mma a wɔne asraafoɔ redi dwuma.
Sukuu ne akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yɛ dɔm ketewa a Jihadfoɔ a wɔmpɛ wiase mu nwomasua yi tumi de wɔn ani si wɔn so. Sukuu ahodoɔ a ɛboro 1,000 a wɔ atifi na wɔahyɛ wɔn ama wɔatom a, ama mmɔfra mmɔfra 150,000 na wɔnkɔ sukuu.
Human Rights Watɔh nso bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ aban asraafoɔ nso bu nnipa yiedie so berɛ wɔretu atuterafoɔ yi nnwuma ase. ɛbi ne Fulanifoɔ a wɔn mmu dodoɔ no ara Nkramofoɔ a wɔkuu wɔn no.
Owura Audet-Gosselin se, “Asraafoɔ no tirim yɛ den na wɔde wɔn ani asi Fulafoɔ mpɔtam no so a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Fulanifoɔ no di fo wɔne Jihadfoɔ yi wɔ twaka ... wei nso ma Fulanifoɔ mmabunu nso fa atuo.”
Wɔahyɛ ɔman no sɛ wɔnhwɛ na wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri nsuoyiri a ɛyɛ a ɔnante anaa ɔtwi lɔɔre fa mu no ho
ɛtɔ da a, nsuo a ayiri ɛyɛ a na ɛyɛ yɛn adwene sɛ yɛabɛtumi adware afa mu nanso no anoden no bɛtumi de yɛn akɔ sɛ yɛyɛ yɛn adwene sɛ yɛredware afa mu a
Mr. Richard Amo-Yartey a ɔyɛ nhwehwɛnim hwɛsofoɔ wɔ National Disaster Management (NADMO), atenae kɛseɛ no mu no de too Ghana News Agency berɛ a na ɔne no retwetwe nkɔmmɔ no sɛ, ɔhyɛ sɛ anka adrɔbafoɔ bɛgyae nsuoyiri mu fa. Lɔɔre bebree na nsuo de wɔn kɔ ɛnam sɛ adrɔbafoɔ dwene sɛ nsuo no ano nyɛ den nanso wɔbɛhuno ara na ɛde wɔn kɔ
ɔkaa sɛ mpo no ɛbia na obi bɛtumi adware atwa deɛ nanso no ɛtɔ da a na nneɛma pii bi te sɛ agyanan, nyarewa ne mmoa ahodoɔ a wɔtumi pira nnipa nso nam mu
Mr. Amo-Yartey kaa sɛ, ɛho bɛhia sɛ wobɛnya aboterɛ atwɛn akɔsi sɛ nsuo no bɛtwe ansa na woakɔ sene sɛ wobɛkɔ akɔhyia atoyerɛnkyem bi
ɔsan nso hyɛɛ wɔn a wɔtete mmeaɛ a nsuo tumi yiri no sɛ, wɔntu nkɔ mmeaɛ a ɛhɔ yɛ na wɔnkɔte sɛdeɛ wɔnkɔ nsuoyiri ahohiahia mu
Mr. Amo-Yartey kae ɔmanfoɔ san nso kae ɔmanfoɔ sɛ, aberɛ a aban no gu so reyere ne ho apere ɔmanfoɔ yiedie no, wɔn ankasa nso nnwene wɔn atenayie ho
Nsuo no ne yɛn na ɛwɔ ha
ɔka kaa ho sɛ, nnipa nna wɔn ho so, na wɔnyɛ ahwɛyie wɔ saa wiemsakrae yi ho
Mr. Amo Yartey see NADMO rekyerɛkyerɛ nkurow ahodoɔ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so atwe wɔn ho afiri nsuoyiri mu haw ho ɛnnɛ nsunsuansoɔ a nsutɔ berɛ no de ba
ɔhyɛɛ nnipa no sɛ, sɛ wɔrekɔ ahohiahia mu a wɔnfrɛ NADMO wɔ saa namba yi 112 ne 0299350030 so
Mmom no, Ghana wiem nsakrae adwumakuo no ahyɛ ɔmanfoɔ sɛ wɔkenkan wiem nsakrae ho nsɛm wɔ wɔn ntentan fidie no so daa ne nnawɔtwe biara na wɔnhu sɛdeɛ wɔbɛtoto wɔn nneɛma
Nsuo bi a, ɛtɔɔ dunhwere nan Kwasiada yi a ɛtwamm no de nsuyiri baa Ghana anaafoɔ fa mu a Kasoa, Weiɛa, Adenta ne mmeaeɛ mmeaeɛ bi
Na ɛsɛ sɛ nnipa pii no ara twɛn dunhwere pii ansa na wɔatumi asan akɔ wɔn afiefie mu ɛnam nsuyiri no nti
Nkurow bebree no a, ɛwɔ Nanumba South mansin a ɛwɔ Atifi mantam no mu no gu so berɛ wɔ nsuoyiri ho ɛnam sɛe a ɛsɛe ɔmanfoɔ fie ne wɔn mfudeɛ
Nnipa pii no ara ɔte Asuo Oti ho no gu so redi abooboo ɛnam nsu brane a ɛtɔɔ Kwasiada, Ahinime 11, 2020 no a ɛyiri faa nkurow bebree no
ɛkwan no nyinaa asi a, ɛmma ɔmanfoɔ ntumi nkɔ wɔn mansin ahenkurow no mu nkɔtɔ deɛ wɔpɛ
Saa nkurow yi ne Chichagi, Lahato, Egambo, Mualaa, a ne nyinaa wɔ Nanumba South Mansin no mu.
Adan abubu, mfuo ne atwe nsuo abubu
Nnipa no sɛ wɔnni baabi a wɔde wɔn ti reto nti no mpaninfoɔ mmra mmɛyɛ wɔn mmoa
Wɔn nneɛma nyinaa nsuo no de kɔ
Deɛ wɔbɛdi mpo yɛ asɛm
Nnipa no mu baako kaa sɛ, yɛhia aban no mmoa. Me nneɛma nyinaa kɔ
M’agyapadeɛ nyinaa kɔ
Deɛ aka nyinaa ne ataadeɛ a ɛhyɛ me yi
Baako nso kaa sɛ, yɛn adan nyinaa abubu, nti meresrɛ aban no sɛ ɔmmɛsi mma yɛn
Mansin no National Disaster Management Organisation (NADMO) panin no, Yaw Kojo Kumah Edward de too dwa pɛɛ mmoa maa wɔn a wɔn ho aka no
Adan bebree no ara abubu nti no yɛntumi nhu saa mmeaɛ yi yie
Yɛahu nnipa 157, yɛgu so rehwehwɛ wɔn a aka no
Yɛresrɛ aban no, somkuo ahodoɔ ne akorɛankorɛ nnwuma no sɛ wɔmmɛyɛ yɛn mmoa
Saa nkurɔfoɔ yi nni obibiara a wɔde wɔn ani bɛto wɔn so
Wɔn yiedie nyinaa gyina wɔn mfuo so, na nnɛ yi a nsuo afa wɔn mfuo yi deɛ wɔnni obiara a ɔbɛma wɔn biribi adie
Mansin soafoɔ a ɔwɔ West Mamprusi a ɛwɔ North East mantam no mu no, Aremeyaw Somo Luɔky, kaa sɛ sika a ɛyɛ GHS100,000 a ɔmanpanin abadiakyire de baa, Dr. Mahamudu Bawumia de baa sɛ wɔmfa mmoa wɔn a wɔnho kae no, wɔde ama wɔn
Dr. Bawumia de sika yi bae sɛ, aban no bɛboa ama wɔasan asisi adan no ama wɔn a wɔn ho aka no
Nsuo faa saa nkurase yi nyinaa ɛnam nsuo a ano yɛ den na ɛtumi maa nsuo no bu faa n’ano no so bɛfaa saa nkurase yi nyinaa
Saa nsuoyiri yi a ɛfaa mfuo bebree ne ayɛmmoa yi nyinaa na ɛnam so ama Dr. Bawumia de sika yi aba sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ na wɔn a wɔn ho aka no bɛnya nhane kakra
Eric Nana Agyemang-Prempeh, a ɔda ɔman no National Disaster Management Organization (NADMO) no ano no akyerɛ sɛ, saa bue a wɔbue Bagre Dam a ɛwɔ Burkina Faso no na ɛde saa nsuyiri yi ba Nkran mmeaeɛ baabi
Nsuo a ɛtoɔ nnawɔtwe yi awie no maa Nkran baabi te sɛ Weiɛa ne nkura a ɛbɛn no no nyinaa yirii yɛ, a na ama akɔneaba die ho ayɛ den
Kanee no na nsuo a, ɛfiri Bagre Dam no mu ba no ba gaalɔn ɔpepem 4-8 miniti baako biara nanso ɛnnɛ yi no ɛba ɔpepem 29 miniti baako biara a ama Ghana nsuwa no nyinaa ayɛ ma nti nsuo tɔɔ kakra bi no ara na kyerɛ sɛ nsuo reyiri afa yɛn nyinaa
NADMO paninyi kaa eyi berɛ a ɔkɔɔ mmeaeɛ binom a nsuo ayiri afa wɔ Nkran mantan no mu no
Deɛ NADMO rekyerɛ ne sɛ, afe yi no ɔne mansin asɛmbili ahodoɔ no aka abɔ mu sɛ, wɔnyi mɔnkye mɔnka pii mfa nhwɛ nsuo no anim nanso nsuo no ntumi nkora nsuo a ɛfiri Bagre dam no mu reba no
Mr Agyemang Prempeh tuu wɔn a wɔtu nwura gu agatase a adi kan ayɛ ma no mu sɛ wɔnnyae, ɛnam sɛ ɛka deɛ ɛde nsuyiri ba no ho
Nkran mantam NADMO panyin, Archibold Cobbina, mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Weiɛa-Gbawe, Tina Naa Ayeley Mensah ne mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Bortianor Ngleshie Amanfrom, Sylvester Tetteh kɔsraa wɔn ɔmanfoɔ a wɔwɔ saa nsuoyiri mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ yi
Wɔne wɔn dii wɔn abene, na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔde nneɛma kakra bɛba abɛboa wɔn
Mansin soafoɔ a ɔwɔ Mamprusi Atɔeɛ Asɛmbili no a Atifi Apueɛ mantam no mu no, Isshaku Aremeyaw Somo, kaa sɛ otumi dwanee akorɔmfo werɛmfoɔ bi Ahinime da a ɛtɔ so12, 2020 no
Eyi sii yɛ berɛ a na ɔsoafoɔ yi ɔnam de sika kɔma wɔn a atoyerɛnkyem ato wɔn wɔ nsuyiri no mu
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ Eyewitness News so no, Mr. Somo de too dwa sɛ, ɔtumi dwanee ɛnam sɛ banbɔfoɔ tumi duu hɔ berɛ ano na ɔtotoo atuo maa akorɔmfoɔ yi dwanee yɛ
Deɛ ɛboa yɛ ne sɛ, apolisifoɔ tumi baa hɔ, na ɔbɔɔ motokafoɔ bi nan mu
Na me ne ahemfo no wɔ hɔ a merekyɛ sika no na wɔde no bae
Na wɔde no de mmirika kɔɔ ayaresabea
Menyaa nteɛ, nti ɛhɔ no ara na ɛsɛ sɛ medwane kɔ Walewale
Saa kwan no so no akorɔmfoɔ wɔ hɔ pa ara nti no, yɛde banbɔfoɔ pii no ara akɔgu hɔ nti no aboa rete korɔno bɔ no so nkakrankakra
Nansa yi ara no apolisifoɔ nyaa akwanhia bi wɔ hɔ nti ama wɔato wɔn bo ase kakra ɛno na ama akorɔmfoɔ yi refa ho di bɔnefo sɛm yi no
Nanso wɔn ti anni ammoa wɔn
Yawda, Ahinime 1, 2020 no nsuo faa nkurase nan a ɛyɛ Gaagbini, Dimia Tinkaya ne Banawa ɛnam nsuden a ɛtɔɔ yɛ na dam mmiɛnsa bueɛ maa ɛbɛfaa saa nkura yi
Aban no ama mansin soafoɔ no Ghana sika 100,000 sɛ ɔmfa mmoa wɔn a nsuo no faa wɔn no
Mr. Somo se, ɔsusu sɛ, akorɔmfoɔ no baa ne so ɛnam sika a na ɔkura no nti
Mesusu sɛ ɔbaa sɛ ɔbɛgye GHS 100,000 no na ɛfiri hɔ no daa me ne apolisifoɔ na ɛnam
ɛno no no, mensuro sɛ merekyɛ sika no a
Ghana nsuo adwumakuo no nso ahyɛ aseɛ retwe nsuo firi Weiɛa dam no mu
Eyi firi nsubrane a, ɛtɔɔ wɔ Asuo Densu mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ no
ɛhyɛɛ nsuo twe no ase Kwasiada, Ahinime 11, 2020
Weiɛa dam no nsusui beae no yɛ anamɔn 47, nanso no nsubrane no de n’anamɔn no firii 46.8 de kɔɔ 48.4 a dunhwere aduonu nan mpo amma a ɛno maa GWCL de amirika kɔhyɛɛ nsuo no twe no ase.
Wɔaka akyerɛ NADMOfoɔ, banbɔkuofoɔ, Bureau of National Investigation (BNIɔ ahemfoɔ, Mansin aseɛmbili, wɔn a wɔka bi a, ɛyɛ yie ne ɔmanfoɔ nyinaa a wɔbɛn nsuo no ho sɛ, wɔntu ntɛm pa ara sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a ɔhaw biara a nsuo no de bɛba no ɛnka wɔn
Saa nkurow yi a wɔn ho aka yi ne Tetegu, Oblogo, Pambros Salt, Lower McCarthy Hill, Lower Weija, Bojo Beach, Ada Kopey ne nkurow binom a atwa wɔn ho ahyia.
Adwumakuo no rehwɛ anim sɛ nsuo pii bɛtɔ ɛno nti no, NADMOfoɔ reyɛ ntotoeɛ ama wɔde nsuo akɔma wɔn a nsuyiri no ama wɔn afiri beaɛ a wɔwɔ no
Wɔn a wɔte Weiɛa no ɛsɛ sɛ wɔte nsuoyiri no ase ɛnam nsuo ahodoɔ a atɔ nnaawɔtwe yi a etwaa mu no awie no
Wɔresrɛ sɛ anka wɔbɛnya agatɛse a etumi fa nsuo bebree sene deɛ ɛma nsuo no kɔ kɛkɛ no
Wɔn a nsuoyiri yi kaa wɔn no wɔ West Mamprusi mansin no mu no gu so resu pɛ mmoa ɛnam sɛ wɔnni baabi te
ɛfiri da a saa nsubrane yi a ɛtɔe Yawoada yi a aban no de GHS 100,000 ne nneɛma kakra ba bɛtee yɛn haw so wɔ West Mamprusi mansin mu ha no afei na yɛrebɛte mmoa foforo bi bio
Berɛ a wɔne Citi News rekasa no nnipa a wɔne baabi te no kasa faa aduane a na anka wɔse asɛmbili no de bɛbrɛ wɔn no mma
Aberɛ a nnipa baako a ɔka wɔn a wɔn ho aka no ho rekasa no ɔkyerɛɛ deɛ wɔrefa mu wɔ sukuu adan ahodoɔ a wɔada mu nna mmiɛnsa yi a atwam no
Yɛama yɛn sukuu adan abien pɛ sɛ yɛnna mu
Nanso yɛ dodoɔ yɛ ahaasa, ɛnam saa nti no yɛagya adan no ama mmaa no ne mmoɔfra no sɛ wɔnna mu na yɛn deɛ yɛbɛda abɔntene. Aduane a wɔde brɛ yɛn no sua, wɔde aduɔson nson pɛ na ɛba berɛ a yɛn dodow no rekeka kɔ ahaasa
Mansin soafoɔ no maa yɛbaa ha sɛ ɛnkyɛ yɛbɛ te no nka
Aduane a wɔde ma yɛn no soa
Nanso wɔse wɔabrɛ yɛn aduane, nanso yɛnhu so nsunsuansoɔ. Yɛnni biribi biara a yɛn ani da so
Saa sika no a wɔse aban no na ɛde ama yɛn no wɔmfa mmaa yɛn, mansin soafoɔ no ne onipa a ɔregyina NPP amanyɔkuo no de sika no kɔ Walewale, yɛntee wɔn nka bio
ɔmanpanin abediakyire atwa ne Nkran mantan nsrabɔ no so rekɔ akɔhwɛ wɔn a wɔn ho aka no
Berɛ a ɔdue no, ɔmaa wɔn GHS 100,000 sɛ wɔmfa ntɔ nnuane
Gaagbini, Dimia, Tinkaya ne Banawa ne nkurow a wɔn ho aka pa ara
Yawoadano, nsuo faa nkurase binom ɛnam nsuden a ɛtɔɔ yɛ na dam mmiɛnsa bueɛ maa ɛbɛfaa saa nkura yi ase.
ɛfaa mfuao ekase pii ne ayɛmmoa binom nso kɔe
Wɔakye nantwie hwɛsofoɔ bi wɔ Tamale a ɛwɔ Atifi mantam no sɛ wɔdaadaa Tamale polisi paninChief Superintendent, Iddrisu Tanko Issifu.
ɛnam sɛ, polisi paninyi Chief Superintendent, Iddrisu Tanko Issifu yɛɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔyɛn nantwie nti no, wɔne saa anantwie hwɛsofoɔ, Osman Mumuni and Seidu Braimah yi kɔɔ apam na wɔhyɛɛ no sɛ wɔbɛma no anantwie.
Nsɛnkae a apolisifoɔ de baa abɔntene ne sɛ, saa anantwie hwɛsofoɔ yi dii kan hyɛɛ no sɛ wɔbɛbrɛ no anantwie aduonum ne mmiɛnsa na wɔgyee Ghana sika no 36,000.00.
ɛnna saa nnipa yi ne no yɛɛ apam sɛ wɔbɛto ne Toyota Sɔion a ne namba yɛ GW 7-Z no ama no anantwie aduanan
Wɔsan faa Chief Superintendent Tanko Issifu Land ɔruiser Prado a ne namba yɛ GS 5939 a na wɔse wɔbɛma no anantwie ahaasa
Apolisifoɔ nsɛnkae no mu no, mansin no polisi paninno tee aseɛ na wɔsan maa wɔn GHS 56,000 sɛ ɔde bɛto anantwie no aduason aka ho
Nsɛnkae no kyerɛ sɛ na ɛsɛ sɛ saa nnipa yi hwɛ anantwie a wɔbɛyɛ 556 no
ɛyɛɛ no, sɛ polisi paninyi bisa anantwie no asɛm biara a, na wɔredaadaa no
Nsɛnkae no kyerɛɛ sɛ, berɛ a ɔpɛɛ sɛ wɔkɔhwɛ anantwie no wɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ anantwie wɔn dodoɔ bɛyɛ 556 ne anantwie mma 40 no rekɔdidi wɔ baabi a wɔnnim beaeɛ ko
ɔkɔɔ beaeɛ a saa nnipa yi te yi sɛ ɔkɔhwɛ n’anantwie a nantwie biara nni hɔ, na wanhu nipa biara nso wɔ hɔ.
Nsɛnkae no kyerɛ sɛ, polisi paninyi ma wɔkyeree nnipa yi mu baako a wɔgu so hwehwɛ baako, Seidu Braimah a ɔno deɛ ɔredwane no
Regional Coordinating Director a ɔwɔ Ahafo mantam no mu atu, Ebenezer Amoah, atu mmabunu a ɔwɔ mantam no mu no sɛ mma wɔn mfɛre sɛ ɔbɛyɛ nsaa no dwuma na nyinaa nso yɛ ɔkwan a yɛfa so de pɛ biribi de didi
Mmabunu kuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ mantam no mu no hyia Wukuada, Ayɛhumɔmmɔ 30 hyia mpaninfoɔ a ɔda mantam no ano de mpontuo mu haw bi kɔdann wɔn
Kurontihene a, wɔwɔ ntotroso ne ne mpɔtam, Nana Akofo Amankonah I, rekasa afa mpontuo mu haw ahodoɔ no ho no, ɔsan hyɛɛ mmabunu no sɛ, ɔnhwɛ na wɔntu abrabɔ mu anammɔn a ɛbɛboa wɔn ama wɔatumi adu deɛ ɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ho na wɔanya dwa
Sɛ woyɛ ɔdepamfoɔ a, wonbɛtumi asua sɛdeɛ yɛyɛ bɔsa nko ara, te sɛdeɛ vulganisas. Baako sua sɛdeɛ yɛyɛ atikulata tae nko ara no na obi nso asua sɛdeɛ yɛ lɔɔre nketewa tae nko ara no
ɔman mu no nyinaa mmabunu kuo no, National Youth Authority (NYAɔ ne ActionAid kuo no ka bom aberɛ biara yɛ dwuma soronko ma mmabunu a wɔwɔ mantam no mu no de boa wɔn wɔ nneɛma ahodoɔ a ehinta mmabunu mpontuo
ActionAid nam ne mfeɛ mmiɛnsa dwumadie a wato ne din Promoting Employment Opportunities for Young people in Ghana (PEOY) a ɔde reboa mmabunu ama wɔanya adwuma mu kwan na ama wɔn anya nimdeɛ ahodoɔ a wɔbɛfa so de ayɛ wɔn abrabɔ ho ntotoeɛ ne wɔn daakye ho dwumadie
Saa dwumadie yi bɛboa ama mmabunu no bi anya kwan ne wɔn a wɔanya PEOY ho mfasoɔ, wɔn a wɔwɔ mmabunu mmarahyɛbadwano, Mmaa Mmabunu kuo no ne wɔn adi nkɔmmɔ na aboa ama wɔate nneɛma binom ase na wɔatumi atoto wɔn nneɛma yiye
Nneɛma titiriw binom a wɔdwenedwene ho no ne, mmabunu a wɔnnya adwuma nnyɛ, nnubɔnenom, mperewa nyinsɛn ne akwanfo a wɔwɔ
Asɛm a KPMG de bɛtoo dwa ne sɛ, Ghana wɔ akwanya pii no ne amenamutu adwuma no mu, ne titiriw sikafuturo. Nokorɛ a ɛwɔ mu ne sɛ, Ghana sikakɔkɔɔ no nko ara yɛ ɔman no GDP no ahamu nkyekyɛmu fa (Ministry of Land and Natural Resources (MLNR), 2003).
Ghana nso na ɔtɔ so mmienu sɛ yɛpɛ ɔman a yɛtu sikakɔkɔɔ wɔ mu pa ara na yɛ yi South Africa firi hɔ a
Agudeɛ bio a yɛwɔ no bi nso ne fangoo, dɛnkyɛmbour, bauxite, maganesiɔm
Agudietuo abɛyɛ adwuma a nnipa ani aba ho pa ara wɔ baabiara
Akyinegye ahodoɔ a ɛrekɔ so nyinaa fa agudietuo ho, ɛnam boa a ɛboa ɛkonomi no
Mfeɛ du a atwam yi no, Ghana agudietuo no ne titiriw amenamutu nketewa adwuma anim asɛe ɛnam ɔhaw a ɔde rebrɛ ɔman no mpontuo nti
Amenamutu nketewa adwuma a ɛwɔ Ghana no, dodoɔ no ara frɛ no galasey ɛnam agudie tiriw a wɔtu a ɛno ne sikakɔkɔɔ ne dɛnkyɛnbour no. Saa galamsey yi yɛ ɔkwan a nnipa fa so tu agudie a wɔde wɔn ankasa ahoɔden tu na ɛnya nsunsuansoɔ bɔne wɔ wɔn nnipadua so ne asaase no nso so.
Ghana man no mu no, deɛ yɛahu ne sɛ, nnipa bɛyɛ ɔpepem mmiɛnsa na wɔde wɔn ho agye saa adwuma yi mu a emu bɛyɛ 170,000 deɛ wɔyɛ bi wɔnnam mmara kwan so na ɛno nso na wɔyɛ de didie
Saa asɛm galmsey yi yɛ ɔmamfoɔ no ara kasa a wɔfa firii pɔtɔ kasa mu a ɛyɛ gather ne sell a ɛkyerɛ wɔn adwuma a wɔreyɛ no mu
Saa adwuma yi yɛ kwantia a Ghanafoɔ nam so nya sika pa ara ne titiriw ne mmabunu a wɔde wɔn ho ayɛ saa adwuma yi mu no
Saa galamsey yi yɛ ɔkwan baako a ɔmanfoɔ nam so de tu hia firi wɔn ho wɔn ho mu na mmom no ɛyɛ nneɛma mmienu, ɛde ohia ba yɛn apomuden mu, nyarewa, akwanhyia ne nimdeɛ a yɛnni mfa ɔkwan papa a yɛbɛtumi afa so atu saa agudie yi
Nansa yi ara mu no, ɛbɛtɔɔ dwa sɛ nnipa binom ahwere wɔn nkwa ɛnam sɛ amena no buguu wɔn so nti
Wukuada, Obubuo 11, 28, ahwea bu guu nnipa a wɔsusu sɛ wɔbɛyɛ 30 so wɔ Dopoase Wassa Amenfi East mansin a ɛwɔ Atɔe mantam no mu no.
Bio nso no saa, atoyerɛnkyɛm yi bi san sii wɔ Dunkwa-On-Offin so 2010 wɔ Mfinimfini mantam no mu berɛ a amenamutufoɔ binom ahwea bu guu wɔn so wɔ Asuo Offin ho maa emu bɛyɛ 100 wui. Saa nneɛma yi a, ɛsisi no nyɛ adeɛ a yɛde hyɛ obi na mmom no ɔmanfoɔ no ara na ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde soboɔ no bɔ wɔn
Deɛ yɛahunu ne sɛ, wɔyɛ saa adwuma yi wɔ esum ne kwae mu, mfuo, nsuo ano, abepɔ so ne mmeaɛ huhuuhu ne titiri Chinesefoɔ
