ɛwom sɛ ebia na ngudeɛ asoeɛ no antumi deɛ, nanso wɔn nimdeɛ ne ntease a wɔwɔ fa amenamutu adwuma no ho no bɛboa ama wɔatumi asi agyinatukuo no anan mu.
Sɛ wɔgu agyinatukuo no a, ɛsɛ sɛ nneɛma bi te sɛ Galamstop, durones ne lɔɔre ahodoɔ no nyinaa wɔde ma ngudeɛ asoeɛ no na etumi wɔn ma wɔyɛ wɔn adwuma.
mmarahyɛbɛdwani a ɔwɔ Temale atifi, Alhassan Suhuyini ahyɛ ɔmanpanin sɛ ɔmfa nneɛma ahodoɔ a wɔgye afiri amenamutufoɔ no hɔ nyinaa mmɛto dwa.
Kuo ahodoɔ binom adi kan ahyɛ aban sɛ ɔmfa ɔko a ɔreko atia galamsey nhyehyɛe no nyina mmɛto gua. National Democratic Congress (NDCɔ amanyɔkuo no nso kyerɛ aban no nna mfidie a wɔde tutu fam a wɔgye no nyinaa adi nkyerɛ ɔmanfoɔ
Benada no, berɛ a Alhassan Suhuyini suree sɛ ɔrekasa wɔ mmarahyɛbadwamu no, ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ ɔmanpanin a wɔayɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔde ne manpanyindie no bɛko atia galamsey adwuma no, anka ɔmanpanin bɛma Ghanafoɔ nyinaa ahunu nneɛma ahodoɔ a wagyeɛ, ɛyɛ lɔɔre, akodeɛ, ne sikafuturo ahodoɔ nyinaa a wɔn a wɔyii wɔn sɛ wɔnkɔko no agyeɛ sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ na yɛbɛhu baabi a emu biara wɔ.
ɔsan hyɛɛ mmarahyɛbadwa no sɛ anka ɛbɛyɛ a ɔmma wɔn nhunu sika bɔtene a wɔde hyɛɛ galamsei ko no mu, na ɛno na ɛbɛma wɔhunu sɛ, ampa wɔde ayɛ deɛ wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ no a.
mmarahyɛbɛdwani panyin, ɛyɛ ɔko yi a yɛreko tia galamsey yi, anka ɛbɛyɛ a, mesusu sɛ anka mmarahyɛbadwa no bɛhwɛ na ɔde n’ani adi sika a ɔde reko ɔko yi akyi na watumi ahwɛ ampa sɛ deɛ wɔkaa sɛ wɔde sika no bɛyɛ no anyɛ biara wɔatumi de ayɛ.
ɛfiri sɛ, saa sika yi yɛ wɔn a wɔn nti yɛte ha yi deɛ
NDCfoɔ ahyɛ aban no sɛ, ɔnkyerɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam ahodoɔ ne akodeɛ ahodoɔ a wagye nyinaa wɔ monnyae galamsey ko yi mu no.
Asɛm a wɔn nkitaho nnaanoni, Sammy Gyamfi kae ne sɛ, aban no agye exkaveitors 900 wɔ saa ɔko yi mu.
ɔbobɔɔ nneɛma bi a ɛwɔ 2020 bagɛte a aban no de kɔtoo Mmarahyɛbadwa no anim no de hyɛɛ deɛ ɔreka no mu kena.
Berɛ a Sammy Gyamfi ne nsɛntwerɛfo rekasa wɔ Asuo Pra so wɔ Twifo Praso a ɛwɔ mfinimfini mantam mu no, ɔkaa sɛ aban no ɔmfa nneɛma ahodoɔ a wɔgye no nyinaa mmɛkyerɛ.
ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nsaase, abɔdeɛmunyansapɛ ne mfidie so wɔ ɔmanpanin Mahama aberɛ so no, Akwasi Oppong Fosu kyerɛɛ sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu mapa fa mfidie a wɔde tutu fam a ayera no ho.
Nkɔmmɔ a ɔne Mr. Fosu dii no, ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ nhwehwɛmu mapa no bɛkyerɛ biribiara a ɛfa deɛ aban no reyɛ no ho.
Ghana Penteɔostal ne ɔharismatiɔ Council nsɔre no nso de wɔn ano ato mu bi rehyɛ aban no sɛ ɔmmɔ mmɔden na ɔnhwehwɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam ne sikafoturo no a ayera no mu
Deɛ ɛbaa nansa yi ara yɛ deɛ wɔn a wɔfoɔ amenamutufoɔ dwumadie soɔ nso aka no (ɔonɔerned Small Sɔale Minersɔ.
Wɔne Citi News redi nkɔmmɔ no, deɛ wɔn twerɛtwerɛfoɔ paninRev. Emmanuel T. Barrigah kaa ne sɛ, wɔn a wɔbɛhunun sɛ wɔn ho bɔn asɛm yi mu no ɛsɛ sɛ mmara ne wɔn di pa ara.
Na Alliancefor Social Equity and Public Aɔɔountabilityfoɔ (ASEPA) adi kan nso de krataa akɔ ma aban kwantenkoro mmaranimni sɛ ɔnhwɛ na ɔnhwehwɛ kataasehyɛ ne dwirim a ɛrɛkɔ so wɔ amenamutu a ɛnnam mmara kwan so no mu.
ASEPA pɛ sɛ agyinatukuo a ɔreko atia amenamutu adwuma a ɛnnam mmara kwan so no ne ɔhyɛkuo no ne Operation Vanguardfoɔ no nyinaa no aban kwantenkoro mmaranimni hwehwɛ wɔn nnwuma mu.
Wɔn krataa a wɔde kɔ maa aban kwantenkoro mmaranimni kyerɛ sɛ ɔnhwehwɛ nneɛma ahorow a wɔgyegyee wɔn amenamudwumafoɔ no hɔ no a ayera no, eyɛ exkaveatase no, sikafuturo ne akodeɛ binom a ɛkeka keka no no.
mfidie a wɔde tutu fam yi a ayera yi ho nsɛnsɛm yi hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a Professor Kwabena Frimpong Boateng, ɔsoafo a ɔhwɛ Nsaase, abɔdeɛmunyansapɛ, mfidie ne mpontuo so a ɔno ara san ne agyinatukuo no nnaanoni kaa sɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam bi a wɔgyee no 2017 ne 2018 no ayera.
Nnipa binom a amenamutu adwuma nketewa no hia wɔn no fa too wɔn ho so kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔnim baabi a mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no wɔ, na nnipa bi de reyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu baabi.
Mfinimfini mantam NPP amanyɔkuo no nnaanodani abediakyire a ɔdi kan a wɔatu asɛn no, Ekow Ewusi, a aban no hyɛɛ no sɛ anka ɔmfa mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no, lɔɔre binom, ne akadeɛ bi nsie no wɔase sɛ ne ho bɔn asɛm no mu.
Krataa a Citi News twee adwene kɔɔ so a Prof. Frimpong-Boateng kyerɛ de kɔmaa apolisifoɔ no kyerɛ sɛ, ɔnhwehwɛ n’adwuma mu wɔ kwaadu a wɔde abɔ no wɔ mfidie a yɛde tutu fam  a ayera no mu

Yɛbɛkae sɛ, ɔko a yɛreko atia galamsey yi no, ɛduu n’atenkon soɔ no asoeɛ a ɔhwɛ nsaase ne fam agudeɛ so no gyee mfidie mmaako mmaako bɛyɛ 500 wɔ afe 2017 no ne 2018 no mu

ɔkaa saa asɛm yi, aberɛ a wɔtee sɛ wɔkye nnipa binom afa mfidie a wɔde tutu fam a, ayera no ho.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ “Point of View” dwumadie no ho no, ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ aban no mfa nsɛm ahorow no nyinaa a ɛfa mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no a ayera no mmra nkran mmɛdi wɔ hɔ, na ɛhɔ no deɛ wɔbɛnya adagye ama no
Atemmuafoɔ adwuma no, yɛ adwuma baako a wɔmmoa koraa
Ansa na mfidie a wɔde tutu fam yi ho nsɛm bɛba no, yɛtee sɛ Operation Vanguard no rekasa fa nneɛma num bi ho a, yɛnnyinaa so rekasa fa ho bi.
Mekae sɛ, “Media Coalition” no kyerɛw maa aban faa Chinafoɔ a wɔkyeree wɔn no na wɔdii wɔn asɛm wɔ Circuit Court a ɛwɔ Tarkwa no.
Ansa mpo na wɔbɛyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu no, na asotwe a wɔde ama wɔn no nnu Ghana sika no 2,400
Sɛ na ɛdɔɔ so sene saa de a, na kyerɛ sɛ sika na yɛregye afiri wɔn hɔ.
Mekae sɛ me Supreme Court temuafoɔ baako rekasa no, ɔsusu sɛ, sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛde yɛn ani di saa nsɛm yi akyi pa ara deɛ a, biribi biara a, ɛfa asɛnie no ho no yɛmfa mmra nkran ɛfiri sɛ, sɛ wɔdi wɔ wɔn nkurow toa no mu a, nneɛma bebree no ara na ɛkɔ mu
Enni kwans sɛ yɛyɛ adeɛ, a ɛbɛyɛ de te sɛ yɛde mpɔnkye resesa nneɛma
mfidie a wɔde tutu fam yi a ayera yi ho nsɛnsɛm yi hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a Professor Kwabena Frimpong Boateng, ɔsoafo a ɔhwɛ Nsaase, abɔdeɛmunyansapɛ, mfidie ne mpontuo so a ɔno ara san ne agyinatukuo no nnaanoni kaa sɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam bi a wɔgyee no 2017 ne 2018 no ayera.
Nnipa binom a amenamutu adwuma nketewa no hia wɔn no fa too wɔn ho so kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔnim baabi a mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no wɔ, na nnipa bi de reyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu baabi.
Mfinimfini mantam NPP amanyɔkuo no nnaanodani abediakyire a ɔdi kan a wɔatu asɛn no, Ekow Ewusi, a aban no hyɛɛ no sɛ anka ɔmfa mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no, lɔɔre binom, ne akadeɛ bi nsie no wɔase sɛ ne ho bɔn asɛm no mu.
Krataa a Citi News twee adwene kɔɔ so a Prof. Frimpong-Boateng kyerɛ de kɔmaa apolisifoɔ no kyerɛ sɛ, ɔnhwehwɛ n’adwuma mu wɔ kwaadu a wɔde abɔ no wɔ mfidie a yɛde tutu fam  a ayera no mu
Nnipa baanu bi nso a wɔsusu sɛ ɔka Mr. Ewusi ho no nso no wɔakye wɔn nyinaa
Saa nnipa yi ne FredErick Ewusi, ɛoel Asamoah, Adam Haruna, Frank Gyan ne John Arhin
Wɔma wɔn baili a wɔrehwe anim sɛ wɔbɛdan wɔn ho adi Wukuada a ɛyɛ ɔgyefo 5, 2020 wɔ ɔriminal Investigations Departmentfoɔ atenae.
Mr. Ashigbey adi kan abobɔ n’adwene ama aban no ɛfa nhyehyeɛ bi a wantumi amfa angu akwan mu ahwɛ ammɔ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam a Operation Vanguardfoɔ no gyee no ho ban
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ Citi News no “Umaru Sanda Amadu, Mr Ashygbey dwene ho a, ɛnsi no pi sɛ anyɛ bi a, mfidie a wɔde tutu fam yi a wɔgyee yɛ yi apolisifoɔ bɔɔ ho ban deɛ.
Mr Ashigbey kyerɛɛ sɛ anka mfidie a wɔde tutu fam yi nyera sɛ aban no abɔ ho ban yiyi a
Na ɔsan hyɛɛ sɛ, ɔmanpanin Akufo Addo mpam mansin soafoɔ ahorow a mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no ayera afiri wɔn nsa no nyinaa
Deɛ ɔreka ne sɛ, saa nhyehyɛe yi bi na ɛsɛ sɛ aban no de to hɔ ko tia amenamutu adwuma no, ɛnnam mmara kwanso no
ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ, yɛrehyɛ ɔman no nnwumakuo ahorow mu kena no, ɛsɛ sɛ nnipa ahorow a wɔdeda nnwuma binom ano no ɛsɛ wɔtwe wɔn aso fa nneɛma binom a wɔyɛ ho.
Onipa a na kanee no ɔda, ngudeɛ asoeɛ ano no, Dr. Tony Aubynn kyerɛɛ sɛ, galamsey koɔ no atɔ nsuo mu
Nsuo ani ayɛ fɛ? Dabi. Nnipa retu galamsey no berɛ a wɔkura nkrataa a ɛma wɔn kwan? No. ɛkɔ asaase no ase mpo.
Dr. Aubynn, kyerɛɛ sɛ nsusudua no da hɔ fann, ɛnne sɛ yɛbɛhwɛ sɛ nnipa redi mmara no so anaa mpo no nsuo no ani ate anaa
Wokyerɛɛ wei nyinaa ase a, wohu sɛ anoyie no da hɔ fann. Yɛnnii nkonim wɔ ɔko yi mu, ngudeɛ asoeɛ paninyi de too dwa.
Na Dr. Aubynn, bɛfiri Minerals ɔommision 2017 ɛnna saa galamsey ko yi hyɛɛ aseɛ
Nanso saa berɛ no, na ɔwɔ awerɛhwɛmu sɛ amenamutuo adwuma no a, ɛnnam mmara kwan so no a wɔfrɛ no galamsey no bɛtumi agyae ɛnam dawurobɔ ahodoɔ a nsɛntwerɛ adwuma no bɔ faa ho no.
Berɛ na ɔwɔ hɔ no, aban no pamm mansin nkron ngudeɛ asoeɛ no nnaanodafoɔ sɛ ɔnkɔ koraa wɔ afe 2017 no mu.
Saa nnipa nkron yi kɔhwɛɛ amenamutu adwuma bi so wɔ mansin nkron mu na wɔhuu sɛ wɔanyɛ wɔn adwuma yie.
Asoeɛ a ɔhwɛ nsaase ne fam agudeɛ so soafoɔ, John Peter Amewu kyerɛ sɛ, wɔayɛ nhwɛ hann ama galamsey rekɔ so wɔ wɔn mansin no mu.
ngudeɛ asoeɛ no adwuma a ɔdii ne sɛ, ɔbɛhwɛ atoto nneɛma ahorow a ɛfa agudeɛ tuo a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no ho. Na wasan nso ayɛ mmara de abɔ Ghana fam agudeɛ no nso ho ban
Seesei Ghana Water companyLimited (GWCL) abɔ yɛn kɔkɔ sɛ, ɔbɛgyae nsuo a ɔde rema no no sɛ yɛnnyae Galamsey tuo no a
Onipa a ɔda Atɔe mantan GWCL ano no, Francis Agyei-Boatenga akyerɛ sɛ wɔretete nsuo a wɔde ma ɔmanfoɔ no ho abɛhia ɛnam galamsey adwuma no nti.
Ghana nsu papa no mu fa kɛseɛ no ara asɛe ɛnna mfuw nsaase bebree nso asɛe ɛnam galamsey nti
Nansa yi ara, wɔakyerɛ sɛ Ghana tɔ so ɔha mu nkyekyɛ mu aduanan baako a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔtɔ so aduɔwɔtwe wɔ wiase aman nyinaa mu ɛbɛ kataahyese ne porɔeɛɛ a ɔorruption Perɔeption by Transparenɔy International yɛe no
Berɛ a merekan deɛ ɔde bɛtoo dwa no, na ayɛ sɛdeɛ mensere sɛ mensu nso ooo, ɛfiri sɛ ɛmfata yɛn koraa
Berɛ na yɛhwɛ ɔha mu nkyekyɛ mu no a ɛbaa afe a etwamm no yɛ aduanan no a na ɛkyerɛ sɛ kataahyese a ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu no gu so renyini.
Na deɛ ɛkyerɛ ne sɛ, adwene a yɛwɔ fa kataahyese ne porɔeɛɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu no nsesaa koraa na mmom no ɛrenyini
Afei megye di sɛ wɔate deɛ mereka no ase
Da biara mebisa me ho sɛ, yɛretu mpon sɛ ɔman anaa sɛ yɛgyina beaɛ no a yɛgyina no ara sɛ ɛba kataahyesɛ ne porɔeɛɛ ho a
ɛmfa ho sɛdeɛ medwene asɛm yi ho, menya anoyie baako, a ɛno ne sɛ yɛnni kataahyese ne porɔeɛɛ so nkonim koraa mpo yɛ
Makan biribi afa nsɛnkae bi a abɛto dwa ho a ɛfa kataahyese ne porɔeɛɛ ho
Yɛse ɔmanpanin dada ɛ.A Kufuor kaa sɛ ayini te sɛ Adam.
Asɛm a mene no yɛ adwene nanso adwene foforo bi a ɛwɔ mu no nti
Ne nyinaa ne sɛ deɛ ɔkaa no sɛ akyire ɔbɛkyerɛ mu yie anaasɛ, anaasɛ adwene a ɛtaa akyire no nti no ɛsɛ sɛ metwe me ho firi ho koraa
Kataahyese ne yɛn atena firi tete na anya nsunsuansoɔ binom wɔ yɛn abrabɔ so.
Kataahyese biara nni hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛsosɔ so nanso yɛn man yi mu deɛ, yɛnhu no saa koraa
Yɛregye adaamudeɛ, sɛ ɛyɛ sika anaa ade foforo bi wɔ yɛn amanyɔsɛm mu, ɔman no dwumadie ahodoɔ mu, atemmuafoɔ mu, yɛn sukuu ahodoɔ mu ne yɛn nneɛma a yɛreyɛ no nyinaa mu
Nsunsuanso bɔne a kataasehyɛ ne porɔeɛɛ renya wɔ ɔman yi mpontuo so no nyɛ asɛm ketewa a ɛnam saa ama ɔman yi ntumi ntu mpon
Wo ara hwɛ sɛ, sika a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde yɛ ɔman no adwuma no bi kodi nkurɔfoɔ nsɛm na ɛnam kɔnterate nti na nsuo kɛkɛ nnipa nnya bi nnom.
Hwɛ sɛdeɛ kataasehyɛ resɛe ɔman yi toɔ wɔ yɛn asoeɛ asoeɛ, nnwumakuo ne ɔfesese ahodoɔ a ɛmma ɔman yi ntumi ntu mpon
Eyi mma no nyɛ nwanwa deɛ nti dawubɔ ne nneɛma ahodoɔ a amamnyɔkuo ahodoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu reyɛ de ako atia galamsey no nyinaa atɔ nsuo mu no
Aban no hyɛɛ bɔ ɛfiri 1992 sɛ ɔbɛko atia kataasehyɛ nanso yɛnhuu nsunsuansoɔ mapa biara atumi afiri mu aba
ɛnam saa nti na yɛhu no sɛ aban kwantenkoro ɔfese a NPP aban no bɛbuee no bɛboaa ama anka yɛatumi asi kataasehyɛ ano kwan nanso no ade papa biara mpo antumi amfiri mu amma
Onipa a yɛde no too saa beaɛ no ano no yɛ deɛ odi ne ho ni, ɔpɛ adwuma na onim n’adwuma nanso sɛ na ɔte saa berɛ a na onni aban mu no
Anaa anka ɛsɛ sɛ yɛgyae no na anka ɔyɛ ‘Citizen vigilante’, anka saa berɛ yi deɛ anka watumi agye Woyome sika no ne afoforo bi deɛ nyinaa
Eyi nso nkyerɛ sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ yɛtwee twee ɔfese no, ebia na afei na ɔrebɛyɛ adwuma, nanso mfeɛ mmiɛnsa yi a yɛanhu hwee, ɛnna ɛma medi abooboo
Ebi nso a amanyɔsɛm a yɛde awurawura kataasehyɛ ko a yɛreko wɔ ɔman no mu no nso na ɛmmoa ɔman no wɔ kwan biara so
Kataasehyɛ ho nsɛm yɛ adeɛ enni kwan sɛ yɛtoto n’ase koraa wɔ ɔman yi mu koraa
Eyi nso nyɛ adeɛ a nnipa a wɔyɛ amanyɔfoɔ nko ara na wɔde wɔn ho gyegye mu na mmom ankorɛankorɛ bi ne adwumakuo binom de wɔn ho gyegye kataasehyɛ yi mu
Mma wo werɛ mfiri sɛ deɛ ɔde rema ne deɛ ɔregye nyinaa ayɛ bɔne
Asɛ yɛbɛyɛ kataasehyɛ ho anomaa konkonene a abere biara no yɛpɛ sɛ yɛtua berɛ mpo a wɔmmisa yɛn
ɔman no aman a wɔretu de ako atia kataasehyɛ no, mehu no sɛ yɛwɔ ani dodow ɛsɛ sɛ yɛpagya mu kakra
Yɛn tease a yɛwɔ fa kataasehyɛ ho no wɔ fam ɛno nti ɛma nneyɛe bi wɔ hɔ a yɛgye tom
Gye sɛ yɛgyae, ɔko a yɛreko atia galamsey no ɛsan atɔ nsuo mu bio, yɛn suo no ani redan kɔkɔɔ, mfidie a yɛde te nsuo no ani no resɛe
Amenamutu adwuma yi a ɛnnam mmara kwan so yi a yɛsan frɛ no Galamsey yi a ɛrekɔ so yi, mehu no sɛ ɛyɛ kataasehyɛ nti na ɛgu so kɔ so no anaasɛ yɛn ara agye atom sɛ yɛne no bɛtena.
Ayɛ sɛ asɛm a yɛka no daa sɛ, daa dua a aka wɔ wiase no bɛwu no, nipa wɔaka no nso bɛwu no ɛno na ɛmma yɛnhu sɛnti no bio no
Nsɛntwerɛfoɔ ne aban no kaa wɔn ntoma paa ano sɛ wɔde reko atia galamsey no, wɔyɛɛ adeɛ nanso ankɔ si aga.
Galamsey ko no yɛ deɛ ɛhia pa ara a ɛnni kwan sɛ yɛtoto no ase koraa.
Yɛn kwae ne yɛn nsuo ahodoɔ nyinaa resɛe
Nansa yi ara nsuo a ɛho akɔ atwee wɔ mfinimfini mantam mu no, ɔape ɔoast no kyerɛ me sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ yɛsɔre
Kaseɛ a ɛbaa no kyerɛ sɛ galamseyfoɔ adwuma na ama mfidie a wɔde te nsuo no ani no bi resɛe a ɛnam so nti no ɛsɛ sɛ wɔte nsuo no kyɛ no so, a ɛkyerɛ sɛ mmerɛ rekɔ n’anim no wɔbɛgyae nsuo no kyɛ koraa
Kaseɛ a ɛoyNews kasamafoɔ a ɔwɔ mfinimfini mantam de bɛtoo dwa kyerɛ sɛ Sekyere Hermang afidie a a ɔde te nsuo no mu no mu, atɛkye ne efi ahyɛ no ma
Nti mebisa sɛ, ɔko a yɛreko atia galamsey no yɛredi nkoguo anaa? Megye di
ɛfiri sɛ, nsuo a ɛbɛka akyiri no nyinaa we a, nipa a waka no nso bɛwu
Ayɛ sɛ mereka no dodo nanso mede galamsey nsunsuansoɔ no nyinaa bɛhyɛ kataasehyɛ
Ne mmienu nyinaa yɛ adeɛ a a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛko tia nanso ɛyɛ me sɛ yɛredi nkoguo
ɔmanpanin Akufo Addo yɛe sɛ ɔreko saa ɔhaw yi nanso mehu no sɛ galamsey mmom na ɔne yɛn reko
Yɛtetee kuo ahodoɔ bi te sɛ GalamStop, asoeɛasoeɛ agyinatukuo, Operations akuo ahodoɔ sɛ wɔmmɛko ntia kataasehyɛ nanso emmu biara antu annyina
ɔkwan yi boaeɛ kakra nanso yɛn nsuo ani te sɛ deɛ ɛte no ara ɛnam ankorɛankorɛ bi sika a ɔpɛ no nti no ɔman no nyinaa mmɔ
Ekuo ahodoɔ a yɛyii wɔn sɛ ɔmmɛko ntia galamsey no adan sika gyegye kuo a ɔnam ɔman no ho regye adaamudeɛ
Aberɛ a temanmufoɔ nyinaa agye saa abrabɔ yi ato mu na wɔrema kwan ama wɔn a wɔmfiri ɔman yi mu de wɔn ho gye mu, aberɛ a wɔwɔ nnipa binom a wɔwɔ tumi na wɔredi yie wɔ wɔn nkurow mu na wɔnni adwene pa ma Ghana, yɛgyegye wɔn so
Akwan ahodoɔ nso a yɛfaa so sɛ yɛde reko ɔhaw yi nso no antumi annyina ankɔsi aga
Yɛbɔɔ mfidie a yɛde rebɛkɔ saa ɔhaw yi ho dawuro wɔ 2018 no mu nanso ɛrekame ayɛ sɛ yɛkɔdae no ɛyerae. Berɛ yɛbɛnya adwene papa bi sɛ yɛde bɛboa ɔman no, yɛntumi nsɔ mu yie na agye agu
ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nsaase ne agudeɛ soɔ no, Mr. Asomah-ɔheremeh kaa no ɛbɔ 2019 mu sɛ, aban no atumi adu ɔha mu nkyekyɛ mu aduɔwɔtwe num ho wɔ ɔko a ɔreko galamsey no
Berɛ a wamfa adanseɛ biara amma amɛsi deɛ ɔreka no so dua. Menni nnyinasoɔ biara a ɛbɛma maka sɛ deɛ ɔreka no nyɛ nokware na mmom no deɛ menim ne sɛ yɛn nsuo no ani da so yɛ fi
Agudeɛ ne amenamutuo adwuma no mmara no kyerɛ sɛ, sɛ ɔkye obi a, onii no anna afiase koraa no nyɛ mfeɛ 15 na enni kwan sɛ ɔkɔ boro mfeɛ 25 anaasɛ ɔretua 10,000 anaa 15, 000 nanso asoɔdenfoɔ no deɛ ɔgu so reyɛ adwuma no
Berɛ a soafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nsaase ne agudeɛ soɔ no hyia nsɛntwerɛfoɔ no ɔde too dwa sɛ, amenamutuo adwuma no maa ɔman yi Amɛrika sika no ɔpepepem 1.3 wɔ 2019 mu ɛnna ɛde nnwuma 26, 425 baa amenamutuo adwuma no mu
Sɛ wohwɛ nneɛma pa a ɛwɔ amenamutuo adwuma no mu a, anka ɛbɛtumi aboa atwe sika abrɛ ɔman yi na asan ama no atu mpon pa ara sɛ yɛrefa mmara kwan so de ayɛ a. Nanso no kwan biara nni hɔ a galamsey no yɛbɛtumi atoto no yie
ɔko a yɛreko tia saa nnneɛma abien yi, kataasehyɛ ne galamsey yi a ɛmma yɛnkɔ yɛn anim yi, ɛsɛ sɛ yɛhwɛ na yɛtumi di so
Nsuo ne kwae ho a ehia no yɛntumi ntoto no ase, ɛno nti no aberɛ biara no ɛsɛ sɛ yɛbɔ ho ban
Galamsey ne kataahyɛ wɔ nsunsuansoɔ bɔne wɔ yɛn man yi mpontuo so, na sɛ yɛtumi so ano ntɛm de a, ɛbɛboa yɛn pa ara
ɛsɛ sɛ kataasehyɛ ano sie yɛ adeɛ a ɛsɛ sɛ edi yɛn tirim mu dɛm pa ara, na yɛtumi kyerɛkyerɛ nneyɛe pa a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛn manfoɔ bɛdan no adi wɔ yɛn sukuu ne ɔsom bea ahorow nyinaa mu
Asotwe mapa a nhinhim biara nni mu na ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde ma obi biara a ɛbɛfom
Sɛ mmara yɛ adwuma yie a, na yɛkyekye wɔn a wɔnnam mmara kwan so reyɛ nnwuma no a, eyi bɛbɔ afoforo hu ama sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ biribi saa a, wɔbɛtwe wɔn ho afiri mu
Enni kwan sɛ yɛtena hɔ na nhyira a yɛanya wɔ yɛn nsaadeɛ mu no dan nnomee ma yɛn.
Nsuo yɛ nkwa momma yɛntena ase nyɛ nhwɛ hann
Onyame nhyira yɛn man yi na ɔman no yɛ kɛseɛ
Afei deɛ ayɛ sɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam 500 no a wɔgyee no berɛ a na wɔreko tia galamsey wɔ afe 2017 ne 2018 no mu no nyerae te sɛdeɛ na ɔsoafoɔ a ɔda asoeɛ asoeɛ no agyinatukuo no ano no, Professor Frimpong Boateng reka no
Nnipa binom a wɔka amenamutu adwuma nketewa kuo a ɛwɔ Ghana no kyerɛ sɛ wɔnim baabi a wɔde saa mfidie no akɔgu.
Ekuo no baanodani, Richard Kojo Peprah ne Citi News rekasa no ɔkaa sɛ, wɔn nkurɔfoɔ no bi dii mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no akyi kɔɔ mmeaɛ binom a wɔtu agudeɛ no bi wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Yɛhuu saa mfidie yi bi wɔ Tamale. Mfidie yi binom wɔ adeɛ bi wɔ ho a ɛma yehu baabiara a ɛwɔ
ɛno nti yɛtumi dii akyire
Sɛ wɔfa afidie no wɔ Asante mantam no mu a, na wɔde kɔ atifi mantam no mu
Wɔde reyɛ adwuma foforo binom
Wɔde ebi nso reyɛ galamsey
Asoeɛ asoeɛ agyinatukuo no titenani Professor Frimpong Boateng kyerɛ sɛ mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no ayera.
Yɛresi deɛ ɔsoafoɔ no kae no so dua, ɔsee, yɛgyee mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no na yɛde kɔɔ mansin ahodoɔ no asɛmbili, mfidie yi yeraa firii asɛmbili ahodoɔ a yɛde kosisii no.
Nsɛntwerɛfoɔ kuo ne Oɔɔupy Ghanafoɔ sɛ, wɔhia nkyerɛkyerɛmu afiri aban no hɔ ɛkwan a ɛnam so a saa mfidie yi tumi yerae
Saa ekuo mmienu yi kyerɛ sɛ, ɛyɛ mpaninfoɔ yi asɛdeɛ sɛ wɔma mmara yɛ adwuma wɔ agudeɛ tuo no mu
Deɛ ɔboaboa dɔm ano ma nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a ɔreko tia galamsey no, Ken Ashigbey, kaa sɛ nnipa a, wɔwɔ saa nneɛma yi a ayera no nyinaa no, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwehwɛ no na ɔde asotwe mapa ma no
Sɛ yɛanhwɛ ama mmara a yɛwɔ no anyɛ adwuma a, anyammara sɛm no bɛtoa so
ɛyɛɛ dɛn na yɛnhu mfidie a wɔde tutu fam no bi
ɛyɛ asɛnhia sɛ yɛbɛhu abanmufoɔ anaa ankorɛankorɛ a ɔhyɛ saa ade yi ase.
Wei yɛ adeɛ a yɛhia ho mmuae
Asoeɛ asoeɛ agyinatukuo a no adwuma ne sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama amenamudwuma nketewa no nyinaa agyae na wɔahwɛ atoto wɔn ano ama wɔn tumi krataa
ɔmanpanin Akufo Addo bue saa ekuo yi ano wɔ Obenem, 2017 no mu sɛ ɔmmɛhwɛ na ɔnsesa amenamutu adwuma no mu na ɔnyɛ nhyehyɛe mapa bi mfa mma wɔn
ɔsoaf a ɔhwɛ nsaase, abɔdeɛmunyansapɛ. Mfidie ne mpontuo so, Professor Frimpong Boateng na ɔda ano
Forestry Commission kyerɛ sɛ yɛwɔ akukudam binom a wɔtaa saa galamsey adwuma yi akyi.
Kwae ahodoɔ a galamseyfoɔ yi asɛe no no mu baako ne Amansie Centralmansin a ɛwɔ Asante mantam no, galamseyfoɔ yi asɛe nsaase bɛyɛ eka nson
Bekwai Mansin no Forestry Commission no nnaanoni, Rexford Twum-Damoah ka kyerɛɛ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ sɛ, adeɛ no reyɛ agye nsam ɛnam sɛ ɛtɔ da a asraafoɔ bɔ saa galamseyfoɔ yi ho ban
ɔkaa sɛ, galamseyfoɔ yi, bɔ nnipa bi a, wɔwɔ tumi sɛ wɔn ne wɔn mpaninfoɔ
Kwae pii no ara a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no resɛe ɛnam galamseyfoɔ a wɔsɛe nnua ne nsuo ahodoɔ tu sikafuturo nti no
Citi News‘ ɛonas Nyabor de too dwa 2019 kyerɛkyerɛ ɔman Ghana kwae ahodoɔ a emu nsaase yɛ bɛdeɛ a saa galamseyfoɔ yi asɛe sɛe no wɔ saa mfeɛ du yi a atwam yi no.
Saa kwae yinom ne Desiri, Kutukrom, Kobro, Oda, Jimira, Atewa, ne Tano-Offin a ɛwɔ Ahafo, Atɔe, Asante ne Apue mantan no mu.
Nsuo binom a ebi ne, Birim a ɛwɔ Apue mantan ne nsuo nkae no nyinaa a ɛfiri kwae ahodoɔ yi mu ba no nyinaa asɛe, a ɛnam saa nti no wɔn a wɔte ho mpo nnya nsuo nnom, ɛnna wɔn nso a wɔwɔ anaafoɔ fam no nso no bɛyɛ ɔpepemnum a ɔdan nsuo yinom no so nnya nsuo.
Anodisɛm no mu no, ɛdaa adi sɛ Forestry Commission kyee nnipa no bi a wɔreyɛ saa adwuma yi nanso ɛnam nnipa binom a wɔnim wɔn no nti no wɔgyae wɔn kwa
Accra High Court kyerɛ sɛ Nii Amanoo Dodoo, a ɔyɛ ɔgyefoɔ wɔ uniBank a ɛnte ase bio no bɛtumi abɛdi adanseɛ ama Dr. Kwabena Duffour a Sikakorabea no yɛ ne deɛ no
Wɔfrɛ Mr. Dodo sɛ ɔdanseni a ɔdi kan wɔ asɛnnie no mu, nanso mmaranimfoɔ a wɔdi Dr. Duffuor akyi no kyerɛ sɛ ɛmma asɛnnibea no mma kwan mma Mr. Dodoo nni adanseɛ
Dr. Duffour mmaranimfoɔ no kyerɛɛ sɛ, saa ɔgyefoɔ yi ato sikakorabea no mmara a ɛyɛ Specialized Deposit Act, 2016
Deɛ mmaranimfoɔ no rekyerɛ ne sɛ, ɔdanseni a ɔdi kan no, Nii Dodoo, nsɛ mfata sɛ ɔbɛdi adanseɛ ɛfiri sɛ ɔfaa no sɛ Unibank Gyefoɔ berɛ a ɔbɛkaa KPMG ho ma wɔdetee sikakorabea no akaunto no.
Mrs Yvonne Attakora Obuobisa a ɔyɛ Director of Publi Prosecution (DPP), sɔre tia asɛm yi.
ɔgyee too mu sɛ, kan no na Nii Dodoo ka KMPG ho, a ɛkyerɛ sɛ KPMG enni biribiara a wɔde ahyɛ uniBank mu anaasɛ onni diberɛ biara wɔ hɔ
Maame a ɔda Public Proseɔution ano yi gye gyinaa mu sɛ KPMG mmuu mmara biara so na Nii Dodoo fa a wɔfaa no no ɛyɛ ankorɛankorɛ bi na wɔfaa no na na ɛnam mmara kwan so
ɔka kaa ho sɛ, ne a na ɔne KPMG ayɛ adwuma pɛn no nkyerɛ sɛ, Bank of Ghana ntumi mfa no sɛ, ɔnkɔyɛ ɔgyefo mma uniBank.
Mrs Obuobisa kyerɛɛ sɛ, fa a wɔfaa no sɛ ɔgyefoɔ no nam mmara kwan so ɛno nti no wɔmmɔ wɔn asɛm no ngu.
Justice Bright Mensah, “Court of Appeal” temmuani a na ɔno nso te hɔ sɛ High Court temmuafoɔ no nso kaa sɛ, fa a a DPP faa no Nii Dodoo no nyɛ adeɛ a ɛnnam mmara kwan so.
Faa a ɔfaa no no nam mmara kwan so
ɔkaa sɛ, section 59 of the Evidence Act no kyerɛ onipa a ɔntumi nni adanseɛ wɔ asɛnnibea, a ɛyɛ obi a kasa ho yɛ no den, anaasɛ ɔkasa a nnipa nte aseɛ papa anaasɛ ɔhia obi a ɔte ɔno nko ara asɛm ase, anaa ɔnte sɛdeɛ yɛdi adanseɛ wɔ asɛnnibea no ase.
ɔtemmuafoɔ Mensah kaa sɛ, ɔhu no sɛ ɔdanseni no yɛ obi a ɔbɛtumi adi adanseɛ ɛnam sɛ ɔnim biribi fa deɛ ɛrekɔ soɔ no ho.
ɔka kaa ho sɛ, ɔfa a ɔfaa no no no no nam mmara kwan so
ɔsan kaa bio sɛ A1, A2 ne A4 ama asɛnnibea no ahu sɛ adanseɛ a wɔrebɛdi no deɛ ɛnteɛ bi frafra mu ɛnam sɛ wɔantumi anka hwee amfa anodisɛm a ɛbaa no ho
ɔtemmuafoɔ no kaa sɛ, akyinneɛ yi yɛ deɛ emu da hɔ fann, ɛno nti no yɛntumi nka sɛ ɔkwan a yɛrefa so no nneɛma bi a ɛnnyɛ abɛfrafra mu
Na Court of Appeal temmuafoɔ no kaa sɛ, asɛm yi yɛ deɛ ɛmfa asraafoɔ ho ɛno nti no ɔyɛ obi a ɔbɛtumi adi adanseɛ yie.
Afei asɛmnibea no kɔ kyerɛɛ no ɔgyefoɔ no sɛ ɔnka ne ntam na ɔnhyɛ n’adansedie no ase
Wɔde kwaadu aduɔson baako abɔ Dr. Kwabena Duffour ne nnipa nwɔtwe bi ɛnam dwuma bi a wɔdii a ama sikakorabea no agu no
Ghana sikakorabea kuo no kyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ krado sɛ Bank of Ghana bɛma wɔn akwankyerɛ na wɔama nnwuma kuo binom a wɔgyegye sika no agyae sika binom a wɔgye wɔn adwadifoɔ hɔ no ɛnam nneɛma bi a wɔyɛ ma wɔn no nti
Ekuo yi ani nnye ho sɛ sikasie nnwuma ahodoɔ no bɛgyae sika a ɔte wɔ sevines akaunt so de yɛ nsiesie adwuma no
Berɛ a ɔne Citi News rekasa no, ekuo no anobaanodani, John Awuah, kyerɛkyerɛ sika a ɔte firi sevines akaunt mu no, ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ sevines akaunto no bi wɔ hɔ a, ɛne karɛte akaunto no bi bɔ mu
Wɔn a wɔpɛ wɔn no mpo nyɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ sikakorabea adwuma no mu no, na mmom wɔn a wɔyɛ sika ho adwuma nyinaa
ɛnam saa nti na yɛfoa, nyɛ ne nyinaa deɛ na mmom no sɛ wɔntwa saa ntetee no mu
ɛsɛ sɛ yɛne adwadifoɔ no di no yie
Sevines akaunto no nyɛ deɛ da biara yɛyi sika wɔ mu
Nanso yɛhu no sɛ nnipa binom de wɔ Momo wallet no ama no, na wɔn de wɔn ATM kaade no yi sika firi wɔn akaunto no mu
Eyi ma akaunto no nhyehyɛe no tɔ nsuo mu. Deɛ sikakorabea no reka ne sɛ, sɛ adwadifoɔ de wɔn akaunt a wɔhyɛ sɛ ɔde resie sika ayi no daakye di dwuma sɛ akaunto a adekyee biara ɔbɛyi sika wɔ mu a, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtua ho ntwama
ɔsan kyerɛ mu sɛ, ɛnam saa nti no wɔwɔ akwansideɛ kakra
CentralBank de nsɛm bi too dwa Fiada, Ayɛwohummɔ 18, 2021, hyɛɛ sikakorabea ahorow ne sika nnwuma binom a wɔgyegye sika sɛ wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri nneyɛe nson bi a ɛma wɔn tete adwadifoɔ sika so ɛnam sɛ saa dwumadie no ne sikakorabea no no nhyehyɛe bɔ abira
Saa sika a teteɛ yɛ a CentralBank hu no sɛ ɛnam mmara kwan so na sikakorabea ahodoɔ no resi si adwadifoɔ no ne credit Insurance Premium Overcharges, Maintenance Fees on Savings Account, ne Over the counter (OTC) Withdrawal ɔharges ne sikakorabea binom rema wɔn a wɔ bɔ wɔn bosea de wɔn din aka deɛ wɔde sika no reyɛ no sɛ ɛyɛ wɔne wɔn dea no
Sikasɛm nimdeɛfoɔ, Dr Akwasi Atuahene, akyerɛ sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ Bank of Ghana tu anammɔn bi de si sikakorabea ahodoɔ no kwan wɔ wɔn adwuma yɛ mu sɛ wɔamfa saa mmara no anyɛ adwuma a
Fiada, a ɛyɛ Ayɛhumɔmmɔ 18, 2021 no Bank of Ghana hyɛɛ sikakorabea ahorow no nyinaa sɛ wɔnnyae ntwama a ɛde sika soɔ a ɛnam mmara kwan so no
ɛno ara mu no CentralBank nso hyɛɛ sika nnwuma kuo ahorow no nso sɛ wɔnnyae saa sika gyegyeɛ no anyɛ saa ɛmmoa sika adwumakuo no nyinaa
Saa nhyehyɛe weinom nyinaa no wɔhu no sɛ, ɛyɛ deɛ ɛnna kwan mu koraa na bio nso no ɛyɛ ɔkwan bi a ɔrefa so asisi adwadifoɔ ɛno nti eyi bɛboa abɔ adwadifoɔ sika ho ban
Saa nteteɛ yi a ɛnnam mmara kwan so yi a Bank of Ghana reka yi ne credit Insurance premium overɔharges, maintenanɔe fees on savings aɔɔounts, over the ɔounter withdrawal ɔharges, ne afoforo be a ɛkeka ho.
Nteteɛ nson yi a yɛreka ho asɛm ne deɛ ɛwɔ aseɛ hayi ne nhyehyɛe a BoG de ato ho
ɛnam atoyerɛnkyɛm nti no sikakorabea no hwɛ sɛ ansa na ɔbɛbɔ obi bosea no, na onii no wɔ nsiakyibaa a ɛfa atoyerɛnkyɛm ho sɛ ɛyɛ owuo, dɛ die anaa w’adwuma resɛe
ɛnam sɛ Bank of Ghana hu no sɛ, saa nhyehyɛe yi boa sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a sikakorabea ahodoɔ no nneɛma nnye ngu no nti no, sikakorabea no bi afa ho de gye sika binom firi wɔn adwadifoɔ hɔ a ɛrema wɔn bosea a wɔbɔ no kɔ soro pa ara
Wɔahyɛ sikakorabea ahodoɔ no nyinaa sɛ, wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri saa nneyɛe no ho na wɔnni saa nhyehyɛe yi so
Sikakorabea a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔfa nsiakyibaa adwuma bi ntete yɛ adwuma no, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔfa saa ntete no a nsiakyibaa no de yɛ adwuma no nso de di dwuma
Sikakorabea ahodoɔ no nni ho kwan sɛ ɔgye nsiakyibaa sika biara a firi adwadifoɔ hɔ a wɔn adwene nyinaa ne sɛ, ɔreyɛ nsiakyibaa nhyehyɛe bi ama wɔn
Eyi nka sika a ɔnya firi nhyehyɛe a ɛda sikakorabea no ne nsiakyibaa adwuma no ntam
Saa sika yi a ɛyɛ ‘Aɔɔount Maintenanɔe Fees’ yi mma kwan mma adwadifoɔ ne sikakorabea no nni dwa
Bank of Ghana ahwɛ mu ahu sɛ, saa sika tetee yi ama nnipa pii no ara atwe wɔn ho afiri sika a yɛde to sikakorabea no mu. Na ama wɔn nso a wɔdwene sɛ anka wɔde sika bɛto sikakorabea hɔ a ɔbɛnya mfasoɔ wɔ so no nso agyae
Saa nneɛma ahodoɔ yi resɛe sikakorabea adwuma no na ɛretwe nkurɔfoɔ firi sika a na anka wɔde sie wɔ sikakorabea ahodoɔ no ho
Bank of Ghana ahu sɛ sikakorabea no bi de ntetee bi ato sika a adwadifoɔ yi firi wɔn ankasa akaunto mu wɔ sikakorabea no mu no
Deɛ ɔka fa ho nyinaa ne sɛ, ɔde eyi ato hɔ sɛdeɛ nnipa pii no ara mma sikakorabea hɔ mmɛyi sika na mmom no wɔde wɔn foonu ne kaade mmom na ɛbɛyi sika afiri sika korabea ahodoɔ no mu
Saa foonu ne kaade a wɔde yi sika yi nso nyɛ adeɛ a wɔnte wɔn sika kakra mfiri so
Berɛ Bank of Ghana refoa sikakorabea ahodoɔ no wɔ foonu sikasɛm dwumadie mu no, saa nneyɛe nso ma nnipa binom twe wɔn ho firi akaunto a ɔbɛbue no ho ne titiriw ne wɔn a wɔnnim foonu no mu yie
Saa nneyɛe yi nso nya nsunsuansoɔ bɔne wɔ Bank of Ghana so ɛnam sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔhu nneɛma binom mu nti.
Wɔahyɛ sikakorabea no sɛ wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri ntwatema bi a wɔde to adwadifoɔ so no sɛ wɔyi wɔn ankasa sika na annu deɛ wɔhyɛɛ sɛ wɔbɛyi no a
Bio, nso no sikakorabea ahodoɔ no, enni kwan sɛ ɔte adwadifoɔ a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔhu sika a ɛda wɔn akaunto mu wɔ sikakorabea hɔ no
Bank of Ghana asan ahu sɛ sikakorabea no bi wɔ hɔ a, wɔhwehwɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔrebɛbɔ bosea no de wɔn agyapadeɛ bi ba na wɔsesa yɛ no sɛ, ɛyɛ wɔne sikakorabea no deɛ
Deɛ ɛka ho ne sɛ, deɛ ɔbɛbɔ bosea no na ɔma no na ɔma no bɔ saa ka no ansa na wɔama no sika no
Saa nneyɛe yi a sikakorabea no bi dan no adi no ne bosea bɔ mmara a ɛyɛ section 7 ( Borrowers and Lenders Act, 2020 (Act1052ɔ no bɔ abira a ɛmma kwan sɛ deɛ ɔrebɔ bosea no no ne deɛ ɔregye bosea afiri ne hɔ no de wɔn din bɛto n’ade so
Saa nneyɛe yi ma nnipa twe wɔn ho firi akwanya a wɔwɔ sɛ anka wɔde bɔ bosea no ho ɛnam sɛ adeɛ a ɔde bɛsi akagyina mu no, gye sɛ ɔne deɛ ɔbɛbɔ ne hɔ bosea no de wɔn din to so
Seesei no sikakorabea ahodoɔ no, yɛasi wɔn kwan sɛ wɔne wɔn a wɔrebɛpɛ bosea wɔ wɔn hɔ no de wɔn din bɛto ade ko no ara ɔde bɛsi akagyina mu
Bank of Ghana asan ahu sɛ, sikakorabea no bi wɔ hɔ a, ntwama a ɛdeda bosea a wɔde ma adwadifoɔ no yɛ deɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔde nya mfasoɔ firi wɔn hɔ kɛkɛ
ɛne sɛ, ntwama yi wɔde ka ntetee a ɛda bosea no so no
Saa nneyɛe yi kɔwie sɛ, bosea no, adwadifoɔ ntumi ntua a ɛno nti no bosea bɔ ntumi nkɔ so
Saa nneyɛe yi sɛ sɛe adwadie a ɛkɔ so no
Wɔahyɛ sikakorabea ahodoɔ no sɛ wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri ntwama a wɔama adwadifoɔ tua sɛ berɛ a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde tua wɔn sika no boro so no a
Deɛ ɛteɛ ne sɛ, saa ntwama yi no ɛsɛ sikakorabea no gyeɛ berɛ wɔatwentwen ntwama no tua soɔ anaasɛ sika no ankasa na ɛnyɛ bosea no a ɔbɔɔ yɛ no ho sɛdeɛ bosea bɔ mmara no te no (section 55(3) of the Borrowers and Lenders Act, 2020 (Act1052)
Sɛ yɛhwɛ boseabɔ mmara no mu a (section 55 (20 of the Borrowers and Lenders Act, 2020 (Act1052) ɛsɛ sɛ sikakorabea no de ntwama bi a ɔgyina sika a ɔregye no afe mu no nyinaa so de biribi asi ho.
Seesei deɛ, wɔahyɛ sikakorabea no sɛ wɔntwe wɔn ho mfiri bosome ntwama a wɔde to bosea so no.
Deɛ ɔde aba bio ne sɛ, seesei no ɛsɛ sɛ sikakorabea biara ma yɛhu wɔn afe no ntwama sɛdeɛ Disclosure and Product Transparency Rules a yɛde bɔ bosea no teɛ pɛpɛɛpɛ
Bnak of Ghana asan ahu sɛ, sikakorabea no bi nnye nnipa a wɔde sika to anaa wɔyi sika firi afoforo akaunto no mu no ho asɛm. Wɔhu no sɛ, krataa a wɔtwerɛ so de yi sika no saa akwan no bi nna so
Saa nneyɛe yi ma nnipa binom a akaunto no nyɛ wɔn dea no de sika to afoforo akaunto mu na wɔatwerɛ ‘me ara’ wɔ baabi a anka deɛ akaunto no yɛ no dea no bɛtwerɛ ne din no
Kasanoma adwuamkuo MTN, asi beaeɛ a yɛtwe mogya a ne boɔ du Ghana sika 300,000 de ama wɔn a wɔhwɛ awoɔ, nyinsɛn ne mmaasɛm mu wɔ ɔape ɔoast ayaresabea. MTN ahyɛ Ghanafoɔ nyinaa sɛ ɔnhwɛ na wɔmmoa ɔman no mogyakuo adwuma no na wɔntumi ntwe mogya pii
Da a ɔde saa dan yi rehyɛ wɔn nsa no na ɛyɛ Wiase Nyinaa Mogya di da
Chief ɔorporate Services nnaanodani ma MTN Ghana, Samuel Koranteng, kyerɛɛ sɛ, saa beaeɛ yi bɛboa ama mogya a wɔtwe no wɔ ɔman yi mu no atumi akɔ yie wɔ mfeɛ a ɛdeda yɛn anim no
Saa beaeɛ yi a yɛasi yi, gyina hɔ ma nmmoa a yɛbɛtumi de aboa mogyatwe ne mogyasie wɔ Ghana.
Yɛn ani gye pii, ɛnam sɛ yɛreboa ayaresa ne ayarehwɛ wɔ ɔman yi mu
Samuel Koranteng san de too dwa sɛ, mogya ho hia wɔ ayarehwɛ mu pa ara ne titiriw ne awoɔ mu na ɛnam saa nti no yɛntumi ntoto no ase koraa
ɛnam saa nti no MTN de afe biara mogya tweɛ aba a, afe biara no wɔanya koraa no wonya mogya toa 20,036.
ɔpanina ɔda ɔape ɔaost ayaresabea no ano, Dr. Eric Kofi Ngyedu, de too dwa sɛ nyinsɛn ne awoɔ mu wuo nko ara ayarebea no nyaa no afe 2020 no yɛ aduonunsia.
ɛwom sɛ ɛso ate afiri aduonu nwɔtwe no yɛnyaa no afe a ɛtwaa mu deɛ nanso ɛsɛ sɛ yɛtumi te so ba fam
Dr. Ngyedu daa MTN ase wɔ nneɛma ne mmoa a wɔde reboa nyinsɛn ne awoɔ mu ayarehwɛ no
Ghanafoɔ pii no ara ani gyeɛ bere a ɔman paninde mansin baako mfidi dwuma baako bae no ɛnam sɛ na wɔgye di sɛ ɛreba abɛhyɛ ɔman no mpontuo mu kena ama temanmufoɔ nso atumi anya adwuma ayɛ na ate adwuma a enni hɔ no so
Mmom ankorɛankorɛ no bi nyaa mmoa firii saa dwumadie yi mu na ebinom nso antumi annya bi ɛnam sika ho haw a ɛbae no nti
ɛnam saa nti no, onipa a ɔda Agriɔultural Development Bank (ADBɔ ano no, Dr. John Kofi Mensah kae sɛ, sikakorabea no rehwɛ aboa ama Ghanafoɔ a wɔwɔ kuadwumay no mu sika kakra de a de aboa mansin baako mfidi dwuma baako nhyehyɛe no a ɛfa kuadwuma ho no.
Mansin baako mfidi dwuma baako no, yɛn manpaninna ɛde bae, na yɛakɔ yɛ sikakorabea a yɛhwɛ kuadwuma mpontuo so no deɛ, yɛbɛhwɛ na yɛboa mfudeɛ ne kuayɛ a ɛwɔ dwumadie yi mu no
ɛne sɛ, mfidi dwuma ahorow no a wɔresisi no nyinaa akɔ yɛ deɛ ɛfa kua ho, nti no yɛpɛ sɛ yɛde sika hyɛ mu
Yɛmfa Ekumfi ɛuiɔe fididwuma a ɛwɔ mfinimfini mantam no a nansa yi ara ɔmanpanin kɔ bua ano no nyɛ nhwɛsoɔ, ADB de sika awura ne mfudeɛ a ɛyɛ abɔrɔbɛ no mu
Yɛadi kan de Ghana sika ɔpepem aduasa na ahyɛ abɔrɔbɛ no dua no mu
Deɛ mɛtumi asan aka ho asɛm bio yɛ ntooso fididwuma a ɛwɔ Berekum a ɛwɔ Bono Ahafo mantam no mu
Yɛde sika ahyɛ ntooso no dua no mu
ɛnam saa nti no Ghanani biara a ɔpɛ sɛ ɔkɔ aduaba dua mu no, mmra ne ADB mmɛkasa, yɛbɛboa no wɔ sika fa mu, na watumi adua no nneɛma no na n’adwuma no angu
Yɛde yɛn ani asi Ghana nneɛma a yɛde ba abɔtene no so ne titiriw ne nneɛma ahodoɔ a yɛdua no
Adwuma baako a ɛwɔ Ghana a ɛntumi nnyina ne nan so ne nkokɔ yɛn adwuma no
Dr. John Kofi Mensah a ɔda ADB sikakorabea no ano de ato gua sɛ, sɛ ɛbɛyɛ na wɔn a wɔnyɛn nkokɔ wɔ ɔman yi mu no bɛtumi ne wiase nyinaa nkokɔyɛnfoɔ de asi ani nti no, ɔde nhyehyɛe bi a yɛfrɛ no broiler value ɔhain sɔheme aba a, ɛbɛboa ama sikakorabea no abɔ wɔn bosea de ahyɛ wɔn adwuma no mu a, nsisoɔ a ɛfata bi pɛ na ɛda so.
Yɛde broiler value ɔhain sɔheme aba a eyi boa yɛde sika hyɛ nkokɔ yɛn adwuma no mu, eyi ma yɛde sika hyɛ berɛ a akokɔ no bɛhyɛ aseɛ ato de kosi berɛ a wɔbɛnyini a, kosi sɛ yɛde bɛkɔ adwamansoɔ.
Yɛahu sɛ nsisoɔ yɛ ɔhaw pa ara, na yɛrehyɛ yɛn adwadifoɔ bɔ sɛ yɛn nhyɛhyɛe foforo yi bɛhwɛ atete nsiho no so.
Onipa a ɔda sikakorabea yi ano de saa asɛm yi too dwa berɛ a ɔne n’adwadifoɔ no bi hyiaa wɔ Kumase na wɔtoo wɔn nsa didii wɔ dwumadie bi ase.
Onipa a ɔda sikakorabea no nhwɛsokuo no ano, Mr Alex Bernasko de too gua sɛ, ɛwom sɛ COVID-19 sɛe nnwuma bebree no ara deɛ nanso ADB deɛ etumi bɔɔ ne ho mmɔden nyaa mfasoɔ ɔpepemɔhansia num wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu no mu na san de nhyehyɛe mapa baa de bɛboa n’adwadifoɔ.
ɔsan nso de too gua sɛ, sikakorabea no san de mfehyia mmieɛnsa nhyɛhyɛe bi asan aba de bɛhyɛ ne nnwuma no mu kena.
COVID-19 yareɛ no bae no, yɛde nhyehyɛe bi bae bɛtee yɛn adwadifoɔ berɛ so kakra.
Nokwasɛm ne sɛ, na emu baako yɛ deɛ yɛgyina yɛn akadeɛ ahorow so reyɛ no mmerɛ pɔtee bi mu
ɛno firi hɔ a, ebi nso deɛ yɛmaa wɔn sikatua no ho mmerɛ ne ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so atua no na ɛnyɛ asodie mma wɔn
Mo ne yɛn nyinaa bɛyɛ adwene sɛ, yɛn nsiho ahodoɔ no nyinaa yɛatete so ɛnam sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ mo ho dwo mo wɔ abra no mu nti. ɛne sɛ, ADB ayɛ mfehyia mmiɛnsa nhyehyɛe a ɛrebɛboa apagya nneɛma ahodoɔ ne ne dwumadie ahodoɔ nhyehyɛe no mu.
Nhwɛsokuo a ɔda ADB sikakorabea no nam wɔn nsrahwɛ a wɔkɔɔ no wɔ Asante mantam no mu no so kɔsraa Asantehene, Otumfoɔ ɔsɛe Tutu II
Asantehene bɔɔ sikakorabea no abaso wɔn dwuma sononko a wɔredi de boa kuadwuama na ɔsan hyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnkɔ so mmoa nnwuma ahodoɔ no nyinaa.
ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nnwuma ne afisɛm so, Francis Asenso Boakye, de ato gua sɛ aban no ne Wiase Sikakorbea kɛseɛ (World Bankɔ reka abom de sika botene a ɛyɛ Amɛrika sika ɔpepemhanu abɛhwɛ asi nsuo ahodoɔ a eyiri wɔ Nkran no.
Deɛ ɔkyerɛ ne sɛ, saa nneɛma yi nyinaa ka aban no tirimpɔ a ɔnam so pɛ sɛ ɔde si nsuo a eyiri afe biara mu wɔ Nkran no.
Mr. Asenso Boakye dann yi adi wɔ krataa a ɛkɔ dawubɔfoɔ hɔ no mu Yawda, Ayɛwohumɔmmɔ da a ɛtɔ so mmiɛnsa no mu wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako yi mu de kai deɛ ɛsii afe mpem mmienu ne dunum no mu.
ɛnam eyi nti no, aban no ne Wiase Sikakorabea kɛseɛ (World Bankɔ aka abom de sika botene a ɛyɛ Amɛrika sika ɔpepemhanu de bɛhyɛ Greater Accra Resilient and Integrated Prroject no mu.
ɔsoafoɔ no kyerɛɛ sɛ, Akufo Addo aban bɛkɔ so ayɛ deɛ ɔbɛtumi biara de asi nsu ahodoɔ a eyiri wɔ Nkran ne ɔman no nkurow binom afe biara no.
ɛnam so maa Mr. Asenso Boakye nso hyɛɛ ɔmanfoɔ nso sɛ wɔmmoa na aban no tirimpɔ yin so ntumi mmra mu
ɔkyerɛɛ sɛ, aban no nko ara ntumi nsi saa ade yi ano kwan, sɛ temanmufoɔ ansesa wɔn suban a.
Saa dwumadie yi bɛboa ayi nsunsoanso bɔne a nsu yi de ba no afiri hɔ, na asan nso asi efi ne nwura ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ ɔdaw asutene no kwan no mu
Saa dwumadie yɛ bɛma yɛayɛ fasuo a ɛbɛboa ama yɛayi ɔhaw ahodoɔ a sɛ nsu tɔ a entumi ntene nkɔ no afi hɔ. Yɛbɛsi nsutwaa kɛseɛ wɔ ɔdaw asutene no so na atumi akora nsuo bebree a ɛmma nsuo no nyiri bio mfa baabi te sɛ Kwame Nkrumah Cirle.
